evamutpannanirdoShaH' ityAdinoktArthe smR^itisammatimAha- evamAdIti ||
Adipadenaitadupayuktamanyat.h | bhAShyAdAvudAhR^itaivarchanairapItyaperarthaH | yadvaivamAdItyetadadhikaraNaprameyaM tadupayuktaM cha gR^ihyate | apipadena prathamAdhikaraNaprameyasya samuchchayaH | athavA.adhikaraNaprameyasya samuchchayaH | athavA.adhikaraNadvayAthar evamAdItyanena gR^ihItaH | dvitIyAdyadhikaraNArthagrahaNAyApishabdaH | puruShArthAdhikaraNe stutyadhikaraNe cha j~nAnaphalasya tAratamyamabhihitam.h | tatsaMsArikaphalasya na vipratipannamiti muktigatasya sAdhayitumuttaro granthaH | ye mokShe bhedameva nAN^gIkuvarte ye chAN^gIkR^ityApi bhedamAnandAdikaM nAbhyupayanti na tAnprati tAratamyasAdhanasyAvakAshaH | kintu bhedAdisAdhanameva katarvyam.h | kariShyate cha chaturthe.adhyAye | ye punarbhedamAnandAdikaM chAN^gIkR^ityApi tAratamyaM na manyante tAnpratyaya prayatnaH kriyate | yAvadadhikAramityadhikaraNArthasyaivAyaM prapaJNcha iti na doShaH | 
tatra tAvachChatyA muktAvAnandatAratamyamupapAdayati- tAratamyamiti ||
brahmAdInAM j~nAnaphale muktigAmityAnande yadi yadi tAratamya no bhavettarhi kathaM "sa yo havai manuShyANAM rAddha' ityAdikA vAjasaneyinAM saiShA.a.anandasya mImAMsA bhavati' ityAdikA taittirIyANAM cha shrutisteShAM brahmAdInAmAnandasya tAratamyaM brUyAt.h | sarve.apyuttarottaraM shataguNanandA ityanabhidhAya pR^ithakpR^ithageva bravIti | tena tatra tAtparyasadbhAvashchAvagamyate | brahmAdInAmAnandasya yashcha shrutirbravIti muktAnAM tu tatsAdhyata iti kiM kena saN^gatamityata uktamavR^ijina iti | yashcha shrotriyo.avR^ijino.akAmahata ityAdyA | shrotriyasya chAkAmahatasyeti dvitIyA | yadyapi shrotriyatvamapi muktij~nApakamityanyatroktam.h | tathA.api bahusaMvidhAnasAdhyaM taditi na saN^kItirtam.h muktiM cha nigadya teShAM muktAnAmAnandatAratamyaM cha bravIti | chashabdau mithaH samuchchaye | taittirIyashrutirapyatropalakShitetyuttaratra j~nAsyate |

nanu saMsAriShvapyakAmahatatvAdikaM kathaJNchitsambhavati | satyam.h | mukhyato na sambhavatIti brUmaH | nacha vinA bAdhakenAmukhyAN^gIkAro yuktaH | etenAvR^ijino.akAmahata iti muktiM nigadyetyetadvivR^itaM bhavati | kathamakAmahatatvAdeH saMsAriShvasambhava ityato.akAmahatatvasya tAvadupapAdayati- kAmasyeti ||
yatra loke kAmasyechChAyAH kAmA viShayA AptAH paryAptAstatra mAmamR^itaM muktaM api kurviti vAyuM prati prArthanam.h | yadyasmAditi shrutirityAptakAmatvaM mukterlakShaNatvenAha | visheShaNasyetaravyAvR^ittyarthatvAt.h | niravakAshatvAdinA balIyasAH shruteranyathayitumashakyatvAt.h | tasmAtkAmAhatirakAmahatatvaM muktAdanyatra kutaH sambhavet.h | AptakAmatvasya muktalakShaNatvena shrutyuktatve tadevaM saMsAriShvasambhavi syAt.h | akAmahatatvaM tu kathamasambhavItyata Aha- prApteti ||
sA kAmahatiH | akAmahatatvasyAptakAmatvaM hetuH | nacha nimittAbhAve naimittikasya sambhavo.asti | tatra nimittaM chAptakAmatvaM saMsAriShu na sambhavatItyuktam.h | tato naimittikamakAmahatatvamapi tatrAsambhavIti |
AptakAmatvasyAkAmahatatvaM prati nimittatvaM vivR^iNoti- aprayatneneti ||
sA.akAmahateti sambandhaH | yA.akAmahatashabdAtpratIyate setyarthaH | anyathA.aprayatnena kAmAnAmavAptyabhAve kuta eva kAraNAtsA.akAshamahatayA bhavenna kuto.apItyanvayavyatirekAvuktau | etaduktaM bhavati | kAmenopadravo hi kAmahatatA tadabhAvashchAkAmahatatA | kAmanimittopadravAbhAvashchAnAyAsena tattadviShayaprAptAveva bhavati nAnyathetyanubhavasiddham.h | ataH prAptakAmatvAkAmahatatvayornimittanaimittikabhAvo yukta eveti |
nAyamasti niyamaH, yadAptakAmasyaiva, kAmanimittopadravAbhAvo nAnyatheti | kAmabhAve.api tannimittopadravAbhAvasambhavAditi chet.h | kimanenoktasya vyabhichAramAtraM chodyate kiM vA prakR^iteShu saMsAriShvapyAptakAmatvAbhAve.apyakAmatvenAkAmahatatA sambhavatItyAshAsyate | nAdyaH | vakShyamANanyAyena visheShaNaprakShepAt.h | na dvitIyaH | brahmAdayo na kAmarahitA 
asuptAmUDhachetanatvAddevadattavadityanumAnavirodhAdityAshayavAnanumAnasya vyAptimupapAdayati- chetanasyeti ||

moho.atrApi grAhyaH | vyAharatItyataH paraM yatastasmAdityadhyAhAryam.h | yadbhojanAdikaM kAmayamAno devadattaH svApAdikamApnotyutthApitaH punastadeva kadAchidvayAharatIti tAvadanubhavasiddham.h | tasmAdvayAharaNavisheShAchcha tasya tadA tatra kAmo.astItyanumIyate | sa cha na tAvadutthAnAnantaramutpannaH | tadA devadattasyAvAshatvAt.h | vastudarshane.anumAnAdineShyasAdhanatAj~nAne cha sati khalu kAmodayaH syAt.h | nachAvashasyaiShA kAmasAmagrI kalpayituM shakyate tataH prAktana eva kAmaH suptyAdau sannataro(vyakto).anuvartamAnaH punaH sahakArilAbhakrameNa vyajyata ityevAN^gIkAryam.h | tathAchAha pataJNjaliH | avidyAkShetratvamuttareShAM prasuptatanuvichChinnodArANAmiti | yata evaM tasmAtkutaH suptyAdAvAtmano.akAmatA syAt.h |

anena "so.ashnute sarvAnkAmAnsaha brahmaNA vipashchitA' iti shrutimupAdatte | paryetItyanena "sa tatra paryeti jakShankrIDan.hramamANaH' iti | jakShanniti vaidikatvAtsAdhuH | kAmAnnItyanena "imAँllokAnkAmAnnI kAmarUpyamanusaJNcharan.h | etatsAma gAyannAste' iti | Adipadena "sa ekadhA bhavatItyAdeH saN^grahaH | balAtkAmasadbhAvAvagateriti sheShaH | yadyepyetAH shrutayo na sAkShAnmuktasya kAmasadbhAvamAchakShate | tathA.api sAmarthyAttaM gamayantyeva | tadidamuktaM shrutibalAditi | tachcha sAmarthyamavyabhicharitameva na tu sambhAvanAmAtramiti sachChabdenAha | tathAhi | kAmakarmatvAddhi viShayAH kAmAH | karmaNi ghaJNo vidhAnAt.h | tayA cha so.ashnute sarvAnkAmAnityatra sannidhestatkAmakarmabhUtAnviShayAnashnuta ityuktaM syAt.h | niShkAmasya shilAsamasya kAmAvAptiH kIdR^ishI syAt.h | paryaTanAdikaM cha kAmakAryaM na vinAna kAmena sambhavati | strIbhirniShkAmasya smaraNamatyantAsambhAvitam.h | annAdInAM cha kAmatvaM kAmyatayaiveti pUrvavatkAmAvagatiH | yadyapi sa yadi pitR^ilokakAmo bhavatItyAdyA vispaShyAH shrutayo.atra santi tathA.api shiShyairnyAyamanusandadhAnairbhAvyamityetAsAmudAharaNam.h | muktasyAkAmatvAbhAvAnnAnaikAntyaM hetoriti |

iti shrutirityanvayaH | antaHkaraNasthAnAmeveti cha | natu sarvathA.apItyevArthaH | hishabdo yasmAdityarthe | tasmAdakAmaH syAtkathaM mukta iti sambandhaH | kutaH shruterarthasaN^kochaH kriyata ityata Aha- hR^idItyeveti ||

kutrachidindrAdipadavyatirikte kAminaH puMsaH kvachitkvachidindrAdipade kAmAbhAvAdindrAdisamAnasukhAnubhavo.astIti vyAkhyAne.anubhavavirodhaH syAt.h | rAjyamakAmayamAnasya rAjasamAnasukhAnubhUteranubhavabAdhitatvasya spaShyatvAt.h | vairAgyaprashaMsAto na tattvaM mArgaNIyamiti chenna | niravadhikAnandasvarUpo.ayamAtmA kAmAdyupadravAvaraNAttu tathA na bhAsate | ato yAvadyAvatkAmakShayastAvattAvadAnandotkarSho dR^ishyata ityasyArthasya pradarshanArthamasya prakaraNasyAvatAritatvAt.h | AnandotkarShe(.atra)tu tAtparyaM shataguNatve tu na nirbharaH kArya iti chenna | devapadAkAmAdindrapadAkAmasyAnandavisheShAdarshanAditi |

arthAntarapratIternirastatvAt.h | amuktamanuShyAdisukhasambandhitAratamyaM te ye shatamityAdivAkyaiH pR^ithak.h pR^ithaguktvA yashcheti shrotriyasya cheti cha vAkyena muktAnAM manuShyagandharvAdInAM sukhe tAratamyaM shrutiratideshenAheti vyAkhyAnameva peshalam.h |

nanvevaM tarhi kathaM bR^ihadAraNyakavAkyaM bhAShye muktamAtraviShayaM vyAkhyAtam.h | yashcheti visheShaNasamuchchayaparamuktam.h | ayamabhiprAyo bhAShyakArasya | sarvathA vAkyadvayamevedaM bhinnaviShayam.h | ekavAkyatAshraddhAyAmapi muktamAtraviShayamastu | tatrAnupapattInAmalpatvAt.h | nAmuktamAtraviShayam.h anupapattibAhulyAditi |
mAnuShAdihiraNyagarmAntAnAmamuktAnAM muktAnAM chottarottaraM shataguNAnandatvaM shrutidvayamAhetyayuktam.h | mAnuShAnandanirdesho muktaj~nApakAbhAvAt.h | nahi tatrAkAmahatatvAdikamanyadvA kimapi shrUyate ityAshaN^kAM nirAkurvan.h shrutyarthaM vivR^iNoti | rAddha itayAdinA.abhivIkShata ityantena | tatra tAvat.h bR^ihadAraNyake manuShyamuktasya j~nApakaM darshayati- rAddha iti || 
sa yo manuShyANAM rAddhaH samR^iddho bhavatItyupakramavAkye rAddha iti padena mukta eva gR^ihyate nAmuktaH | kayA vR^ittyA.abhidhayaiva na tUpacharyate | yena mukhyArthAnupapattyAdikaM vyutpAdanIyaM syAt.h | katham.h? saMsiddha iti | etaduktaM bhavati | rAdha sAdha saMsiddhAviti paThyate | rAdhadhAtoshcha "gatyarthAkarmakashliShashIN^.hsthA.a.asavasajanaruhajIryatibhyashcha' ityakarmakatvAtkartari ktaH | tato rAddhaH saMsiddha ityuktaM bhavati | saMsiddhishcha muktireva nityatvena duHkhAsambhinnatvena cha samIchInasiddhitvAt.h | netarA, anityatvena duHkhasambhinnatvena chAsamIchInatvAt.h | nacha mukhye sambhavatyamukhyArtho.aN^gIkartuM shakyata iti | evaM samR^iddhashabdo.api muktasyaiva vAchakaH | muktiM vinA samyagR^iddherabhAvAt.h | anyeShAmadhipatirityAdikaM tu muktAmuktasAdhAraNam.h | yathA  cha mukte sambhavati tathoktaM bhAShye |

evaM vAjasaneyashrutau "sa yo ha vai manuShyANAmityAdeH sampannatama ityantasya, taittirIyashrutau cha yuvA syAdityAdeH pUrNA syAdityantasya' muktAmuktaparatvavarNanena sa manuShyANAM parama Anando.atha(te)ye shataM manuShyANAmAnandA ityetatsa eko mAnuSha Anandaste ye shataM mAnuShA AnandA ityetachcha muktAmuktaviShayamiti siddhe taittirIyashrutigataM sa eko manuShyagandharvANAmAnandaH shrotriyasya chAkAmahatasyetyetAvadvayAchaShye- sa eka itIti ||

umAparyantaM tu pashchAtpashchAduktAH pUrvapUrvairdR^iShyebhyo dR^iShyAnAmanantAMshAneva vAsudevasya visheShashanvichakShate | shakrakAmAdayashcheti chastvarthaH | evashabdasyomAdibhirevetyanvayaH | prabuddhebhya iti pUrvavat.h ShaShThayarthe | chakShate pashyanti |
udAhR^itAnAM vachanAnAM prayojanamAha- ityAdIti ||
yathArthata iti || na paramatAnuvAdarUpeNetyarthaH | muktAnAM cha sAdhanAnAM cheti yojanA | sAdhanatAratamyapratipAdanAyodAhR^iteShveve keShuchidvAkyeShu muktAnAM tAratamyaM pratIyate | tadapi prakR^itatvAd.h grAhyamityarthaH |
astu mumukShUNAM sAdhaneShu tAratamyaM mA cha bhUmnokShe tAratamyamityAshaN^kAyAM prAgbAdhakamuktam.h | idAnIM shaN^kaivaiShA nopapadyate dUre dUShaNAbhidhAnamityAha- sAdhyeti ||
sAdhyamavichitraM sAdhanaM vichitramiti sAdhyasAdhanayorvairUpyaM kena bIjena kalpyate shaN^kayate na kenApi | ayamabhisandhiH | pakShe vipakShatvashaN^kA khalu kenachidbIjena syAt.h | nirbIjaM shaN^kamAno na laukiko nApi parIkShaka ityunmatta ivopekShaNIyaH | bIjaM cha vyabhichAradarshanaM vopAdhidasharnaM vA tayoranyatarashaN^kA vA | tatrAdyaM tAvadiha nAsti | tadidamAha- adR^iShyamiti ||
nApi dvitIyam.h | pakShe sAdhyasadbhAvasya shrutyAdisiddhatvena yasya kasyachidAshaN^kayamAnasyAvashyaM sAdhyavyApakatvAbhAvenopAdhitvAsambhavAt.h | pakShe.api tad.hvR^ittau sAdhanavyApakatvAt.h | ata evopAdhishaN^kA.api nirastA | tato vyabhichArashaN^kA.api | udAhR^itavAkyairvyApteruktatvAt.h | ato bIjAbhAvAchChaN^kaivaiShA.anupapanneti |
Ishvaro mumukShubhyo vichitraM phalaM dadAti vichitrasAdhanairArAdhitatvAt.h | vichitrasAdhanAnyapekShya phaladAtR^itvAdityanumAnAntaraM hR^idi nidhAyAnyathAsisiddhinirAsArthaM vipakShe bAdhakamAha- vaiShamyamiti ||
tena sAdhyasAdhanavairUpyeNa | dvitIyashchashabdaH pramANAntarasUchanArthaH | yadIshvaro.anuShThitAlpasAdhanAyAnuShThitamahAsAdhanasamAnaphalaM dadyAt.h | tadA.asau viShamaH prasajyeta | yadi vA.anuShThitamahAsAdhanAyAnuShThitAlpasAdhanasamAnaphalaM dadyAt.h | tadA nirghR^iNaH syAdityarthaH | 
Ishvarasya vaiShamyAdyApattirnAniShyA | duHkhAdyahetutvAdityata Aha- sApekShatvAditi ||
anena "vaiShamyanairghaNye vA sApekShatvAt.h' iti sUtramupAdatte | tau cheti sambandhaH | tau vaiShamyanairghaNyalakShaNau doShau | yaddhi pramANaviruddhamaprAmANikaM vA taduchyate.aniShyamiti | vaiShamyaM(myAdikaM)che(mI)shvarasya sUtrakAreNa vAritatvAtpramANaviruddhamiti kathaM nAniShyam.h | aN^gIkR^itasUtraprAmANyAnpratyayaM yatna iti nAsaN^gatiH | ye tu sUtraprAmANyamanaN^gIkR^ityeshvarasya vaiShamyAdyApatteriShyatvaM manyante | tAnprati vedAprAmANyahetutvena vaiShamyAderdoShatvaM sUchayituM pulliN^ganirdeshaH | anyathA prakaraNAtte vArite ityavakShyat.h | napuMsakaprayoge.api dUShaNe iti shakyate j~nAtumiti chenna | te vaiShamyanairghR^iNye iti nirAkAN^kShatvAt.h | 
prasaN^gasya viparyaye payarvasAnamupapAdayati- tAratamyAditi ||
sAdhanAnAM tAratamyAtsadaiva niyameneshato bhavataH sAdhyasya tAratamyaM parameshvare.avaiShamyAdihetuH syAt.h | ApAdakaviparyayasya khalvApAdyavipayaryaM prati nirvAhakatve bhavetprasaN^gasya viparyayaparyavasAnam.h | niragnikatvaviparyayo hi nirdhUmatvaviparyayaM ghaTayati | asti chaitatprakR^ita iti | 
yadvA kathaM vaiShamyAdi sUtrakAreNa vAritamityataH sApekShatvasya vaiShamyAdyabhAvena saha hetuhetumadbhAvaM vyutpAdayati- tAratamyAditi || pUrvaiva yojanA |
vyarthamidaM sUtrakArasya sAdhanasaMskArapUrvakarmApekShA.aN^gIkAreNa vaiShamyAdinivAraNam.h | phale tatparihAre.api sAdhanAdau parihartumashakyatvAt.h | tathAhi | sAdhanAdau parameshvarasya prayojakatvamasti na vA | neti pakShe parameshvaratvahAniH | Adye nirnimittaM vichitrANi sAdhanAni prayojayataH kathaM na vaiShamyAdItyato.anupapannasya sUtrasya kathaM bAdhakatvamiti | maivam.h | asyAkShepasya sUtrakR^itaiva nirastatvAdityAha- svAtantya iti ||
svAtantyaM prayojakakartR^itvAt.h | vaichityaM sAdhanAdeH | apekShya preraNAditi sheShaH | doSho vaiShamyAdiH | tadvachaH sUtrakR^ito vacho.asti |
nanvevaM savartra sApekShasya hareH svAtantyahAnirdoShaH syAdityata Aha- svatantya iti || ayamapi doSho nAsti | katham.h | pareshituH sAdhanAdau svAtante vidyamAne.api svechChayA.anAdivaichityamapekShya prerakatvamityetadarthapratipAdakaM tadvacho.asti yata iti | kiM tadvacha ityataH krameNa sUtradvayaM paThati- nAnAditvAditi ||
tatrAdyadoShaparihArAya "na karmAvibhAgAditi chennAnAditvAt.h' itrata sUtraM(maneno)upAdatte | dvitIyaparihArAya "upapadyate cha' iti | 
evamanumAnasyAnyathAsiddhiM nirasya bAdhakapratirodhau nirAkaroti- apekShyeti ||
tathAsthitirviShamateshvareNa kriyata iti sAdhyamAneti sheShaH | mayA pramANena | kayA na kayApi | paramaM sAmyamityAderanyathAvyAkh.hyAtatvaditi bhAvaH | anumAnAdervyAptipratipattaye dR^iShyAntamAha- rAjAdAviti ||
prekShAvati rAjAdau sevAnurUpaphaladAnaM vaiparItyakartaryaprekShAvati vaiShamyAdikaM cha dR^ishyata ityarthaH | sAdhyasAdhanavairUpyakalpane bAdhakAntaramAha- tyAga iti ||
sarvatra sAdhyasAdhanaikarUpyasya dR^iShyatvAttadvairUpyasya kvApyadR^iShyatvAtprakR^itavairUpyaM shaN^kamAnasya dR^iShyatyAgo.adR^iShyakalpanA cheti doShau prasajyete | nacha syAtAM tAviti shakyate vaktum.h | prekShAvatA kenApyanaN^gIkR^itatvAdityAha- suduShkaramiti || mAyAvAdino dR^iShyaM prapaJNchasya satyatvAdikaM tyajanti | adR^iShyamanirvAchyAdikaM kalpayanti | ato mAyibhyo.anyenetyuktam.h | asya chottaratropayogaH | anyairakR^itamapi dR^iShyatyAgAdikaM kurvatAM ko doSha ityata Aha- tatkimiti || 
tat.h tarhi | kimiti gUDhAbhiprAyaH prashnaH | atra dR^iShyatyAgAdyanuShThAnaviShaye | anugamyante anusriyante | etaduktaM bhavati | dR^iShyatyAgAdiprasaN^gena mAyAvAdino dUShayatAM punaratra dR^iShyatyAgAdikaM svayaM kurvatAM vyAhatiH syAditi |
sAdhyasAdhanayorvairUpyaM shaN^kamAnasyAniShyAntaramAha- shruteti || uktavidhayA sAdhyasAdhanasArUpyasya shrutatvAdanyathA chAshrutatvAdatra vairUpyAN^gIkAre shrutahAnyashrutagrahAvapi syAtAm.h | mAyinAM liN^ge iti tayorvisheShaNaM prayuJNjAnasyokta evAbhisandhiH | mAyAvAdino hi shrutaM sArvaj~nAdyupetaM brahma parityajyAshrutaM nirguNamupayanti |

tat.h tatra prakR^itadoSheShu | tato dR^iShyatyAgAdeShaH | adhikA bahirbhUtAH | dR^iShyatyAgAdikaM kurvANenAnyadapi pramitaM tyAjyaM syAt.h | adR^iShyakalpanAdikaM cha kurvatA.aprAmANikamanyadapi kalpanIyaM bhavediti(tyarthaH) bhAvaH | 
syAdetat.h | yadi muktAstAratamyopetAH syustadA parasparaM dveShavantaH syuriti pratikUlatarkaparAhataM muktatAratamyAnumAnamityata Aha- nishsheSheti ||
nishsheSheNa gatA apagatA doShA yebhyAste tathoktAH | punaH shravaNAdimatAmiti sheShaH | teShAM harerAparokShyamiti tAnprati harerAparokShya(raparokShatva)mityarthaH | anubandhAdibhya ityatra pratipAdito.ayamartha iti hishabdaH | yasmAdityarthe vA | dveSherShyAdidoShastatastasmAtkuto muktAnAM nApAdayituM shakyata ityarthaH | 
etaduktaM bhavati | ye tAratamyopetAste dveShAdimanto dR^iShyA yathA laukikAH puruShA iti khalvatra vyAptirabhidhAtavyA | nachaivam.h | laukikAnAM dveShAdimattve doShitvasyaiva prayojakatvAt.h | yatra dveShAdimattvaM tatra doShitvamita vyApterdarshanam.h | nacha doShitvaM mukteShu

nanu pareNApi na mukteShu dveShAdimattvaM sAdhyate kintvApAdyata iti | tatasstebhyastadvayAvR^ittisAdhanamasaN^gatam.h | maivam.h | tarkamUlabhUtavyAptAvupAdhiH khalvatra kathitaH | tasya cha pakShAdvayAvR^ittiH svavyAvR^ittyA vivakShitadharmavyAvartanashaktishchAvashyaketi tad.hvyutpAdanasya kriyamANatvAt.h | atra dveSherShyAsantApapareShyapratighAtaprayatnechChA vyApyAH | avidyA.ahaN^kArAdyA vyApakA iti vivekaH |

ataH kimityata Aha- yadIti ||
yadyevaM doShANAmeva dveShAdikAraNatvam.h | tatra mukteShu | nirdoShatA chAN^gIkR^itA | tadA Adhikyena hInAdhikabhAvenAN^gIkR^itena | kiM dUShyate na kimapi | sAmyamaN^gIkurvANenApi nirdoShatayaiva dveShAdiprasaN^go vAraNIyaH | tAratamyamaN^gIkurvANairasmAbhirapi tathaiva nirAkariShyate | iyAMstu visheShaH | yattAratamyaM pramitaM na sAmyamiti samudAyArthaH |

bhavedetadyadi sAmyena prasaktaM dveShAdikaM nirdoShatayA nivArayAmaH | nachaivam.h | kinnAma samasattAmAtraM hi na dveShAdikAraNamatiprasaN^gAt.h | api tarhi samadarshanam.h | nacha muktaH samaM muktAntaraM pashyatyato na dveShAdIti | evaM tarhi na tAratamyasattAmAtraM dveShAdikAraNaM kintu svato.adhikadarshanameva | nacha muktaH svato.adhikaM muktAntaraM pashyati | tasmAtsatyapi tAratamye na dveShAdiprasaN^ga iti kuto na santoShyavyamiti parihAro.atra shakyate vaktum.h | tathA.api nAsau tAttvika ityanyadarshanAbhAvameva dUShayati- adarshanAditi ||

"j~nAnamapratighaM yasya vairAgyaM cha jagatpateH | aishvaryaM chaiva dharmashcha sahasiddhaM chatuShyayam.h' ityevaM pramitasyApItyarthaH | pUrvam.h AdikAle | shrutAviti jAtAvekavachanam.h | tAH shrutIrarthataH paThati- naiveti ||

tat.h tatra muktau | tatra anyadarshanaviShaye | ichChA naivAstIti mR^iShaiva kalpya teyadIti yojanA | bhidyate hR^idayagranthirityAdishrutyuktA | svayaM sAkShAchChatyukteti sambandhaH | tarhIti sheShaH | tachChabdo vA tarhyarthaH | idamuktaM bhavati | muktAnAM sAmyamaN^gIkR^ityAnyadarshanAbhAvena dveShAdiparihR^ityAnyadarshanechChAbhAvena chAratyAdikaM pariharato.aprAmANikAnekakalpanaM prAmANikaparityAgashcha syAtAm.h | sAmAnyadarshanAbhAvenAbhAvavatadichChAbhAvAnAmaprAmANikatvAt.h | tAratamyAdeH prAmANikatvAt.h

uchyate | muktAstadAnIntanena parasparaM tAratamyenopetAshchetanatvAtsaMsAriNo yathetyayamartho.atra vivakShitaH | tAratamyaM cha kutashchiddhInatvaM kutashchidadhikatvamityetayoranyataraditi noktadoShaH | sAmAnyasya cha visheShanirAsenApAkaraNe chAtiprasaN^gaH | yadvA maktyuttarakShaNavartI muktaH prAg.h yato.adhikatvahInatvAbhyAmupetasvarUpo.abhUdidAnImapi tAbhyAmupeta iti pratij~nArtho vaNarnIyaH | sAmAnyata eva vyAptirabhidhAtavyeti |

|| iti kAmachArAdhikaraNam.h ||
|| atha ubhayaliN^gAdhikArikAdhikaraNe ||
|| OM sarvathA.api tu ta evobhayaliN^gAt.h OM || OM na chAdhikArikamapi patanAnumAnAttadayogAt.h OM || atra prathamAdhikaraNe.anAdij~nAnayogyatAvatAmevaj~nAnaprAptirnAnyeShAmityuktam.h | dvitIye cha devatAdipadaprAptiranAditadyogyatopetAnAmeva netareShAmityabhihitam.h | seyaM jIvAnAM nAnAvidhAnAdiyogyatA prasiddhaistaistaiH kAraNairutkarShAparkaprAptirbhavatIti vadadbhirvAdibhirnAbhyupagamyate.atastAM sAdhayitumAha- anAdIti ||

bhagavAnnirdoSha iti yatprAguktaM tatsamarthanArthamuttaro granthaH | nanu "na sthAnato.api' ityAdinaiva samarthitametat.h | satyam.h | yuktyAdinA prAptaM sadoShatvaM tatrApAkR^itam.h | atra tu pratyakShaprAptamiti bhedAt.h | etadapi tatraiva kuto na dUShitamiti chet.h | vishvAdiShu pratyakShasyApravR^itteH | prAsaN^gikaM tu nirAkaraNaM tatra vA.atra vA na kashchidvisheShaH | prAguktArthaprapaJNchashchAtrAnubhAShyakR^itA kriyate | muktatAratamyAdeH prapaJNchanAdeH | ato.atraiva nirdoShatAprapaJNchanaM yuktam.h | kiJNchAtra j~nAnasvarUpanirUpaNaM bhaviShyati tatprasaN^gashcha j~nAnapAde samuchitaH | api cha na bhagavatsAkShAtkAramAtreNAsheShapuruShArthaprAptiH kintu nirdoShAdbhagavaddarshanAdityuktam.h | tachchAnena nirdoShabhagavaddarshanamupadarshitaM bhavati | tarhi tatraivAyaM granthasandarbhaH kuto na niveshita iti chet.h | devadAnavamAnavasvabhAvaprapaJNchanasyAtropayuktatvena tadAnantaryopapatteH | tathAcha vakShyAmaH |

tatashcha sarveShAM svAtantAnupapatteH | keShAJNchitpAratantyam.h | evamanye.api bhedAnuShaN^giNo doShA draShyavyAH | samAnanyAyatvAt.h | vedAdhidoShAshcha pratyakSheNekShyanta iti na bhagavato nirdoShatvamiti | tatra tAvadbhedasya pratyakShasiddhatAM nirAkartumAgamavAkyaM paThati- nacheti ||
cho.avadhAraNe | anyabhedavaditi vyatirekadR^iShyAntaH | anyeShAM ghaTAdInAM yathA.anekatvAtirikto.anyonyAbhAvalakShaNo bhedo dR^ishyate na tatheti | viShNau bhedo na dR^ishyata ityevokte.anekatvasyApyadarshanaM pratIyeta tadarthamidaM vachanam.h | yadvA yathA viShNAvanyapratiyogiko bhedo dR^ishyate na tathA svapratiyogika iti yojanA | anyathA ghaTAdipratiyogiko.api bhedo na dR^ishyata ityapi pratIyeta | athavA.anyapratiyAgikabhedavati viShNAvityaikapadyena vyAkhyeyam.h | prayojanaM tUktameva | viShNau rAmakR^iShNAdirUpe | adhunAtanairbhedo na dR^ishyata iti parasyApi sammatam.h | atastaddarshinAmapItyuktam.h | tR^itIyArthe ShaShThI | avatAradarshibhirapItyarthaH | taddarshinAM pratyakSheNApIti vA | svabhAvata eva jIvAstrividhAH | devadAnavamAnavabhedAt.h | tatra daivaM pratyakShaM tAvadavatArANAM parasparaM na bhedaM gocharayatIti bhAvaH |

nanu bahutvaM bhedena vinA.a.anupapadyamAnaM tamAkShipati | tathA cha bahurUpeShu pratyabhij~nA na sambhavatyeva | sambhavantI vA bhrAntiH syAdityata Aha- bahutvaM cheti ||
bhagavadrUpANAmiti sheShaH | anyathopapattikuNThitArthApattirna bhedaM pramApayatItyarthaH | anyathA.apyupapattipakShe bhedasandehaH syAtso.apyaniShya ityanyathaivopapattiM sUchayati- na bhedeneti ||
upapadyata ityubhayatra sheShaH | kutaH | bhagavadrUpANAM bhede niravakAshapramANAbhAvAttadvirodhAchcha | tadidamAha- kathaJNchaneti ||
evamuttamAnAM puMsAM bhagavadekarUpadarshanasamaye rUpAntarapratItAvasatyAM tato bhedaj~nAnamasambhAvitam.h | pratiyogij~nAnAbhAve bhedaj~nAnAbhAvasya niyatatvAt.h | satyAmapi tathA virodhinyAH pratyabhij~nAyA bhAvAdityuktam.h | tathA.api madhyamAdijanAnAM pratyakShaM bhagavadrUpabhede pramANaM bhaviShyati | ekarUpadarshanasamaye rUpAntarapratItyabhAve bhedadarshanAnupapattAvapi tadbhAve sambhavatyeva | nacha teShAmapi pratyabhij~nA bhavadbhirabhyupetuM shakyate | uttamatvaprasaN^gAdityato madhyamAnapekShya tAvadAha- pratyabhij~nA cheti ||
chastvarthaH | yeShAM tu madhyamAnAM janAnAM pratyabhij~nA bhagavadrUpeShu nAsti te.api tatra bhedaM naiva pashyantIti yojanA | pratyabhij~nAbhAve kAraNaM tena bhagavatA muShyApahatA dR^iShyireShAmiti | tena bahutveneti vA | bhagavadichChAyA teShAM yogyatayA chopodbalitaM bahutvamupalabhyamAnaM pratIyamAne(.api) vastuni vidyamAnasyApyabhedasya j~nAnaM pratibadhnAti | atra tanmuShyadR^iShyayaste.apItyanuvAdAttanmuShyadR^iShyitvAtpratyabhij~naiShAM nAstIti labhyate | 
bhagavadrUpe bhedaM naiva pashyantItyukte ghaTAdibhyo.api bhedaM na pashyantIti mandasya pratItiH syAttAM nivArayitumAha- bhedamiti ||
anyebhyo bhedaM pashyantyeva cheti yojanA | 
nanu pratIyamAnaM vastudvayaM bhedena vA pratIyate.abhedena vA | bhedAbhedodAsInatayA tu pratItiH kathamityata Aha- evamiti ||
teShAM yogyateti sheShaH | anyathA gatibuddhItyAdinA karmasaMj~nAyAM dvitIyA syAt.h | vibhaktivyatyayo vA ChAndasaH | anyathA bhedenAbhedena cha darshayati | yathA khalvakhyAtavAdinAM sahakArisAmarthyAdbhedAbhedaudAsInyena vastupratItiH | yathA vA.anyeShAM shuktikAshakaladarshanAnantaraM vyAsaktau | tathA parameshvarashaktyA.atrApi tathA pratItau ko virodhaH | adhamajIvapratyakShasya tvanyA gatirbhaviShyati | evamIshvararUpabhede pratyakShaM nirAkurvatA.anumAnamapi nirAkR^itam.h | bahutvasyAnyathAsiddheruktatvAt.h | tannyAyena chAkAravisheShAdInAmanyathAsiddhatvAditi | vachanam.h astIti sheShaH | 
mA bhUdbhagavadrUpabhedaH pratyakShAnumAnasiddhaH | Agamasiddhastu bhaviShyati | purANeShu tatra tatrAnyAdishabdashravaNAditi chenna | neha nAnAsti kiJNchanetyAdivedavAkyavirodhAt.h | purANameva vedasya kinna bAdhakaM bhavatItyata Aha- neti ||
vachanamiti vartate | purANavachanaM khalu lokAnAM yadbhagavadrUpeShu bhedadarshanaM tadanuvAdaparameva | na vastuniShTham.h | upakramAdinA tathA.avagamAt.h | vedastu vastutathAtve tAtparyavAn.h | liN^gaiH tathA.adhyavasAyAt.h | ato na tat.h tadbAdhanAya shaknoti |
nanvetadvayAhatam.h | yatprAgbhagavadrUpabhedaviShayaM pratyakShaM nAstItyuktam.h | idAnIntu tadastIti | tasyaivAbhAve purANavachanasya tadanuvAditvAnupapatteH | maivam.h | bahutvAdyanumAnAbhAsajanitabhedadasharnAnuvAditvopapatteH | 
kiJNchottamamadhyamAnAM bhedaviShayaM pratyakShaM nAstItyabhihitam.h | adhamAnAM tu tadastItyadhunA aN^gIkriyate | tarhi tadeva bhagavadrUpabhede pramANaM bhaviShyatItyapi na vAchyam.h | uttamAnAmabhedaviShayeNa pratyakSheNa bAdhitatvAt.h | nacha tadeva nAsti | pratyabhij~naiva bahurUpeShu dR^ishyata ityAgamoktatvAt.h | tathAcha bhIShmavAkyam.h | "tamimamahamajaM sharIrabhAjAM hR^idi hR^idi viShThitamAtmakalpitAnAm.h | pratidR^ishamiva naikadhArkamekaM samadhigato.asmi vidhUtabhedamohaH ||' iti |
atha bhedadarshanamevAbhedadarshanasya bAdhakaM kuto na bhavatItyata Aha- aparIkShiteti ||
aparIkShitA parIkShayA pramANatvenAnishchitA | netyasyAnukarShaNArthashchashabdaH | parIkShApUrvaH prAmANyanishchayo yasya darshanasya tatparIkShApUrvadarshanam.h | parIkShApUvarM darshanaM prAmANyanishchayo yasya pratyakShasyeti vA | kvApItyanena niyamamAha | tadanena yatparIkShayA na nishchitaprAmANyaM j~nAnaM na tannimittaprAmANyaM j~nAnAntaraM bAdhata iti vyAptiruktA | parIkShAgrahaNaM prAmANyanishchayopalakShaNameva, natu niyamArthamityuttaratra sphuTIbhaviShyati |
atra dR^iShyAntamAha- devadatteti ||
yathA yaj~nadattAdAvanishchiprAmANyA devadattAdidR^iShyirna nishchitaprAmANyAM yaj~nadattAdidR^iShyiM bAdhate tathetyarthaH | tataH kiM yadyevaM vyAptiriti chet.h | bhedadarshanamanishchitaprAmANyamabhedadasharnaM tu nishchitaprAmANyam.h | ato na tattasya bAdhakaM kintu vaiparItyameveti vadAmaH | 
kuto bhedadarshanamanishchitaprAmANyamityata Aha- na cheti ||
cho.avadhAraNe | kvachitpradeshe | hishabdo hetau | parameshvararUpabhedaviShayaM pratyakShaM tAvadasmAkaM purANavAkyAdeva siddham.h | purANavAkyaM cha kechidbhedaM pashyantIti vA pratipAdayatu | anuvAdakatayA liN^gatvena vA | atastatprAmANyanishchayastata evAnveShyavyaH | nacha bhedadarshanasya prAmANyaM nishchAyayatpurANavAkyamasti | ataH pramANAbhAvAnna bhedadasharnasya prAmANyanishchaya iti bhAvaH | 
prAmANyanishchayo dvAbhyAM prakArAbhyAM bhavati | arthatathAtvanishchayena vA j~nAnaparIkShayA vA | AdyAbhiprAyeNoktaM satyatayA nishchitabhedasyeti | dvitIyAbhiprAyeNa tu bhedasya darshana iti samAsaH | ShaShThayA Akrosha ityaluk.h | nishchitaM parIkShitaM cha tadbhedasyadarshanaM cheti tathoktam.h | tatra svAbhiprAyeNAkroshaH parAbhiprAyeNa nishchitatvamityavirodhaH |
yadi purANavAkyA(deva)nnishchitaprAmANyaM bhedadarshanaM na pratIyeta tarhi kIdR^ishaM tatpratIyata ityata Aha- sammugdhamiti ||
pramANatvApramANatvAbhyAM sandigdham.h | dasharnaM bhedasya | tatra purANavAkye | etaduktaM bhavati | purANavAkyaM bhedadarshanamAtraM gamayati | na tu tasya prAmANyamaprAmANyaM vA | tataH prAgabhedadarshanAvagamAttatra prAmANyAprAmANyasandeha eva yuktaH | avagate tvabhedadarshane tasyAprAmANyameva nishchIyate | purANavAkyAdeva tatprAmANyasya nishchitatvAt.h | samadhigatosmIti saMshabdashravaNAt.h | hR^idi hR^idi naikadhA sthitamapItyanumAnAnAmAbhAsatvasyoktatvAt.h | vidhUtabhedamoha iti bhedaj~nAnasya mohatvAbhidhAnAchcheti | evaM bhagavadrUpeShu bhedAbhAvaH siddhaH | tathA vedhAdidoShAbhAvashcha | pramANAbhAvAt.h | 
nanvasti taddarshitA pratyakShamatra pramANam.h | maivam.h | mahatAM pratyakSheNa vedhAdyabhAvagrAhiNA bAdhitatvAt.h | idameva tasya bAdhakaM kinna syAdityata Aha- aparIkShitameveti ||
atra vedhAdi(doSha)tadabhAvayormadhye | adhIshituratrAvatAreShviti vA | dR^ishyata iti sambandhaH | yadvA vedhAdikamiti taddarshanamupalakShyate | parIkShayA yuktaM darshanaM parIkShAdarshanam.h | yadvA parIkShyata iti parIkShA | guroshcha hala ityakArapratyayaH | parIkShA cha taddasharnaM cha tasmin.h | dR^ishyate vedhAdikaM kvachit.h | doShadarshanamaparIkShitaM nirdoShatvadarshanaM tu parIkShitamiti bhAvaH | 
nanu doShAbhAvaviShayaM mahatAM pratyakShaM tAvatkutaH siddhamityata Aha- nirdoShameveti || 
adrAk.h adrAkShIt.h | anityamAgamashAsanamiti vachanAt.h | purandaro.adrAkShIt.h | anyairapi surottamaiH | sadoShA dR^iShyAH | tasmAnnirdoSho harireka eva | chashabdaH shrutyantarasamuchchayArthaH | asya parameshvarasya viShaye mahatAM darshanaM sadoShaM doShagrAhi naiva, kintu nirdoShameva gR^ihNAtIti |
doShadasharnamaparIkShitaM tadabhAvadarshanaM tu parIkShitametatkuta ityata Aha- aviddha iti ||
aviddhamiva viddhavat.h | ChAndaso dvitIyAntAdvatiH | evashabdasyAviddha ityAdinA sambandhaH | darshayatyAtmAnam.h | pUrvashrutyA.apyayamartho.arthAtsiddhayatIti paiN^gishrutishchetyuktam.h | nirdoShatAmiti phaloktyA vivakShitamarthamupalakShayati | atraiva spaShyAM shrutimudAharati- aparIkShiteti ||
Aha doShadarshanasyAparIkShitatvaM nirdoShatAdarshanasya parIkShitatvaM cha | tataH kimityata Aha- pramANaM hIti ||
yatparIkShitaM parIkShayA pramANatvenAvadhR^itaM tadeva pramANam.h | aparIkShitaM tvApAtataH sandigdham.h | nishchitavirodhyupanipAte tvapramANameva | ataH parIkShitena nirdoShatAdarshanenAparIkShitaM doShadarshanameva bAdhyate | natu viparyayaH | prAmANyanishchaye parIkShopayogaH pramANasiddha iti hishabdaH | tathAcha vakShyate | 
atra kechidAhuH | svata eva j~nAnAnAM prAmANyaM (gR^ihyate) natu parIkShAdhInam.h | sakalamapi j~nAnaM svaprakAshaM yathArthaM cha | ataH svenaiva svayaM svaprAmANyaM cha siddhayati kA tatra parIkShApekSheti | anye tu bruvate | j~nAnaM tatprAmANyaM chAnumAnenaiva gR^ihyata iti | apare tu vadanti | j~nAnaM tatprAmANyaM cha sAkShiNaiva j~nAyata iti | yadi cha svataHprAmANyagraho na syAttarhi na syAdeva | tasya parIkShAdhInatve.anavasthAprasaN^gAt.h | anumAnavisheShaH khalu parIkShA nAma | tatprAmANyAvadhAraNaM cha parIkShAntareNeti kathaM nAnavasthA syAditi | tatra pAmANyagrahasya parIkShAdhInatve.anavasthAprasaN^gaM tAvatpariharati- neti ||
prAmANyagrahaNasya parIkShAdhInatvAN^gIkAre.apIti sheShaH | tatra hetumAha- sAkShIti ||
dvividhaM khalu j~nAnamantaHkaraNapariNAmarUpaM sAkShirUpaM cheti | tatrAdyAdvisheShyuM tushabdaH | etaduktaM bhavati | syAdiyamanavasthA yadi savartra parIkShA.apekShA syAt.h | na chaivam.h | sandigdhe khalvarthe parIkShA.apekShyate na tvasandigdhe | saMshayashcha manovR^ittiviShaye pAnIyAdau bhavati na punaH sAkShisiddhe sukhAdau | atastAvadeva parIkShA yAvatsAkShigR^ihIteShu sukhAdiShvavatAra iti kuto.anavastheti | prapaJNchitashchAyamartho.asmAbhiH prakR^ityadhikaraNe | 
manovR^ittiviShaya eva saMshayo na sAkShisiddha ityatra kiM kAraNamityata Aha- mAnasa iti ||
manaHpariNatirUpe doShAH kAraNatayA sambhAvitAH syuH | vaishabdastushabdArthe | ayamarthaH | dvividho hi saMshayo bhavati | ekastAvadAdita eva | yathA sthANuvarA.ayaM puruSho veti | aparastu nishchayapR^iShThabhAvI | yathA sthANutayA(vadayaM) pratIyate sthANurbhavati na veti | tatrAdyo visheShAdarshanAdidoShamUlaH | dvitIyo.api prathamaj~nAnasya doShajanyatvashaN^kAmUlaH | doShAshcha mAnasa eva darshane sambhavanti | atastatsaMshayAtmakaM vA jAyate nishchayatayA jAtasya viShaye vA AhAyarH saMshayo bhavati | natu sAkShi(siddhe)darshane doShasambhavaH | ato na tatsaMshayAtmakaM nApi (sAkShisiddhe)tatsiddhe.arthe saMshaya iti |
mAnase darshane doShAH sambhavantIti sphuTam.h | sAkShidarshane na sambhavantItyetatkuta ityata Aha- sudR^iDha iti ||
sudR^iDhaH kadA.api bAdharahitaH | nirNayo.avadhAraNAtmakaH pratyayaH | yatreti nipAto ya ityarthe | idamuktaM bhavati | doShAstAvajj~nAnasya DolAyamAnatAdarshanena balavadbAdhakopanipAtena vA kalpyAH | yathoktam.h | "balavatpramANatashcha'(shchaiva j~neyA doShA na chAnyatA') iti | sAkShidarshanaM cha nirNayAtmakameva bhavati na cha bAdhyata ityupapAditaM pR^ithagadhikaraNe | ataH pramANAbhAvAnna tatra doShaH sambhavati | 
sAkShisiddhe.arthe saMshayo nAstItyuktaM tadanubhavArUDhaM kartuM sAkShisiddhamarthaM tAvadAha- ichCheti ||
Adipadena prayatnadveShAvetadabhAvAshcha gR^ihyante | tataH kimityata Aha- neti ||
tatra kvachiditi sambandhaH | na jAtu mama sukhamasti na veti saMshayo nApi pratIyamAnamidaM sukhaM sadasadveti saMshaya iti hishabdenAha | 
sAkShidarshanamabAdhitameveti na yujyate shuktirajatAdau bAdhadarshanAt.h | nahi pratItisamayamAtravartini tatrAnyaj~nAnaM sambhavatItyata Aha- yadIti ||
yaddarshanaM kvachichChuktirajatAdau viShaye vyabhichAri bAdhitaM syAttachchakShurAdikaraNakaM manaHpariNatirUpameva na sAkShirUpam.h | kuta etat.h | mAnasadarshanasya bAdhyatvAN^gIkAre.aniShyAbhAvAt.h | sAkShiNastu tathAtve sarvavyavahAravilopaprasaN^gasyoktatvAt.h | tadidamuktaM hishabdena | sambhavati chAsya mAnasatvamanyathAkhyAtisamarthanAditi |
mAnasasya darshanasya doShabAdhasambhavo.abhihitaH | kIdR^ishasya tarhi prAmANyamityata Aha- mana iti ||
manashchakShushshabdau shrotrAderupalakShakau | darshanaM sAkShAtkAraH | Adipadena laiN^gikashabdaj~nAnasaN^grahaH | indriyaliN^gashabdakaraNakasya manovR^itterj~nAnasyetyatharH | nirdhAraNe ShaShThI | sambhAvitadoShabAdhasyApItyaperarthaH | yatra j~nAne sugR^ihItaM parIkShayA nishchitaM tatparIkShitadarshanaM pramANamiti sheShaH | pratyakShAgamaj~nAnaprAmANyagrahaNa eva parIkShopayogaH, dharmij~nAnAnumAnopamAnAnuvyavasAyAnAM tu prAmANyagrahaNaM na parIkShApekShamiti kechinmanyante | tannirAsAya sarvamAnasasaN^grahArthaM manashchakShurdarshanAdermadhya ityuktam.h | anyathA yatra j~nAna ityAdikamevAvakShyat.h | tadeve pramANamityetAvatA pUrNe parIkShitadarshanamityanuvAdena sugR^ihItamityetadvivR^iNoti | 
evaM mAnasapratyakShAdij~nAnaprAmANyagrahasya parIkShAdhInatve.api sAkShiprAmANyagrahasya tadanapekShatvAnna parIkShA.anavasthetyuktam.h | tatra kimanayA dvividhakalpanayA | sAkShivatpratyakShAdij~nAnasyApi prAmANyagrahaH parIkShAnapekSha evoktavidhayA svataH kinna syAdityAshaN^kAM pariharati- neti || 
j~nAnasya dR^iShyirj~nAnadR^iShyiH | tasya j~nAnasya | 
etaduktaM bhavati | vR^ittij~nAnAnAM svaprakAshatvameva tAvadasat.h | pramANAbhAvAt.h | j~nAnavyavahArasya sAkShivedyatvenaivopapatteH | idamahaM jAnAmItyanubhavasya sAkShirUpatvAt.h | vimataM j~nAnaM na svaprakAshamanAtmatvAtkAryatvAdanityatvAnmanorUpatvAtsukhAdivadityAdipramANavirodhAchcha |
bhavatu vA j~nAnaM svaprakAshaM tathA.api svarUpamAtra eva na tu svadharme prAmANye.api | tathA hi | vedavAkyashravaNe sati bAhyasya vAkyArthaj~nAnamutpadyate na vA | na dvitIyaH | satyAM sAmagyrAM kAryAnudayAnupapatteH | anyathA mImAMsakasyApi tadanudayaprasaN^gAt.h | Adye.api tatprakAshate na vA | neti pakShe.apasiddhAntaH | prathame tatprAmANyaM prakAshate na vA | nAdyaH | tannirA(sasyAnu)sAnupapatteH | tato j~nAnadR^iShyimAtreNa na j~nAnaprAmANyaM dR^ishyata iti dvitIya evAN^gIkAryaH | tathAcha svaprakAshaj~nAnenaiva prAmANyagraha iti kathaM syAt.h | apauruSheyatvAdiyuktibhiH prabodhito bAhyaH pratipadyate cha tatprAmANyamiti kathaM na parIkShApekShatvam.h | anyathA vaidikaj~nAnaprAmANye vipratipattireva na syAt.h j~nAnasvarUpavat.h | kiJNchaivaMvAdino mate shuktirajatAdivibhramo na syAt.h | idamanubhavasya rajatasmaraNasya cha bhedAgraho hi vibhramaH | tatra prAmANyavadbhedasyAnubhavatvasmaraNatvayoshcha prakAsho.avashyambhAvIti kathaM vibhramAvakAshaH | nahi prAmANyasya bhedAdeshcha kashchidvisheSho.astIti | Joshi-30
्JNAnaprAmANye sahaivAnumeye ityapyasat.h | j~nAnasyA(pya)numeyatve pramANAbhAvAt.h | tadvayavahArasyAnyathaivopapatteH | AshutaravinAshino j~nAnasya jAnAmIti vartamAnatayA pratibhA(sA).anupapatteshcha | aparokShAvabhAsavirodhAchcha | anumeyatve.api j~nAnasya na j~nAnAnumitimAtreNa prAmANyaM tasya dR^ishyate | taddhi j~nAtatayA vyavahAreNa kAryeNa vA.anumAtavyam.h | nacha tAvatA prAmANyamanumAtuM shakyate | vyabhichArAt.h | tato j~nAtatAdimAtreNa pratIte j~nAne bAdhAbhAvAdinA prAmANyamanumeyam.h | anyathA bAhyAnAmapi vaidikaj~nAnaprAmANyAnumAnaprasakteH | prasaktamapyapodyata iti chet.h | tarhyapavAdanirAsAya parIkShApekShAvashyambhAvinItyAgatam.h | idameva chAsmAbhirabhidhAsyate, sarvathA parIkShA.anapekSheti tu na kShamyate | 
etena sAkShivedyatApakSho.api pratikShiptaH | aupaniShadaj~nAnadR^iShyimAtreNa bAhyaistatprAmANyasyAdarshanAt.h | 
chaturthapakShastvatimandaH | anumAnAdij~nAnadR^iShyimAtreNa tatprAmANyasya chArvAkAdibhiradR^iShyatvAt.h | vibhAge mAnAbhAvAchcha | dharmij~nAnAdiprAmANye vigAnAbhAvAditi che(t.h)nna | nirAlambanAdimatadarshanAt.h | upapattibAdhitaM taditi chet.h | tarhi svIkR^itA.a.apyuShmataiva parIkShApekShetyalaM pallaveneti |
evaM tarhi pratyakShAdivatsAkShiNo.api prAmANyaM parIkShApekShagrahaNamevAN^gIkriyatAm.h | dvidhA kalpanasyAnyAyyatvAdityata Aha- niyameneti ||
dR^ishyata iti vartate | sAkShI gocharo yasya tattathoktam.h | gocharatvaM chAshrayatayA vivakShitam.h | sukhAdiviShaye yatsAkShigataM prAmANyaM tanniyamena dR^ishyate | etaduktaM bhavati | yadi vR^ittij~nAnAnAmiva sAkShij~nAnasyApi prAmANyaM taddarshanamAtreNa na dR^ishyate tadA.adhikamapi kAraNaM kalpayAmaH | nachaivam.h | sukhaj~nAne dR^iShye tatprAmANyAj~nAnasaMshayaviparyayANAM kadA.apyadarshanAd.h | kalpakasadbhAve dvidhA kalpanasyAdUShaNatvAditi |
kiJNcha sAkShiprAmANyasyApi parIkShApekShagrahaNatve.anavasthA cha syAt.h | nanu prAmANyagrahaNamabhilaShatA nAnavasthAto bhettuM yuktam.h | parIkShA.anavasthAbhAve.api grAhakAnavasthAyA duShpariharatvAdityata Aha- svaprAmANyamiti ||
sAkShyeveti sambandhaH | sadA sunishchayAditi | parIkShAnapekShameveti yAvat.h | etachchAnubhavAnyathA.anupapattibhyAM kalpyate | 
nanvevaM sati vR^ittij~nAnAnAM parataHprAmANyamuktaM syAt.h | j~nAnasvarUpasya sAkShivedyatvAt.h | prAmANyasya parIkShAgamyatvAt.h | tathAcha na vilakShaNatvAditi yatsvataH prAmANyamiShyaM tattyaktaM syAdityata Aha- j~nAnasyeti ||
j~nAnasya grAhakeNa sAkShiNaiva j~nAnasya mAnatAyA miteH kAraNAtsvataHprAmANyamiShyata eveti sambandhaH | bhavetsvataHprAmANyatyAgo yadi j~nAnameva sAkShivedyaM na prAmANyamiti brUmaH | na chaivam.h | j~nAnavattatprAmANyasyApi sAkShivedyatvAbhyupagamAditi | kimarthaM tarhi parIkShAvashyambhAvo.abhyupagamyata ityata Aha- doSheti ||
sAkShiNA nishchitatvamiti vakShyamANamihApi yojyam.h | iti prAmANyasyeti padadvayamadhyAhAryam.h | j~nAnaM gR^ihNansAkShI karaNadoShAbhAve.asya prAmANyamityeva prAmANyaM nishchinoti | natu pramANamevedamiti | tataH kimityata Aha- doShAbhAvasyeti ||
parIkShayeti sheShaH | cho.avadhAraNe | kvachideva prayojanavashAjjij~nAsAyAM jAtAyAM parIkShAlAbhe chetyarthaH | doShAbhAvanishchayArthA parIkShA na tu prAmANyagrahaNArthA | tatpunarj~nAnamiva sAkShivedyameva | ato na svataHprAmANyaparityAga iti bhAvaH | 
syAdetadyadIyaM prakriyA pramANavatI syAnna cha tadastItyata Aha- ata iti ||
ata eva hi sarveShAM j~nAnAnAM prAmANyaM prathamato na nishchitaM bhavet.h | kinnAma yatra yadA parIkShAsahakR^itena sAkShiNA prAmANyaM nishchitaM bhavati tattadaiva prAmANyaM svalakShaNaM prAmANyasvarUpamaprAmANyaviviktaM prAmANyaM siddhayati | idamuktaM bhavati | yadi sAkShI doShAbhAve pramANametaditi prathamaM sammugdhaM prAmANyaM gR^ihItvA pashchAjjij~nAsAyAM satyAM parIkShayA pramANamevetyavadhArayatItyeShA prakriyA nAN^gIkriyeta tadA.anabhyastaviShayANAM shabdAdinA jAtAnAM sarveShAmapi j~nAnAnAM prathamameva prAmANyamavadhAryeta | nachaitadasti | tena jAnImo.astIyaM prakriyeti |
uktamatharM buddhayArohAya saN^kShipyAha- nahIti ||
yasmAtsukhAdyeShu kashchitsaMshayaM na karoti yasmAchchAkhilAni vR^ittij~nAnAni darshana eva pramANatayA.akhilo jano na nishchinoti tasmAtsAkShiprAmANyaM parIkShAnapekSheNa sAkShiNaiva gR^ihyate | vR^ittij~nAnAnAM tu tatsApekSheNetyanubhavArUDhaM prameyaM kimarthamapalapyate | nirnimittamapalapituM na shakyata iti | 
"na parIkShA.anavasthA syAt.h' ityuktamupasaMharati- doShAbhAvAdikaM cheti ||
sAkShyeveti sambandhaH | svasya parIkShAyAshcha doShAbhAvaM prAmANyaM cha parIkShAnirapekShaH sAkShyeva samyak.h prapashyati | tasmAnna kA.apyanavastheti |
"aparIkShitameva' ityAdinoktamupasaMharati- taditi ||
tattasmAtparIkShitameva mAnam.h | tena cha bhagavati kvachidapi doSho nAstIti siddham.h | tadvirodhAdaparIkShitaM doShadarshanamapramANamevetyarthaH | 
evamaparIkShitaM doShadarshanaM parIkShitena nirdoShatAdarshanena bAdhitaM na bhagavato doShitvaM sAdhayituM shaktamityuktam.h | idAnIM tAdR^ishasyApi sAdhakatve.atiprasaN^gaM sUchayati- aparIkShiteti ||
shuktyAdInAM rajatatvAdAvapi vidyata eva | tatashcha tathA tadapi siddhayedavisheShAditi bhAvaH | 
tadevaM doShadarshanaM parIkShitapratyakShavirodhAdapramANamityabhihitam.h | niraniShyo niravadya ityAdyAgamavirodhAchcha | syAdetat.h | prAk.h tattvamasyAdyAgamasya pratyakShaviruddhatvAtpratItArthe na prAmANyamityuktam.h | tatkathaM tadviparItaM pratyakShasyAgamavirodhenAprAmANyamidAnImuchyata ityAshaN^kAM parihartumAha- taditi ||
yatra yadA.akShajamAgamasyopajIvyaM tat.h tadA pratyakShaviruddhArthe jAtyA prabalasyApyAgamasya mAnatA nAsti | tasmAdu(ktAdu)pajIvyopajIvakabhAvAdanyatra viparItopajIvyopajIvakabhAve bAdhyabAdhakabhAvasyApi viparyayaH | yadA.a.agamaH pratyakShasyopajIvyastadA.a.agamaviruddhArthe pratyakShasya na mAnatetyarthaH | 
tataH kimityata Aha- laukika iti ||
laukike pratyakShasiddhajIvAdiviShaye brahmAtmakatvAdibodhanarUpe vyavahAre tattvamasyAdyAgamena kriyamANe atra Agame AgamaM prati pratyakShasyopajIvyatA | avatArANAM vishvAdInAM cha doShadR^iShyau pratyakShAdikaM pratyAgamasyopajIvyatA syAt.h | etaduktaM bhavati | prAk.h pratyakShavirodhenAgamasyAprAmANyamabhidhAyedAnImAgamavirodhena pratyakShasyAprAmANyAbhidhAnaM na viruddham.h | nahi nirvisheShaNayoH pratyakShAgamayoH parasparaM bAdhyabAdhakabhAvo.abhihitaH | kintUpajIvakatvena bAdhyatvamupajIvyatvena bAdhakatvam.h | tachcha tatrAnyathA.atrAnyatheti kathaM virodha iti | anena doShaviShayapratyakShavirodhAdAgamasyaivAprAmANyaM kinna syAditi chodyaM garbhasrAveNaiva gatam.h | AgamasyojIvyatayA pratyakShataH prAbalyasyoktatvAt.h |
kathaM pratyakShaM pratyAgamasyopajIvyatvamityata Aha- Agameneti |
atra viShNau | vastutaH kalpanaivaiShA na pramitiritibhAvena kalpyata ityuktam.h | bhavedAgamasyopajIvyatvaM yadi viShNutvaM j~nAtavyaM bhavet.h | tadeva na j~nAtavyamityata Aha- na chediti ||
yadi viShNutvaM rAmakR^iShNAdau na j~nAtaM tadA doShagrAhiNA pratyakSheNa viShNoranyo doShavAniti gR^ihItaM syAt.h | natu viShNurdoShavAniti | nahi devadatte devadattatvAj~nAne devadatto.ayamAgata ityAkAraM j~nAnamutpattumarhatIti | tathA.api nAgamasyopajIvyatvam.h | yataH shrIvatsakaustubhAdilakShaNena viShNutvamanumAya viShNurdoShavAniti pratyakSheNa j~nAsyata ityata Aha- shAstreti ||
shrIvatsAdikaM lakShaNaM viShNutvena vyAptamityetachChAstreNaiva siddham.h | yadyapyasminpakShe sAkShAdAgamo nopajIvyaH | tathA.apyanumAnamUlavyAptigrahaNAya tadupajIvanamaparihAryameveti bhAvaH | nanu viShNutvAj~nAne viShNoranyo doShavAniti j~nAnena kuto bhAvyam.h | viShNutvavattadanyatvasyApyaj~nAtatvAditi chet.h | evaM tarhyaj~nAtaM prasajyata ityAha- kasyachiditi ||
itimAtre etAvatyeva viShaye | viShNurdoShavAniti j~nAnA(syA)nutpAdanaprasaN^ga eva tAtparyamiti bhAvaH | nanu yathA paTo.ayaM Chinno dagdho malina iti parAnupajIvinA pratyakSheNaiva gR^ihyate | tathA.a.agamAdikamanupajIvya pratyakSheNaiva viShNurdoShavAniti j~nAsyata ityata Aha- neti ||
svataH parAnupajIvanena | ayamabhisandhiH | paTatvamavayavasanniveshavyaN^ghayaM pratyakShameveti yujyate tathA j~nAnam.h | viShNutvaM tu samastaguNaparipUrNatvanirdoShatvajagajjanmAdikAraNatvalakShaNaM na pratyakSham.h | ato na tathAvidhaM j~nAnamupapadyate | yathA paJNchapalaparimito.ayaM paTo malina iti j~nAnamiti |
ayaM samudAyArthaH | rAmakR^iShNAdidoShagrAhiNA pratyakSheNa tredhotpattavyam.h | viShNurayaM doShavAniti vA viShNoranyo.ayaM doShavAniti vA kashchidayaM doShavAniti vA | prakArAntarAbhAvAt.h | tatra dvitIyatR^itIyayorna viShNordoShavattve tadudbhAvayituM (shakyate) shakyam.h | viShNurdoShavAniti tenAnavagAhanAt.h | vastuvR^ittyA.asau viShNureveti chet.h | kiM tataH | nahi vastuvR^ittisahitaM yatkiJNchijj~nAnaM vivakShitavishe(ShaNaM sA)ShaM sAdhayati | atiprasaN^gAt.h | Adye viShNutvaM sarvathA j~nAtavyam.h | nachaitatpratyakShavedyaM nApyanumeyamityuktaM shAstrayonisUtre | tasmAd.h "devakyAM devarUpiNyAM viShNuH sarvaguhAshayaH | AvirAsId.h' ityAgamena vA.a.agamAvagatavyAptikAnumAnena vA.avagantavyam.h | tataH sarvathA pratyakShasyAgamopajIvyatvamaN^gIkAryam.h | sarvo.apyAgamastAvadekameva vAkyam.h | sa cha sarvarUpopetasya viShNornirdoShatvaM pratipAdayatIti tadvirodhAdapramANameva doShaviShayaM pratyakShamiti |
itashcha tadapramANamiti darshayitumAha- kechiditi ||
pratyakShaM bhagavadrUpANAM doShitve pramANamiti vadanpraShyavyaH | kechittatkAlavartinaH puruShA bhagavadrUpeShu doShAnpashyantItyatrArthe.asmAkaM kiM pramANam.h | pratyakShamanumAnamAgamo veti | na tAvatpratyakSham.h | parapuruShavartini pratyakShe pareShAM pratyakShAyogAt.h | dUre kAlabhede | nApyanumAnaM liN^gAbhAvAt.h | Agamo.api vedaH purANAdirvA | nAdyaH | tasyAdarshanAt.h | tasmAd.hdvitIya evAN^gIkArya ityAha- paurANamiti ||
atra bhagavadrUpadoShagrAhipratyakShasadbhAve | vaktavyamiti sheShaH | 
tataH kimiti chet.h | tatpurANavAkyaM taddoShadarshanaM kiM pratyakShalakShaNaM pramANatayA manyate, utAparIkShitapramANApramANAbhAvapratItimAtratayA, athApramANatayA | 
Adye doShamAha- taditi ||
bhagavadrUpeShu doShagrAhiNIM pratItiM pramANatayA pratipAdayatpurANavAkyaM doShasadbhAvaM manyata eva | na hi sambhavati tad.hgrAhiNaH prAmANyamaN^gIkaroti nAN^gIkaroti cha taditi | doShasadbhAvaM manyamAnaM cha tatprAgudAhR^itayA shrutyaiva viruddhayata iti |
purANavAkyasya shrutiviruddhatve ko doSha ityata Aha- purANasyeti ||
pauruSheyeNa khalu vAkyena samUlena bhAvyam.h  | yataH kenachitkAraNena kaJNchidarthaM buddhisthIkR^itya vAkyaM prayuJNjmahe | anyathotpatterevAsambhavaH | 
purANavAkyasya cha veda eva mUlaM kuta ityata Aha- nacheti ||
aparaH pauruSheyo granthaH | chashabdaH pratyakShA(gamA)disamuchchayArthaH | pauruSheyastAvadAgamo na purANasya mUlam.h | tasyApi mUlA(ntarA)pekShAyAmandhaparamparApAtAt.h | na(cha) pratyakShAnumAne | tadarthasya tadagocharatvAt.h | nApyutprekShA | pratArakavAkyavadaprAmANyaprasaN^gAt.h | ataH parisheShAdveda eva purANasyopajIvya iti siddham.h |
tataH kimityata Aha- tadvirodha iti ||
upajIvyavedavirodhe | tat.h purANavAkyam.h | tatra bhagavataH sadoShatve | upajIvyaviruddhasyopajIvakasyAprAmANyAvashyambhAvAditi 
chArthaH | 
nanvIshvarapraNItAnAM purANAnAM tadIyaM nijaM j~nAnameva mUlaM na vedaH | anIshvarapraNItAnAmapi yogipratyakShameva | ato vedavirodhe.api ko doShaH | uchyate | vedastAvatpramANameveti niShyaN^kitam.h | nacha pramANayorvirodho.asti | vastuvikalpaprasaN^gAt.h | tato vedavirodhe nijaj~nAnAdimUlatvamevApanIyate | tathA.api veda eva purANasyopajIvya iti katham.h | amIshvarapraNItapurANAbhiprAyeNeti na doShaH | anIshvarA hi svayaMpratibhAte.apyarthe (samAshvA) AshvAsArthaM vedamupajIvanti | yathoktam.h "yatsvayaMpratibhAtasya saMshayArtaM gurorvachaH' iti | yadveshvarapraNItapurANAnAmapi prAmANyAvadhAraNAya vedasaMvAdo.apekShitaH | anyathotprekShAmUlatvashaN^kanAt.h | tadabhiprAyeNa "purANasyopajIvyashcha veda eva' ityuktam.h |
dvitIyaM nirAkaroti- aparIkShiteti ||
akShajaM kathameva bhavediti pratyakShaM pramANatayA.abhilaShitArthe nodbhAvayituM shakyate | nahi pramANatvenAnavadhAritaM pramANatvenodbhAvayanparIkShakaH syAditi bhAvaH | vipakShe bAdhakamAha- yadyevamiti ||
pramANatvenAparIkShitamapi yadi pratyakShatayodbhAvyata ityarthaH | devadattAdibhrama iti | yaj~nadattashuktyAdau devadattarajatAdibhrama ityarthaH | bAdhitatvAttannAkShajaM pramANamiti chet.h | tatkiM bAdhAbhAvamAtraM vastuvyavasthAhetuH | tathAtve nishchAyakapramANavaiyarthyApatteH | asti cha prakR^ite vedabAdha iti |
upajIvyavedavirodhAdupajIvakayoH pratyakShapurANavAkyayoraprAmANyamityuktam.h | tadasat.h | upajIvakamupajIvyavirodhena bAdhyata iti niyamAbhAvAt.h | dR^ishyate hyupajIvyasyApIdaM rajatamiti j~nAnasyopajIvakena nedaM rajatamiti j~nAnena bAdha iti chet.h | kathamatropajIvyopajIvakabhAva iti vaktavyam.h H aprAptasya pratiShedhAyogAtprAptirUpamidaM rajatamiti j~nAnamAdyamupajIvyaM, pratiShedhAtmakaM tu nedaM rajatamiti j~nAnamupajIvakamiti vA, asiddhe dharmiNi pratiShedhAsambhavAddharmij~nAnamAdyamupajIvyaM dvitIyaM tUpajIvakamiti vA | Adye samAdhimAha- yAvachChaktIti || 
parIkShAyAM satyAM pramANatayA pratItasyeti sheShaH | bAdhane upajIvakena kuta iti sheShaH | doSho.asmadabhimata(to)niyamabhaN^gaH syAt.h | upajIvye.ashodhite parIkShayA.apramANAdavivikte upajIvakena bAdhite na doShaH | upajIvyatvamastvalamiti | prakR^itodAharaNe prathamapupajIvyopajIvakabhAvamabhyupaiti | upajIvyatvamityupalakShaNam.h | upajIvakatvaM chetyapi draShyavyam.h | pUrvottaraj~nAnayoriti sheShaH | alaMshabdo.avadhAraNe | 
idamuktaM bhavati | (astveva) astyevedaM rajataM nedaM rajatamiti j~nAnayorupajIvyopajIvakabhAva upajIvyasyopajIvakena bAdhashcha | tathA.apyupajIvyavirodhenopajIvakaM bAdhyata iti niyamabhaN^go nAsti | ayaM khalvasya niyamasyArthaH | parIkShayA shodhitamupajIvyaM virodhyupajIvakaM bAdhate svayaM tena na bAdhyata iti | natu yathAshrutaH | asya tu tadA bhaN^gaH syAt.h | yadi parIkShitamupajIvyaM virodhinopajIvakena bAdhyaM (bAdhitaM) kvachidupalabhemahi | nachaivam.h | idaM rajatamiti j~nAnaM tu na shodhitam.h | tatastasminnupajIvakena bAdhite na niyamabhaN^gaH | nahi nirvisheShaNasya vyabhichAre vishiShyaM vyabhicharatyatiprasaN^gAt.h | nacha vAchyaM vishiShyasya prayojakatAkalpanaM nirmUlamiti | ubhayathA(pi) bAdhyabAdhakabhAvadarshanAt.h | visheShaNAnapekShAyAmavyavasthApAtAt.h | nanu parIkShAyAmaN^gIkR^itAyAM tayaivAlam.h | parIkShitenAparIkShitaM bAdhyata ityetAvataH kvachidvayabhichArAbhAvAtkimupajIvyopajIvakabhAvena | uchyate | bhavedevaM yadyAtyantikIM parIkShAmatrAN^gIkurmaH | nachaivam.h | kintu yAvachChaktiparIkShAmeva | nacha tAvanmAtrasya bAdhakatvaniyamo.asti | yAvachChaktiparIkShitasyApi bAdhadarshanAt.h | ato yuktaM vishiShyasyopAdAnam.h | AtyantikaparIkShaiva bAdhakatvopayoginI bhavatu kimupajIvyatvenetyapi na vAchyam.h | tasyApi sAMvyAvahArikatvAt.h | yathoktam.h | "sannipAtalakShaNo vidhiranimittaM tadvighAtasya' iti | prakR^ite tu vedaH parIkShita upajIvyashcheti |
dvitIye parihAramAha- bhrame.apIti ||
hIti vakShyamANamatrApi sambaddhayate | yadyapyekamevedaM rajatamiti j~nAnaM tathA.api viShayopAdhivashAd.h vibhAgam.h | tatra prakAre bhramatve.api svarUpe.abhramatvameva | tatra kadA.api bAdhAbhAvAt.h | tathA.anyepyAhuH | sarvaM j~nAnaM dharmiNi pramANaM prakAre tu viparyaya iti | bhAgAbhyupagamAdeva na virodhachodanAvakAshaH | tataH kimityata Aha- tanmAtramiti ||
abhramabhAgamAtram.h | tenaiva dharmiNaH siddheH | rajatAkArasya niShedhyatvena dharmitvAbhAvAditi hishabdArthaH | etaduktaM bhavati | asminpakShe yadupajIvyaM na tadupajIvakena bAdhyate yachcha bAdhyate na tadupajIvyamityato nedamasmadIyaniyamabhaN^gasyodAharaNamiti |
atrAntare mAyAvAdinashchodayanti | yaduktamupajIvyavirodhAdadvaitashrutInAmaprAmANyamiti | tadasat.h | tatrApyasya samAdhAnasya suvachatvAt.h | tathAhi | yaH sarvaj~na ityAdInAM tattvamasyAdInAM cha kathamupajIvyopajIvakabhAva iti vaktavyam.h | siddhaM na nivartakatvAdityAdivachanAt.h | tattvamasyAdivAkayamaikyavirodhinAM sAvarj~nAdInAM duHkhAdInAM cha pratiShedhakamaN^gIkR^itam.h | nacha prAptiM vinA pratiShedho.astIti prAptirUpaM yaH sarvaj~na ityAdikamupajIvyam.h, tattvamasyAdikaM tUpajIvakamiti vA, asiddhe dhamirNi pratiShedhAnupapatterdharmipratipAdakamAdyamupajIvyamupajIvakaM chottaramiti vA | Adye rajataj~nAnasyevAparIkShitatvAdupajIvyasyApi prathamasyottareNa bAdhe na kA.apyanupapattiH | dvitIye shuktisvarUpamAtramiva brahmasvarUpamAtramupajIvyaM na sArvaj~nAdivishiShyam.h | tathAcha yadupajIvyaM na taduttareNa bAdhyate | yadbAdhyate sArvaj~nAdikaM na tadupajIvyamiti na kashchidvirodha iti |
atra parihAradvayamapi pratiShedhati- nachaivamiti ||
prasiddhayorbhrAntibAdhayorivAtra samAdhAnaM na vaktuM shakyate | vaiShamyAditi bhAvaH | 
tatkathamityataH prathamapakShe tAvadvaiShamyaM darshayati- suparIkShita iti ||
prathamapramANe suparIkShite sati na chaivamiti sambandhaH | etaduktaM bhavati | idaM rajatamiti j~nAnamupajIvyamapyaparIkShitatvAdupajIvakena nedaM rajatamati j~nAnena bAdhyate | upajIvyopajIvakanyAyasya yAvachChaktiparIkShAviShayatvAti hyasmAbhirabhihitam.h | asmannyAyena cha pareNa pratyavasthAyate | nacha tadyuktam.h | yaH sarvaj~na ityAdInAmahaM duHkhItyAdInAM cha suparIkShitatvAt.h | upapAditaM khalu yaH sarvaj~na ityAdishrutInAM tattvAvedakatvaM sAkShiNashcha niyamenAvyabhichAritvamiti | 
dvitIyapakShe vaiShamyaM darshayati- sarvamiti ||
yataH kAraNAttatsarvaM sArvaj~nAdikamupajIvyaiva tattvamasItyAdikaM pramANaM pravartate.ato na chaivamiti sambandhaH | idamuktaM bhavati | yathA nedaM rajatamiti j~nAnaM purovartinaH svarUpamAtraM dharmIkR^itya pravartate na tu rajatatvavishiShyaM na tathA tattvamasyAdivAkyaM pravartitumarhati | kintu sarvaj~natvAdivishiShyaM brahmasvarUpaM duHkhAdivishiShyaM jIvasvarUpaM cha dhamarIkR^ityaiva | tathAcha dharmigrAhakavirodho.aparihArya iti | atra sarvamiti sarvaj~natvAdyanyatamasyopalakShaNam.h | 
nanu tattvamasyAdivAkyamapi yadi svarUpamAtramupajIvya pravarteta tadA kIdR^isho doSha ityata Aha- kathamiti ||
vAkyadvayametat.h | tatraikasyArthaH | dharmAnvihAya svarUpasyaivopajIvyatvaM chettarhi tatkathaM j~neyaM yattattvamasIti bodhyate | etaduktaM bhavati | shabdenAnUdya hi svarUpaM tattvamasIti vaktavyam.h | nacha nirdharmasya pratipAdakaH shabdo.asti | ataH svarUpamAtrasya buddhAvanArohAdbodhanamevAnupapannamiti | na brUmaH svarUpamAtrasyopajIvyatvam.h | kintu bhedakAnsarvaj~natvAdidharmAnvihAya tattvAdinA vishiShyasya | tathAcha na kashchiddoSha ityataH shiShyaM vAkyam.h | yadi tattvAdidharmopetasyopajIvyatvaM tarhi sarvaj~natvAdikaM vihAya yasmAtkasmAchchittattvAdestadbrahmeti kathaM j~neyam.h | yadyapyasminpakShe noktadoShastathA.api bodhyasya brahmAsmIti j~nAnamanupapannameva | sarvaj~natvAderbrahmalakShaNatvena tadanupAdAne brahmaNo buddhAvanArohAt.h | tattvAderghaTAdisAdhAraNatvAditi bhAvaH | sarvaj~natvAdiparityAgenopajIvane bAdhakamabhidhAya viparyaye paryavasAnamAha- etasmAditi ||
aparathA j~nAnAsambhavAt.h | yAvatA dharmeNa | tAvatopetasyaiva | 
nanu nedaM rajatamiti j~nAnaM yathA svarUpamAtramupajIvya pravR^ittam.h | tathedamapi pravartsyati ko doSha ityata Aha- svarUpasyaiveti ||
upajIvyatvamiti vartate | uktAnupapattereva dR^iShyAnto.api na samasta ityarthaH | 
nanu yatsarvaj~naM tattvamasIti na bodhanIyam.h | kintu tattvamasItyeva | na choktadoShaH | tachChabdo brahma vadati | yogyAnvitAbhidhAyinashchashabdAH | lakShaNaM cha brahmaNA.anvetuM yogyam.h | tatashcha tachChabdenaiva vyAvR^ittasya pratIterityAshayavAnAshaN^kate- sarveti ||
chashabdo.avadhAraNe | bhaNyate tachChabdena iti yadi bhaNyate ityAvR^ittyA yojyam.h | sampratipattimuttaramAha- astviti ||
yatpareNoktaM tadastvityarthaH | prativAdyuktArthAN^gIkAre pratij~nAhAniH kathaM na bhavedityata Aha- na iti ||
anabhimataprameyAN^gIkAre hi pratij~nAhAniH syAt.h | anena chAN^gIkR^itena no.asmAkaM (na pratij~nAhA)naiva hAniH syAt.h | parasya dharmigrAhivirodho hyasmAbhiruchyate | tatparihArAya pareNa chedamuditam.h | nachAnena tatparihAram.h | pratyuta dR^iDhIkR^itamiti bhAvaH | 
kiM prakR^itaprameyAvirodhitvamAtreNedamaN^gIkriyate uta tathAbhUtatveneti jij~nAsAyAmAha- svapakShashcheti ||
aJNjaseti nAbhyupagamamAtreNetyarthaH | tadupapAdayati- yasmAditi ||
sarvasho.apIti sambandhaH | ityetatsUtrasAmarthyena prAgupapAditamiti sheShaH |
kiJNchAsminnapi pakShe brahmaNo buddhAvanArohastadavastha eva | yatastadAdishabdAH sAmAnyata eva yogyAnvitaM bruvate | sarvaj~nAdishabdA eva visheShataH | tathA.anubhavAt.h | nacha sAmAnyato.anvitAbhidhAyinA vyAvR^ittapratItirityAshayavAnAha- visheSheti ||
akhilaM yogyAnvitaM svarUpaM visheShasAmAnyatayA shabdabodhyaM bhavet.h | 
anvitAbhidhAnamAtramaN^gIkriyata eva | tachchaikasya padasya sAmAnyata eva na visheShata iti na buddhau brahmArohaH | yadi cha visheShastadA dharmigrAhivirodhastadavastha eveti samudAyArthaH | kechinmAyAvAdino.anvitAbhidhAnamaN^gIkurvate vij~nAnaghanAdaya sati nAprAptashaN^keyam.h | 
vyAvartakadharmairvyAvR^ittasyaivopajIvyatvamiti yaduktaM tannAsti | bAdhakaj~nAneShu tadabhAvAt.h | nacha tatrApi vyAvR^ittasyaivopajIvyatvaM na svarUpamAtrasyetyuktamiti vAchyam.h | pUrvasminbhramaj~nAne vyAvR^ittatva(sya)syaivAsiddhatvAt.h | siddhau cha bhramatvAnupapatteH | "tanmAtramupajIvya hi' ityuktavirodhAchchetyata Aha- purovartitveti ||
devadattAdau yashchaitrAdibhramastatra purovartitvapUrvANi visheShaNAni devadattAdisvarUpaM devadattAderaviditatvAchchaitramAtrAdvinaivApurovartyAdibhyo vyAvartayanti yasmAttasmAdbAdhakaj~nAnaM vyAvR^ittamevopajIvatIti niyamo nAnupapannaH | nApi bhramAnupapattiH | AropyavyAvR^itteranaN^gIkaraNAt.h | tanmAtrashabdena chAropyamAtravyAvartanAnnoktavirodho.apIti bhAvaH | 
nanvanena nAtyantavyAvR^ittiru(pajIvyatvo)payoginI | kintu vyAvR^ittimAtramityuktaM bhavati | tatprakR^ite.apyasti | tattvAdinA brahmaNo.api vyAvR^ittatvenopajIvyatvasambhavAditi chenna | tAvanmAtreNa bodhyasyApi brahmAsmIti j~nAnAnupapatteruktatvAt.h |
doShAntaraM chAha- brahmaNa iti ||
brahmaNaH punariti sambandhaH | kiM kartR^i, brahma vyAvartayati, na kimapi | 
tattvAdInAmaN^gIkAre.api doShamAha- yasmAditi ||
tattvAdi visheShaNena yasmAtkasmAdapyarthAttattvAdirahitam.h | tAvadvayAvR^ittaM chedupajIvyatvamastIti bodhyate | tadedaM vAkyaM siddhasAdhanaM j~nAtasyaiva j~nApakaM syAt.h | bodhyenAsyArthasya prAgeva viditatvAt.h | tathA chAshAstraM syAt.h | 
mA bhUttattvAdinA vyAvR^ittaM brahmopajIvyam.h | vij~nAnamAnandaM brahmetyAdishrutyA brahmalakShaNatvenoktena chinmAtratvAdinA tu bhaviShyatItyata Aha- chinmAtratvaM cheti ||
mAtrashabdena chitaH sarvaviShayatvAdikaM vyAvartayati | AnandatvAderapyupalakShaNametat.h | brahmaNa iti sheShaH | chinmAtratvAdikaM na brahmaNo bhinnam.h ato nirvisheShatvAvirodhAttadaN^gIkriyata ityata Aha- tAvanmAtramiti ||
tattarhi tasyApi shrutatvAdabhinnatvAchcheti bhAvaH | abhede kathaM lakShaNatvamiti chet.h | samaM vij~nAnAdAvapi | uktashcha lakShyalakShaNaprakAro lakShaNasUtra iti |
shrutatvasAmye.api chinmAtratvAdikameva dharmiNi niveshyate | aviruddhatvAt.h | na sarvaj~natvAdikaM viruddhatvAt.h | yathA nedaM rajatamiti j~nAne.aviruddhapurovartitvAdyupetasya dharmitvaM na viruddharajatatvAdyupetasyetyata Aha- chinmAtreti ||

svasya bodhyasya yadyasmAnmataM sammatam.h |
etaduktaM bhavati | virodhabhayAtsarvaj~natvAdivishiShyaM na dharmIkriyate iti vadatA chidAnandarUpamapi na dharmIkartavyam.h | j~nAtaj~nApanaprasaN^gAt.h | virodha iva j~nAtaj~nApanasyApyashAstratAhetutve visheShAbhAvAt.h | chinmAtraM tvadatiriktaM nAstIti vAkyArtha iti chenna | apratibhAsanAt.h | gatyantarAbhAvAditthaM kalpyata iti chet.h(nna) | sUtrakR^itaivArthAntarasyoktatvAt.h | 
na virodhabhayAdvayaM sArvaj~nAdikaM dharmiNi na niveshayAmaH | kintu sarvaj~natvAdikaM (hi) na brahmaNo bhinnam.h | neha nAnetyAdishrutivirodhAt.h | nApi svarUpam.h | tasya viyadAdisarvasApekShatvAt.h | sarvasya cha mithyAtvAt.h | nahi tathAbhUtasya 
satyasvarUpatA sambhavati | chidAnandAdestu brahmasvarUpatve na kvApyanupapattirityAshayavAnAshaN^kate- sarveti ||
sarvaj~natvaM vartata iti sheShaH | itishabdo hetau | evashabdasya tadevetyanena sambandhaH | nahi mithyetyarthaH | pariharati- chetanatvaM cheti ||
yatparasApekShaM tanna sadityaN^gIkAre brahmaNashchetanatvaM cha na syAdityarthaH | kuta ityato (lyuT.h pratya)yupratyayasyAnekArthatvAtkatarR^ivAchitAM tAvadupAdAya vyAchaShye- j~natvamiti ||
chetanatvaM nAma tAvajj~natvamityarthaH | tataH kimityata Aha- neti ||
j~natvamiti vartate | kintu j~neyasApekShameva | j~nAnakriyAM prati kartR^itvaM khalu j~natvam.h | sakarmakakriyAvachanashcha jAnAtiH | ataH karmApekShakriyAkartR^itvamapi sApekShameva | 
tathA.api kutashchetanatvaM na syAditi chet.h | j~nasya brahmaNo j~neyaM svayameva vA syAtparaM vA | nAdya ityAha- sveti ||
chastvarthaH | asau mAyAvAdI | kuto na manyata ityata Aha- savisheShata iti || savisheShatvaprasaN^gAt.h | pratyak.h parAgbhAvalakShaNo hi kartR^ikarmabhAvo naikatraikasya yujyate | yadi cha syAttadA bhedapratinidhinA visheSheNa ghaTanIyaH | ato brahmaNo j~natvaj~neyatvayoraN^gIkAre visheSho.aN^gIkartavyaH syAt.h | nivirsheShaM cha brahmAN^gIkR^itamiti svaj~neyatvaM na manyate | tatashcha parameva j~neyaM vaktavyam.h | tachcha mithyAbhUtamiti kathaM tadapekShaM chetanatvaM satsyAditi | evaM j~natvasya j~nAnasApekShatvamapi vaktavyam.h |
kiJNchaivaM vadatA svarUpamAtramupajIvyamityapi vaktuM na shakyate | tasyApi svashabdena parApekShatApratIterityAha- svashabdo.apIti ||

parasmAt.h | hishabdo hetau | arthaH pravR^ittinimittam.h | iti proktaH shabdashaktij~naiH | svaM cha tadrUpaM cheti hi svarUpam.h | rUpashabdashcha svaparasAdhAraNaH | tena svasminprApte.apyuchyamAnaH svashabdaH parisaN^khayAnyAyena paravyAvR^ittimeva pratipAdayatIti j~nAyate | Joshi-31
tyametadevaM vyAkhyAne | nachaivamityata Aha- svarUpamiti ||
asmadabhipretaM vyAkhyAnaM na chedaN^gIkriyate tadA svarUpaM nAma kiM, na kimapi | svarUpashabdo nirarthakaH syAdityarthaH | rUpashabdasamAnArthaH svarUpashabda ityataH kathametaditi chedatra vaktavyam.h | svaM cha tadrUpaM cheti vyutpattimaN^gIkR^ityaivamuchyate | utAkhaNDa evAyaM shabda ityupetya | Adye doShamAha- vaiyathyarmiti || yasmAdasminpakShe svashabdasya vaiyarthyaM tasmAtsvarUpaM nAma kimita sambandhaH | kuto vaiyarthyamityata Aha- rUpeti || svarUpashabde yo rUpashabdastenaiva rUpashabdArthAbhidhAnasya pUrNatvAt.h | nahi rUpashabdo rUpashabdArthaM nAbhidhava iti sambhavati | anyathotpalanIlotpalashabdAvapyekArthau syAtAm.h | dvitIyaM nirAkaroti- tachcheti || tat.h rUpapadam.h | cho yasmAdityarthe | sAmAnyatAvachaH sAmAnyAkArasya vAchakam.h | chAturvaNyarAditvAtsvArthe ShyaJN.hpratyayaH | etaduktaM bhavati | pratItipramANaka eva shabdArthanishchaya iti hi shAbdAH | tatra rUpashabdaH sAmAnyAkArasyAbhidhAyakaH | sarveShAM tatastatpratyayAt.h | svarUpashabdashchAsAdhAraNAkArasya | tasmAttatpratIteH | tasmAnna tayorekArthatvamiti |
yaduktaM chetanatvaM brahmaNo na syAditi tadiShyApAdanam.h | na hi vayaM brahmaNashchetanatvamaN^gIkurmaH | kriyAveshalakShaNasya kartR^itvasya nirvikalpake.abhAvAt.h | kintu chaitanyameva brahma | tadarthA eva chetanatvavAdA vyAkhyAtavyA ityatashchaitanyamapi na pareNa shakyAN^gIkAramiti bhAvena tadvayAkhyAti- chetanasyeti ||

tataH kimityata Aha- tasmAditi ||
yasmAchchaitanyaM nAma j~nAnaM tasmAchchaitanyasya brahmaNo, visheShato.atishayena, visheShabAhulyaM prasajyate | j~nAnaM hi j~neyaj~nAtR^ikaraNasApekShaM bhavati | j~nAnatvAdidharmAshchAnivAryAH | nacha savisheShaM brahma pareNAN^gIkriyate | j~neyAdikaM cha na svayam.h | virodhAt.h | parantu mithyeti tatsApekShaM j~nAnaM kathaM satsyAt.h | brahmaNo j~nAnatve j~neyAdyupetatA kuta iti chet.h | j~nAnatvAt.h | prasiddhaj~nAnavat.h | nacha j~nAnatvamasiddhamiti yuktam.h | aN^gIkAravirodhAt.h | vyAptimupapAdayati- neti ||
yaduktaM prAgbrahmaNashchetanatve j~neyaj~nAnopetatvena bhAvyamiti, tatrApi j~natvAtsammatavaditi niyAmakamabhipretam.h | prasaN^gAttasyApi vyAptimupapAdayati- j~neyeti ||
Adyashchashabdo j~neyAdirAhityaj~natvayoH samuchchaye | dvitIyastu vyabhichAradvayasamuchchaye | 
nanu prasiddhasya j~nAnasya j~neyAdyupetatve.apIdaM brahmasvarUpaM j~nAnaM tadrahitaM bhavatu kiM bAdhakamityata Aha- j~nAtR^ij~neyeti ||
hInameveti sambandhaH | kartR^i tADyata iti tADayitR^itADyAbhyAM hInaM syAdityarthaH | dhAtvartho.api j~nAnaM yadi kartR^irahitaM syAt.h | AkAN^kShAvashAtsakarmakatayA pratIyamAnamapi cha yadi niShkarmakaM syAttadokto bahutaro.atiprasaN^gaH, visheShAbhAvAditi | j~naviShaye.apyevaM bhojyabhojanavihIno bhoktA.api syAdityAdiratiprasaN^go vAchyaH | nahi sakarmakakriyAyAH kartA kriyAdirahito yukta iti |
j~nAtA j~neyamiti cha kArakAbhidhAnametat.h | kArakamutpAdakamiti cha paryAyAvetau | kAryameva chotpAdakamapekShate | akAryaM cha brahmAkhyaM j~nAnamiti na tasya kartrAdyapekShetyAshayavAn.h shaN^kate- nityatvAditi ||
nityatvamakAryatvasyopalakShaNam.h | anityasya bhojanAdebharoktrAdyapekShAyAmapIdaM nityatvAttAdR^ishaM j~nAtrAdirahitaM cha syAdityanena vyApakaviruddhopalabdhyA vyApyaviparyayaH shaN^kitaH | notpAdakameva kArakam.h | tathA satyasti gaganamityAdau gaganAdInAmakArakatvaprasaN^gAt.h | kintu dhAtvarthAshrayaH kartA, tadviShayaH karmetyAdi |
AkAN^kShA.anAkAN^kShe eva cha tadanvitatvAnanvitatvayoH prayojake | natu kAryatvAkAryatve | ata eva kashchiddhAtvarthaH karmAdyanvitaH kashchinneti yujyata ityAshayavAnAkAN^kShAmaprayojakIkR^itya kAryatvAdyeva prayojakIkurvANasyAtiprasaN^gamAha- nityeti ||

sA tAdR^ishI naiva hIti sambandhaH | dvitIyaprasaN^gasya viparyayaparyavasAnaM chashabdenAha | kathaM na sA tAdR^ishItyata Aha- draShyAra iti ||
vaktAra iti vaktavye draShyAra ityuktamapauruSheyatvAvighAtArtham.h | aJNjaseti vAchyasadbhAve na kAchidanupapattirityuktam.h |

nanu vAN^.h na dhAtvarthaH | api tu dhAtvatharM prati karma | tatkathamatrodAharaNam.h | uchyate | AkAN^kShAnimittaM pratisambandhyanvitatvaM nityatvena na hIyata ityetAvanmAtre(Na) vAgudAharaNasya gR^ihItatvAnna doShaH | vAgityukte hi kiMvaktR^ikA kiMvAchyetyAkAN^kShA bhavatyeva |

sarvavilopaH sarvasya mithyAtvam.h | na tAvatpratyakSheNa, tasya satyatAgrAhitvAt.h | nApyanumAnena, pratyakShabAdhitasya tasya prAmANyAbhAvAt.h | nachAgamena | prapaJNchamithyAtvaM pratipAdayataH tasyAbhAvAdityAkShepArthaH |

vihInasya viruddhasya | arthastAtparyam.h | etaduktaM bhavati | na brUmo vayaM nAstIdaM vAkyamiti | nApyeShAM padAnAmatra shaktirnAstIti | kintvasya vAkyasya prapaJNchamithyAtve tAtparyaM nAstIti | upapattivirodhAbhAvo hi pratItArthe tAtparyasya j~nApakaH | atra chAstyupapattivirodha iti j~nApanAya vikalpya dUShaNAbhidhAnaM kR^itamiti |
syAdetat.h | upakramopasaMhArAbhyAsApUrvatAphalArthavAdopapattayaH shrutiliN^gavAkyaprakaraNasthAnasamAkhyAshcha tAtparyaliN^gAni | tatropapattivirodhe.apyanyairliN^gairasya vAkyasya prapaJNchamithyAtve tAtparyamavagamyatAmityata Aha- upakramAdIti ||
upakramAdiliN^gAnAM madhye yadyaduttaraM tattadbalIya ityupapattireva balIyasI | shrutyAdau liN^gasamUhe cha yadyatpUrvaM tattadbalIya iti | tatrApi liN^gashabdoditopapattireva balavatI | tato balavadvirodhe satAmanyeShAM liN^gAnAM na tAtparyanishchAyakatvaM yuktam.h | kuta etadityata Aha- brahmatarketi ||

sadgaganamityAdi pratyakSham.h | tachcha sAkShirUpatvAdbalavat.h | upapattishchArthakriyAkAritvAdikA | sA cha vyAptyAdimattvAdbalavatI | AgamAshcha vishvaM satyamityAdyAH | teShA prAbalyavyutpAdanAya bahava ityuktam.h | niravakAshatvAdyupalakShaNametat.h | yadA yasminnarthe.aN^gIkR^ite | yatra yadarthapratipAdane.arthaH prayojanaM cha nAsti | brahmaNo.advitIyatAsiddhiH prayojanamiti chenna | tasyA evAprAmANikatvAt.h | Atmano muktisiddhiriti chenna | vinAshenApi tatsiddheH | bahujIvavAdinAmivAdarshanenApyupapatteH | vairAgyArthamiti chenna | duHkhasAdhanatAj~nApanena tatsiddheH | arthagrahaNamupalakShaNam.h | upakramAdInAmapyAnukUlyaM nAstIti cha draShyavyam.h | na kevalaM liN^gAnukUlyAbhAvaH | kinnAma yatra liN^gavirodhitA cha | etad.hdvayaM granthAntare tatra tatroktaM j~nAtavyam.h |
tarhi niravakAshaM vAkyamapramANaM prasajyata ityata Aha- upapanna iti ||
pratyakShAdipramANopakramAdiliN^gAvirodhini tadAnukUlyopapanne cha bhagavati svagatabhedAbhAve.arthe vAkyasya sati sa evArthaH kathaM grAhyaH | neha nAneti vAkyasyApavyAkhyAne nirAkR^ite labdhamAha- mukhyArtha iti ||

aN^gIkAryam.h dharmitayeti sheShaH | tathA chopajIvyavirodhastattvamasyAdivAkyasya durvAra iti herarthaH |

mithyAtvAbhidhAnam.h | apishabdaH pUrvavAkyArthasamuchchaye | sarvashabdena prakR^itaM guNajAtamuchyate | kathaJNchaneti pramANAbhAvAt.h shrutyAdipramANaviruddhatvAchcha | aprAptatvenAnuvAdatvAbhAvasya choktatvAdityarthaH |
nanu cha tattvamasyAdivAkyameva jIvabrahmaNorekatAM pratipAdayatsArvaj~nAdiguNajAtasya mithyAtvaM gamayati | nahi tasya satyatve jIvabrahmaikatvamupapadyate | tatkathaM guNAnAM mithyAtve pramANAbhAva iti chenna | siddhe tattvamasyAdivAkyasya jIvabrahmaikatvaniShThatve guNAnAM mithyAtvasiddhiH | tatsiddhau cha tatsiddhiriti parasparAshrayatAdoShAt.h | doShAntaraM chAha- anAdIti ||
yasmAjjIvAnAmanAdiyogyatoktA pramANairupapAditA | tena kAraNena sA grAhyaiva sarvathA | etaduktaM bhavati | yadA devamAnavadAnavarUpA tadavAntarabhedarUpA cha jIvAnAM yogyatA.anAdinityA pramitA tadA kA vArtA jIvabrahmaNorekatvasya | tathA 
cha kathaM tatsiddhaye guNAnAM mithyAtvakalpanamiti |
atraiva hetvantaramAha- muktAnAmiti ||

muktAnAM tAratamye pramANAntaramAha- j~nAnino.apIti ||
