viparyayaparyavasAnamAha- kR^ichChreNeti ||
tapo j~nAnaM karmApItyanena shubhamityuktaM bhavati | j~nAnamiti shravaNAdikamuchyate | karmeti yaj~nAdi ete j~nAninaH kR^ichChreNApItyAdivisheShaNAnAM phalamanupadameva j~nAsyate | sakAmAshcha shubhe sadetyekasya tapaAdeshcharaNakAle tapaAdyantaraM kAmayanta ityarthaH | tasmAjj~nAnottarakAlAnuShThitena vichitreNa shubhena vichitrAmAnandabuddhiM prApnuvantIti sheShaH | 
bhavedetadyadi j~nAnottarakAlakR^itAnAM shubhAnAM phalavattvaM syAt.h | na chaivam.h | teShAM karmasvanadhikArAt.h | anadhikAriNA cha kR^itaM viphalamiti prasiddhameva | anuShThAnaM tvanyathA.apyupapadyate | te hi prAgj~nAnodayAdAdaranairantaryAbhyAM shubhAnyanuShThitavantastatsvAbhAvyamApannA j~nAnodayAnantaramapyanutiShThantItyAN^kaya pariharati- nacheti ||
ayaM j~nAninAM shubhAcharaNarUpaH | akaraNe pratyavAyo bhaviShyatItyevaM bhayapUrvapravR^ittitaH kR^ichChreNaivAcharaNAchcha, shubhasyaiveti prekShApUrvamashubhaparityAgenetyarthaH |
etena kR^ichChreNApItyAdivisheShaNaphalamuktaM bhavati | nahi svabhAvakR^itA pravR^ittirevaM bhavitumarhati |
nanvete prAganuShThAnakAle bhayapUrvaM kR^ichChreNAshubhaparityAgenaivAnuShThitavantaH | ataH tatsvabhAvA eva saMvR^ittAra idAnImapi tatsvAbhAvyena tathaiva kurvantItyaN^gIkAre ko doSha ityAshaN^kayAha- tAdR^isho.apIti ||
bhayapUrvapravR^ittyAdirUpo.api |
j~nAninastAvadanuShThAne.aj~nebhyo na vishiShyante | tatra j~nAninAM shubhapravR^ittiH pUrvatarapUrvatamasvabhAvabalAyAtaiva natu phalavatItyaN^gIkurvANaM prati yadi kashchid.h brUyAt.h aj~nAninAmapi shubhA pravR^ittiH pUrvatarapUrvamasvabhAvagataiva na tu phalavatI visheShAbhAvAditi, tadA kiM vAchyamiti | pratibandIM mochayitumAshaN^kate- phalavattva iti ||
aj~nAninAM karmaNo.astIti sheShaH | sAmye hi pratibandIgrahaH | nacha tadatrAsti | yato.aj~nAnikR^itakarmaNAM saphalatve "karmajaM buddhiyuktA hi' ityAdikaM pramANamasti | upalakShaNaM chaitat.h | adhikAriNashchaite vidhigocharAshchetyapi draShyavyam.h | nahyevaM sati svabhAvakalpanA.avakAsho.astIti | evaM tarhi j~nAniShvapi na svabhAvakalpanA yuktetyAshayavAnAha- tatreti ||
tatra karmaNaH phalavattve | tat.h pramANam.h | atrApyadhikArAdikamupalakShaNIyam.h |
kiM tatpramANamityatastaddarshayati- niShkAmamiti |
iha pravR^ittanivR^ittayormadhye | abhyeti atishayenaiti | AnandodrekasAhityena mukto bhavatItyarthaH | etatsmR^itivAkyArthavivaraNAya vAkyAntaraM paThati- shubheneti ||
hyAsashchAnandasya | shubhameva kartavyamashubhaM tyAjyaM cha | anena vidhisadbhAvo.api siddhaH | tato.adhikArashcha | atra shrutimapyAha- upAsta iti ||
anena "sa ya AtmAnameva lokamupAste na hyasya karma kShIyate.asmAddhayevAtmano yadyatkAmayate tattatsR^ijate' iti shrutimupAdatte | AtmAnaM paramAtmAnam.h | lokaM sarvAshrayam.h | upAste kAraNena kAryopalakShaNaM pashyatItyarthaH | sa vidvAnmukto bhUtvA yadyatkAmayate tattatkarmAsmAddhayevAtmano.asyAtmanaH prasAdena sR^ijate | 
avidvAnityanena "yadyapyanevaMvinmahatpuNyaM karma karoti taddhAsyAntataH kShIyata eva' iti shrutimupAdatte | anayA 
chArthAjj~nAnikarmaNaH sAphalyaM siddhayati | upari chopayogo bhaviShyati |
yadevetyanena "yadeva vidyayA karoti shraddhayopaniShadA tadeva vIryavattaraM bhavati' iti shrutimupAdatte | vidyayA brahmasAkShAtkArapUrvakamupaniShadA svayogya(m.h)yA vIryavattaramadhikaphalamityAdivAkyasAmarthyAjj~nAnikR^itakarmaNAM phalavattvaM tAvatpratIyate | tatasteShAM vaichityAdvimuktigaM tAratamyaM cha siddhamityarthaH | 
syAdetat.h | naitAni vAkyAni j~nAnikarmaNAM sAphalyaM pratipAdayanti | sa ya AtmAnamityatra tAvadupAsakakarmaNAmakShayaphalatvashravaNAt.h | itaratra cha j~nAnavidyAshabdayoH parokShaj~nAnArthatvasyApyupapatterityAshaN^kAM pariharati- nacheti ||
atra vAkyeShu | phalaM karmaNAm.h | tathA j~nAnAdipadaM parokShaj~nAnArthatayA na vyAkhyeyamityapi grAhyam.h | kuto netyata Aha- nahIti ||
j~nAnaM brahmasAkShAtkAram.h | kvApi mokShe.anyatra cha | phalasya karmaNAm.h | 
idamuktaM bhavati | brahmasAkShAtkArarahitenopAsakena kR^itAni karmANyakShayaphalAni kena prakAreNeti chintyam.h | kimakShayaM mokShaM kurvantIti | uta svargAdikam.h | nAdyaH | nAnyaH panthA iti shrutivirodhAt.h | na dvitIyaH | puNyachito lokaH kShIyata iti svargAdiphalAnAM kShayitvashravaNAt.h | "anevaMvinmahatpuNyaM karma karoti' "tadeva vIryavattaraM bhavati' ityudAhR^itashrutivirodhashcha pakShadvaye.api | tadevamaj~napakShe vAkyArthAnupapatterupAsakapadasya j~nAnyupalakShakatvameva yuktam.h | tathA brahmAbhyetIti shravaNAjj~nAnapadasya sAkShAtkAravAchitvameva yuktamiti | ata eva vAkyasAmarthyAdityuktam.h | yadyapi pashyannapImamAtmAnamityAdyAH spaShyArthAH shrutayo.atra santi | tathA.api mImAMsArthametAsAmudAharaNam.h |
nanvaj~napakShe.api nAnupapattiH | upAsakena kR^itAni khalvasaN^kalpitaphalAni karmANi j~nAnamupajanayanti | karmaNA j~nAnamAtanotIti shruteH | j~nAnena mokSho bhavatItyaj~nakR^itakarmaNAmapi j~nAnadvAreNAkShayaphalatvopapatterityAshaN^kayAha- j~nAneti ||
karmaphalasyAkShayateti vartate | tasya parakR^itavyAkhyAnasya | asmatpakShapratIpatA muktatAratamyavirodhitA | pratyuta tadanukUlataiva | muktau tAratamyamasahamAnena khalvevamanyathA vyAkhyAnaM kriyate tanmuktatAratamyameva sAdhayati | karmANi hi jij~nAsavo vichitrANi kurvanti | taishcha jAyamAnena j~nAnena vichitreNaiva bhAvyam.h | anyathA kR^itaviprANAkR^itAbhyAgamApatte | vichitreNa j~nAnena vichitra eva mokSho bhAvanIyaH | pUrvoktAdeva hetoriti | tadevaM svamatavirodhiparAnukUlamanyathAvyAkhyAnaM na kAryameva | tathA chAsmadvayAkhyAne sthite prakR^itaM yuktamiti |
astu vA.anyathAvyAkhyAnaM yuktam.h | tatashchaiteShAM vAkyAnAM prakR^itAsAdhakatvam.h | evamapi j~nAnottarakarmaNo mokShAntargataphalahetutAyAH pramANAntareNa siddhermuktatAratamyaM na hAtuM shakyamityabhyupagamavAdenAha- j~nAnottarasyeti ||
karmaNo.akShayatvamakShayamokShAnupraveshiphalatvaM siddhayati | kathamityata Aha- nacheti ||
prakArAntarAbhAvAt.h | parisheShapramANAditi yAvat.h | etena j~nAnottarasya karmaNaH sAphalye.api tasya phalasya mokShAnupraveshitAyAM pramANAbhAvAnna mokShatAratamyasiddhirityapi pratyuktam.h | 
parisheShameva darshayati- pUrveti ||
j~nAnikR^iteShu karmasvetA vidhAstAvatsambhavanti | j~nAnArthatvaM vA bhogArthatvaM vA vyarthatvaM veti | tatra j~nAnikarmaNAM j~nAnArthatvaM tAvannopapadyate | pUrvabhAvishabhaireva j~nAnasya kR^itatvAt.h | tatra hetuH pUrvabhAvIti | j~nAnAtpUrvabhAvinAM shubhAnAM yasamAjj~nAnenaiva kAryeNa kR^itArthatA nAnyena | teShAM kAryAntarAbhAvAt.h | j~nAnArthatvAbhAve vaiyarthyaM syAdityarthaH | pUrvajAtaM prati pashchAdbhAvinaH kAraNatvAyogAchcha | nApi bhogArthatvam.h | prAchInaprArabdhakarmabhireva bhogasya jAyamAnatvAt.h | tatra hetuH prArabdhAnAM cha karmaNAM bhogenaiva kR^itArthateti | pUrvavattAtparyam.h | vaiyarthyanirAsaheturanyatheti | j~nAnikarmaNAM vyarthatve tadanuShThAnaM na syAt.h | nahi prekShAvanto vyarthaM (karma) kurvanti | karaNasvAbhAvyAditi chet.h | abuddhipUrvatAprasaN^gAt.h | lokasaN^grahArthamiti chenna | tatprayojanasyApi vAchyatvAt.h | Ishvaravaditi chenna | muktAvapi prasaN^gAt.h | parisheShaphalakathanaM tattasmAjj~nAnottarakarmaNAM muktAvanupravesho muktigatAnandavR^iddhayarthatvaM syAditi |
pUrvabhAvishubhAni j~nAnArthAnItyuktam.h | tatra sarveShAM j~nAnArthatAyAM prasaktAyAM visheShamAha- j~nAnAdIti ||
j~nAnAtpUrvANyakAmyAnyeva shubhAni karmANi puNyakarmANi j~nAnasiddhaye bhavanti na tu kAmyAni | shubhAnIti visheShaNasya kR^ityamAha- niShiddhAnIti ||
j~nAnAnutpAda utpannasyApyabhibhavo vA j~nAnarodhaH | bhuktaye duHkhasya | evaM kAmyasyApi viniyogo j~nAtavyaH | etachcha(cha)turthe vyutpAdanIyam.h |
nanu yathA.akAmyAni shubhAnIti cha visheShaNamupAdIyate tathA nityanaimittikavyatiriktAnItyapi visheShaNamupAdeyam.h | nityAderapi pratyavAyaparihArAthartvena j~nAnakAraNatvAbhAvAdityata Aha- yogyatAyA iti ||
yogyAta brAhmaNatvAdirUpA pitR^imaraNAdirUpA cha | Adito j~nAnAtpUrvaM kR^itam.h | anyasya pratyavAyamAtraparihArasya | "AdhyAnAya prayojanAbhAvAt.h' ityatrAsyArthasya samarthitatvAnneha heturuktaH | atra yogyatAyA balAchChubhamAditaH kR^itametachcha j~nAnameva kuryAditi cha vaktavye yadubhayatra bAhulyagrahaNaM kR^itaM tattasya nAsmatpakShapratIpatetyuktaprapaJNchanArthamiti |
atra "puruShArtho.ataHshabdAd.h' ityAdinA j~nAnasya mokShasAdhanatvamuktam.h | atra cha karmatAratamyAjj~nAnatAratamyaM j~nAnatAratamyAnmokShatAratamyamiti vadatA cha sUchitam.h | j~nAnapadaM chAvabodhamAtrasya pratipAdakamiti pratItinirAsArthamAha- j~nAnasyeti ||
asmiJNChAstre yatra yatra j~nAnasya mokShasAdhanatvamuchyate tatra tatra j~nAnamiti padena bhaktirIryate lakShyate | kutaH | sambandhAt.h | j~nAnasya bhaktibhAgatvAt.h | mAhAtmyaj~nAnasnehasamudAyo hi bhaktirityuktam.h | tato j~nAnaM bhakterbhAga ekadeshaH | tathA chaikadeshaikadeshitvalakShaNAtsambandhAdityuktaM bhavati | ekadeshenaikadeshilakShaNA cha da(shama)shAmAtraM dattamityAdau prasiddhaiva |
prakArAntaramAha- j~nAnasyaiveti ||
yadyadA j~nAnasyaiva visheShaH snehAdisAhityalakShaNo dharmo bhavati tadA sa piNDo bhaktirityabhidhIyate | etaduktaM bhavati | j~nAnaM snehashcha bhakteraMshau | tatraikenAMshenAMshAntarasyopalakShaNam.h | tathAchAhajallakShaNayA bhaktireva sidhyatIti | ekadeshAntareNaikadeshAntarasyopalakShaNe dR^iShyAntamAha- parokShatveti ||
yathA j~nAnasya parokShatvAparokShatvalakShaNau dvau dharmau | tatra tamevaM vidvAniti parokShaj~nAnasya mokShasAdhanatve.abhihite parokShatvenAparokShatvaM lakShyata ityarthaH | dArShyAntikaM dasharyati- snehayogo.apIti || 
snehashchAsau yoga upAyashcheti snehayogaH | snehena yogaH sambandha iti vA | tata e(kenai)kadeshenaikadeshAntaralakShaNA cha syAditi sheShaH |
lAkShaNikaprayoge sUtrakArasya kiM prayojanamityata Aha- ityabhiprAyata iti ||
dvividhalakShaNAbhkimayeNa shrutayaH tarati shokamAtmavidityAdyAH | idamuktaM bhavati | dvividhA lakShaNA bhavati rUDhArUDhabhedAt.h | tatra dvitIyAyAM prayoktuH prayojanAnusandhAnena bhAvyam.h | na tvAdyAyAmabhidhAtulyAyAm.h | iyaM cha rUDhalakShaNA | shrutiShu prAyikavyavahArAdarshanAt.h | ataH kiM prayojanAnveShaNeneti |
bhaktishabdo mAhAtmyaj~nAnapUrvakasya snehasya vAchaka ityuktaM tathA j~nAnashabdo bhaktyartha iti | tadubhayamapyanupapannam.h | bhaktij~nAnAbhyAM mokSho bhavatItyapi darshanAt.h | tatra bhaktishabdasyoktArthatve j~nAnagrahaNavaiyarthyAt.h | (tasya tatrAntarbhUtatvAt.h) | j~nAnapadasya chobhayArthatve bhaktigrahaNavaiyarthyAdityata Aha- so.ayamiti ||
kvApi bhaktirj~nAnamiti padAbhyAM so.ayaM snehalakShaNo bodhalakShaNashcha visheSho.apyudIryate | na tUkta evArtha iti niyamastasmAnnAnupapattiH | yatra bhaktij~nAne(j~nAnaM) sahochyate tadA punaruktiprasaN^gAdbhaktipadaM svArthaikadeshatyAgena snehAMshasya lakShakam.h | natu mukhyArthaniShTham.h | j~nAnapadaM chAnupapattyabhAvAnmukhyArthameva natu lakShakamiti bhAvaH |
nanu vinA snehAjj~nAnamAtreNa yadi muktiranupapannA syAt.h | tadA j~nAnapadasya lakShakatvamAshrayaNIyam.h | nachaivam.h | puruShArthasya bhaktyekasAdhyatve pramANAbhAvAt.h | dveShiNAmapi shishupAlAdInAM mokShadarshanAchcha | dveShiNaH snigdhA ityasya cha vipratiShiddhatvAt.h | ato.anupapannaM lakShaNAshrayaNamityato dveShasya mokShasAdhanatvaM tAvannirAkaroti- na hIti ||
atra dveShasya puruShArthasAdhanatva niShiddhayate | dR^ishiriti tu prasaN^gAduktam.h | j~nAnasyAvashyakatAmupAdAya snehanirAsAya hi paraH pratyavasthitaH | kaimutyArthaM vA | mAhAtmyaj~nAnamapi na dveShayuktaM mokShahetuH | kimuta kevalo dveSha iti | yathoktam.h | "naiShkarmyamapyachyutabhAvavarjitaM na shobhate j~nAnamalaM viraJNjanam.h' iti | 
dveShasya muktisAdhashratvAN^gIkAre kathaM sarvashrutivirodha ityatastAvadekAM shrutiM paThati- chetanasyeti ||
jIvajAtasya | dvayameva | tatra muktisaMsArayormadhye | madhyaM mAnuShatvam.h | adho narakAdi | nityaM sukhamekaM muktitvena j~neyam.h | tathA nityaduHkhamaparamiti j~neyam.h | saMsR^itau saMsR^itiviShaye, sAdhanamapi dveSho bhaktishcheti yogyatayA sambandhaH | vidhAyakaM 
kArakam.h | nityasukharUpA sanmuktiH | iti j~nAyata iti sheShaH |
sanmuktikAraNatvasyApratiShedhAtkathamevamuchyata ityata Aha- asaditi ||
nityaduHkhasvarUpANAM mukteH kAraNatvena tAvad.h dveSha uktaH | tena sanmuktikAraNaM na bhavatIti j~nAyate virodhAditi | nanvasyAM shrutau muktiviShayau bhaktidveShau sadasanmuktikAraNatvenochyeta | viShNuviShayau tu prakR^itau | ataH kiM kena saN^gatamityata Aha- muktAviti ||
muktAvityatra saptamyante pade muktIti prAtipadikenoditaH | kevalaM muktishabdodita ityukte muktidvayetyatrApi prAptiH | ato muktAvityatretyuktam.h | kena nimittenetyata Aha- mokShamiti ||
muchlR^i mokShaNa ityasmAtstrayAM ktiniti ktin.hpratyayaH | sa cha bahulagrahaNAtkartaryapi bhavati | yadvA karotIti karaNe kartR^itvopachAraH | muchyate.aneneti muktirita karaNe ktinpratyayaH | Joshi-32
्veShasya mokShasAdhanatvAN^gIkAre yuktivirodhaM chAha- dveShato.apIti ||
na kevalaM bhaktyA kintu dveShato.api vishiShyA muktishchedaN^gIkriyate tadA yatsarvashrutyAdInAM bhagavad.hguNotkarSha eva mahAtAtparyaM tadviruddhamApadyeta | kathamityata Aha- bhaktyeti ||
anye.apyAgamAH | shrutyAdayo muktiprayojanAH parameshvaraguNaviShayAshcheti tAvatprasiddham.h | tatra sambandho.ayameva | yadbhagavata eva jIvAnAM muktiH | sA cha prasannAdeva | prasAdashcha bhaktyaiva | bhaktishcha guNaj~nA(nAdeve)na evetyevaM shrutyAdyAstadguNAnvadantIti | tathAcha kathaM dveShato muktyaN^gIkAre na mahAtAtparyavirodhaH |
bhaktermokShasAdhanatvamanena gamyate | nacha tadasmAbhirapAkriyate | kintu bhaktivad.h dveShasyApItyata Aha- yadIti ||
tadA dveShotpAdanArthamiti sheShaH | nachaivam.h | guNamAtrapratipAdanasya pratipAditatvAt.h | tato mokShArthaM pravR^itto vedAdirguNAneva pratipAdayanmokShasya bhaktimAtrasAdhyatvamabhipraitIti gamyata iti bhAvaH |
nanu dveShAchchaidyAdayo nR^ipA ityAdIni dveShasyApi mokShasAdhanatAM pratipAdayanti vAkyAni santi | tatkathaM dveShasya muktisAdhanatvAbhAva ityata Aha- smartavya iti ||
purANe kvachitpradeshe | bhagavAnnityaM smartavya ityabhiprAyeNaiva dveShAnmuktimAheva purANakR^iditi sambandhaH | tasmAnnoktavirodha iti herarthaH |
idamuktaM bhavati | purANavAkyaM dveShasya muktisAdhanatvaM pratipAdayadivApAtato yadyapi pratIyateta | tathA.api tanna tadabhiprAyam.h | kintu mumukShuNA bhagavansarvadA smartavya iti tasyAbhiprAyaH | yathA "vR^iddhau cha mAtApitarau sAdhvI bhAryA sutaH shishuH | apyakAryashataM kR^itvA bhartavyA manurabravIt.h' ityatra nAkAryakaraNe tAtparyaM kintu sarvathA bhartavyatve, tathehApIti | guNAnAheti tAtparyAntaram.h | chaidyAdInAM dveShato muktiM pratipAdayadvAkyaM bhagavataH kR^ipAlutvAdInguNAnAheti | shApAdinA dveShiNo.api chaidyAdyAstAtkAlikadveShamanirUpya pUrvatanIM bhaktimevApekShya bhagavatA sUchitAH | aho kR^ipAlutvaM nirvikAratvaM satyasaN^kalpatvaM cha tasyetyatra tAtparyaM teShAM vAkyAnAmityarthaH | dvividhAni vAkyAni, vaireNa yannR^ipataya ityAdIni smaraNapradhAnAni teShAM prathamA gatiH | dveShAchchaidyAdaya ityAdIni dveShapradhAnAni teShAM dvitIyeti hR^idayam.h |
prathamavyAkhyAne laukikadR^iShyAntamAha- kruddhavAkyavaditi | kruddhavAkyasya yathA na pratIta evArthapramANyam.h kintvanyatra, tathaivetyarthaH |
etadvivR^iNoti- yatheti ||
mareti prakR^ityantarasyaitadrUpam.h | "jIva vA mara vA sAdho vyAdha mA jIva mA mara' iti prayogadarshanAt.h | AkShepo nindA | svena proktasyAnyasya kAryasya | pitA kiJNchitputraM prati vidhatte idaM kurvIti | sa tu shramAdibhIrurakurvANa evAvatiShThate | tadA kruddhaH pitA bravIti | are jAlma vaidhaveya mi्rayasveti | tasya vAkyasya yathA na putramaraNavidhAne tAtpayarM kintu svavihitakaraNe | tathAcha dveSheNa smaraNe muktirbhavatIti purANavAkyasyApi na dveShasya muktisAdhanatve tAtpayarm.h | kintu smaraNasya kartavyatAyAmiti |
iyaM cha vyaJNjanAvR^ittiriti kechit.h | tAtparyavR^ittirityapare | vAkyalakShaNA(a)numA(namityA)naM chetyAchAryAH | pratIta evArthaH kinna syAdityata Aha- shrutIti ||
purANagaM vAkyamiti vartate | shrutayo.atItapAde.atra chodAhR^itAH | yatra dveShasya muktisAdhanatvamuchyate tatraiva tadviruddhamuchyata iti 
svavirodhaH | so.api hiraNyakashipushchetyAdibhAgAvatavAkyAnAM paThitatvAtpradarshita eva | aJNjasA mukhyayA vR^ittyA | dveShAnmuktiM pratipAdayanna bhavati |
AgamavirodhaM darshayati- tama iti ||
viShNau bhaktyA jAtena viShNuprasAdenaiva muktiM saMyAnti | tathA viShNau dveSheNa jAtena vilomatvena viShNukopenAJNjasA tamaH saMyAntIti yojanA | chashabdau samuchchayArthau | uktArthaniyAmakaM viShNubhaktireva muktisAdhanaM na dveSha ityasyArthasya niyAmakam.h | etadvAkyasamAkhyayA chetanasyeti shrutau muktAvitishabdo viShNorvAchaka iti siddhayati | tathAcha dveSho bhaktishchetyetad.h dvayaM sanmukteH kevalo dveShastvasanmukteH kAraNamityanyathApratItirapAstA bhavati |
itashcha naitadvAkyaM patItArthaparamityAha- mahAtAtparyeti ||
mokShaprayojanAnAM sarvAgamAnAM bhagavadguNeShveva yanmahAtAtparyaM tadanyathA.anupapattyA bhaktireva muktisAdhanaM na dveSha ityavagamyate | ato mahAtAtparyavirodhena cha dveShavAkyaM pratItArthe kathaM pramANatAM yAti | 
kathamidaM labhyate | arthashabdo mukhyaM pratipAdyamAha | "sata eva padAtharsya' iti yathA | sa chaikavachanAntaH | tena cha tatpratipAdakatvaM lakShyata iti | kathamayaM mahAtAtparyashabdArtha ityata Aha- vAchakatvaM hIti ||
tat.h paraM pratipAdyaM yasya tattatparam.h | tasya bhAvastAtparyamitye(vamarthavA)vaM vAchakatvaM pratipAdakatvaM hi tAtparyamuchyate | tasya cha mahachChabdena visheShaNe yogyatayaiSho.artho mahAtAtparyashabdasya bhavatIti bhAvaH | tataH kimityata Aha- yadarthA iti ||
yo.artho yeShAM te yadarthAH | ravA AgamAH | ekashabdasya saMshaye ekavAkyasambandhini saMshaye satyekaM sandigdhaM viruddhArthaM vAkyamAdAyetyarthaH | 
etaduktaM bhavati | sarvANi vAkyAni sambhUyAnanyArthatayA yamekamarthaM pratipAdayanti tadviruddhArthaM pratipAdayattadavAntaravAkyaM yaduNlabhyate sAvakAshaM cha tanmahAvAkyArthavirodhAdanyathA kriyate na tu tadviruddho mahAvAkyArthastyajyata iti tAvatprasiddham.h | mahAvAkyasya pradhAnatvAdupakramAdibhirnishchitArthatvAchcha | avAntaravAkyasyApradhAnatvAtsandigdhArthatvAchcha | prakR^ite tu bhaktireva muktisAdhanaM na dveSha iti sarvairvAkyaiH sambhUya pratipAdito.arthaH | arthAkShi(akShi)ptasyApi pratipAdyasyeva tadarthatvAt.h | dveShAnmuktiM pratipAdayadekaM tadavAntaravAkyaM sAvakAshaM choktaprakAreNa | tasmAdidameva bAdhyata iti |
dveShasya muktisAdhanatvanirAkaraNamupasaMharati- ata iti ||
mAhAtmyaj~nAnasnehAbhyAmeva na tu dveSheNetyarthaH | mokSha iti vaktavye paraH puruShArtha iti vadatA j~nAnAdikamapi dveShiNAM na bhavatIti sUchitam.h | j~nAnAderapi dharmAdyapekShayA parapuruShArthatvAt.h | 
evaM dveShasya muktisAdhanatvaM nirAkR^ityedAnIM bhakteH paramapuruShArthasAdhakatve pramANaM nAstIti yaduktaM tannirAsAya pramANAntaramAha- yasyeti ||
yathA deve devayogyA tathA gurau guruyogyetyarthaH | anena j~nAnasya bhaktisAdhyatvamuchyate | bhaktyA j~nAnamityanena j~nAnAdeH | j~nAnaM parokShanishchayo jAyate | tato j~nAnAtpakvA bhaktirbhavati | tato dR^iShyistatashcha sA paripakvA bhaktiH | tato mokShAnantaraM bhaktiravatiShThate | sA sukharUpiNyeva syAnna phalavatI | bhaktyA prasanna ityanenApIdamevochyate | j~nAnAbhAve bhaktyAbhAvAdanAkulamityuktam.h | tayaiva pakvayA etayA paripakvayA | vedairiti bhaktirahitashravaNAdibhirityarthaH | na vidyate.anyo viShayo yasyAH sA.ananyA | "yAdR^ishI tatra bhaktiH syAttAdR^ishyanyatra naiva cheta | ananyabhakti sA j~neyA viShNAveva cha sA bhavet.h' iti cha smR^itiH | vivakShitastu sandhibharvatIti vachanAchChakya ahamiti yujyate | tattvena yAthArthyena j~nAtum.h | ityAdivAkyatashcheti chashabdena chetanasya dvayamityAdIni pUrvodAhR^itavAkyAni samuchchinoti | vAkyata eva na tvarthAt.h | 
anumAnenApyuktamarthaM sAdhayati- nacheti ||
bhagavad.hdveShAdbhagavatprasAdaM naivamApnoti | bhagavadbhaktyA taM bhagavatprasAdaM prApnuyAdityasminnarthe dR^iShyAnusAritvaM patyakShadR^iShyavyAptikAnumAnAnusAritvamapIyate j~nAyate | 
etaduktaM bhavati | bhagavatprasAdAdeva mokSha iti tAvanniShyaN^kitam.h | bhagavatprasAdo bhagavad.hdveShasAdhyo na bhavati | bhagavatprasAdatvAt.h | yo yatprasAdo nAsau tad.hdveShasAdhyo yagA guruprasAdaH | yadvA bhagavad.hdveSho bhagavatprasAdasAdhanaM na bhavati | bhagavad.hdveShatvAt.h | yo yad.hdveShaH sa tatprasAdasAdhanaM na bhavati | yathA gurudveShaH | athavA bhagavAnsvadveShiNi na prasIdati prekShAvatpuruShatvAt.h devadattavat.h | yadvA bhagavad.hdveShI bhagavatprItiviShayo na bhavati bhagavad.hdveShitvAt.h | yo yad.hdveShI nAsau 
tatprItiviShayaH | yathA sampratipanna iti dveShasya prasAdasAdhanatve.apAste muktisAdhanatvamevApAstaM bhavati | tathA bhagavatprasAdo bhagavadbhaktisAdhyo bhagavatprasAdatvAt.h | yo yatprasAdaH sa tadbhaktisAdhyo yathA guruprasAdaH | yadvA bhagavadbhaktiH bhagavatprasAdasAdhanaM bhagavadbhaktitvAt.h | yA yadbhaktiH sA tatprasAdasAdhanaM yathA gurubhaktiH | athavA bhagavAnsvabhakte prasIdati prekShAvatpuruShArthatvAt.h | sammatavat.h | yadvA bhagavadbhakto bhagavatprItiviShayo bhagavadbhaktatvAt.h | yo yadbhakto.asau tatprItiviShayaH | yathA gurubhakta iti | bhakteH prasAdasAdhanatve siddhe muktisAdhanatvameva siddhaM bhavatIti |
nanvalaukike bhagavati lokadR^iShyAntenaivamanumAnaM na yujyate | anyathA.aNutvAdiniyamasyApyanumAnApatteH | ato lokavilakShaNo dviShyo.api prasIdatItyAN^gIkAre na bAdhakamiti shaN^kAmAgamavAkyena pariharati- ya iti ||
pR^ithag.h lokavailakShaNyena, sAdaraM tAtparyeNa, dR^iShyavailomyAd.h dR^iShyavailomyamanAdR^itya | aparaM vedAnuktaM lokavilakShaNaM guNajAtaM naivAN^gIkAryam.h | kintu vedoktAdaNutvamahattvayaugapadyAderanyad.hguNajAtam.h | guNA ityasya prayojanamuchyate- doShAbhAva iti ||
chastvarthaH | lokavilakShaNA avilakShaNAshcheti sheShaH | mahAtAtparyashaktita sati ||
sarvathA.api doSho bhagavati nAstItyatra sAmAnyataH sarvashAstrANAM tAtparyasya nirNItatvAdityarthaH | vedAnuktasyAprAmANikArthasya grahaNamayuktamityAshaN^kAmanena nirAchaShye | visheShato.anuktAvapi sAmAnyataH siddheriti bhAvaH | tat.h tasmAdIrito.arthaH siddhAntaH prAmANikaH | yadvA bR^ihatsaMhiterito.artho hi siddhAnta iti tatra bahumAnamutpAdayati | 
evaM bhaktereva mokShasAdhanatvamupapAditam.h | bhaktishcha kevalaM bhagavadviShayaiveti pratItimapAkartumAha- tAratamyeneti ||
na kevalaM viShNau kintu tadbhakteShu ramAdiShvapi, vinishchayAt.h sarvathA, sA cha kriyamANA tAratamyenaiva | kuta ityata Aha- eShA.apIti ||
yatastadbhakteShu kriyamANaiShA.api bhagavadbhaktirevAtastadviShaye.api bhaktiH kartavyA | etaduktaM bhavati | viShNubhaktistAvatkartavyetyupapAditam.h | sA cha tadbhaktabhaktyaiva sAN^gA nAnyatheti | etadapi kuta ityata Aha- loketi ||
lokashabdena lekasiddhavyAptimadanumAnamuchyate | vedashabdenAgamamAtram.h | 
lokAnusAritAM darshayati- yo hIti || 
pradhAne rAjAdau | viparyaye tadIyabhaktirAhitye | viparItaH pradhAnabhaktirahitaH | niyamena dR^ishyate | anenAnvayavyatirekAvuktau | tathA chAyaM prayogaH | vimato bhagavadbhaktabhaktimAnbhavet.h bhagavadbhaktyA puruShArthabhAktvAt.h | yo yadbhaktyA puruShAtharbhAgyathA sammata iti |
nanu daityAdayo brahmAdiShu bhaktimanto.api tadbhakteShvindrAdiShu bhaktirahitA dR^ishyante | tato vyabhichAra ityata Aha- vyabhichAra iti ||
yadi kvApi pareNa vyabhichArashchodyate tadA.asmAbhiratra puruShe bhaktihrAsaH kalpyate viphalabhaktitvamuchyate | tathAcha vipakShe vishiShyasya hetorabhAvAnna vyabhichAra ityarthaH | kuta evaM kalpyata ityata Aha- bhaktIti ||
tadbhakteShvapi bhaktimAnneti yadasau pradhAnabhaktereva doSho hi | tena pradhAnabhaktireva duShyA na phalAyAlamiti prasiddham.h | hiraNyagarbhAdibhirdaityAdibhyo.amaratvAdikaM sachChalameva dIyate mR^iShA na bhavatIti purANeShu suprasiddhameveti | vedAnusAritvaM tUttaratra pradarshayiShyate |
tadbhaktabhaktiH kartavyetyetadanumAnenopapAdya sA cha tAratamyena kAryetyetadanumAnena sAdhayati- tAratamyeneti ||
teShu tadbhakteShu kriyamANA bhaktiraddhA sarvathA tAratamyena kAryA | kutaH dR^iShyAnusarataH | tAratamyenetyasyaiva vivaraNaM viShNuprasAdAnusArAditi | yasminnadhiko viShNuprasAdastasminnadhiketyAdi | tadanyathA sAmyena vaiparItyena cha karaNe.anartho bhavati | 
dR^iShyAnusArata ityuktaM darshayati- sveti ||
atra svashabdena rAjAdiH kathyate | tatprItyanusAreNa tasya yasminyathA prItistadanusAreNa bhaktikaraNe sati tasminbhakte tasya rAjAdeH prItiraddhA niyamenaiva dR^ishyate | ayamatra prayogaH | IshvaraH svaprItyanusAreNa svabhakteShu bhakteH prasIdati | prekShAvatpuruShatvAdrAjavaditi | anena prameyAntaramapi siddhamityAha- tAratamyeti ||
etenaiva bhagavadbhakteShu ramAbrahmAdiShu tAratamyenaiva muktiH karaNIyeti samarthitenaiva devatAtAratamyaparij~nAnaM yatprAguktaM tadapi mokShasya sAdhanamiti siddham.h | na hyavidite tAratamye tAratamyAnurodhena muktikaraNaM sambhavati | anenaiva prakAreNAnumAnasambhavAditi 
vA.atideshArthaH | 
bhagavatprasAdatAratamyAnusAreNa tadIyeShu muktiH kAryetyatrAgamamapyAha- lakShmIti ||
tena bhagavatprItikrameNaiva | tiShThatu kramasteShu bhaktikaraNameva kutaH | bhagavatprItigocharatvAdeva | kAraNAntaraM chochyate- sarve.apIti ||
gurutvaM vidyApravartakatvena prasiddhameva | pUjyAshchetyAdinA bhaktereva prapaJNchanaM hariM parito na tu pR^ithak.h | vedAnusArata iti yaduktaM tadapyanena dashirtaM bhavati | krameNaiva tayIyeShu bhaktistatsmR^itirityAdau tachChabdena tadIyA uchyante | krameNaiveti sarvatra sambaddhayate | krameNeti hariviShayANi bhaktyAdIni mukhyasAdhanAni tadIyaviShayANi tvamukhyasAdhanAnItyarthaH | muktisAdhanatvAdakhilaimarumukShubhirnityasAdhyAni | sAdhanasya vinirNaya iti sAdhanavinirNayAkhye.avAntaraprakaraNe.astItyarthaH | 
etadeva vivR^iNoti- pravR^itta iti ||
paJNcharAtre pravR^ittaM nAmAvAntaro granthaH | tatrApi sAdhanasya vinirNayo nAma prakaraNamastItyarthaH | 
uktArtheShvanumAnAntarANyAha- harIti ||
sad.hdveShatvAt.h uttamapuruShadveShatvAt.h | vaiShNavairdaityAdiShu kriyamANe dveShe vyabhichAraM vArayituM sadityuktam.h | gurordveShaH | prAgdveShasya bhagavatprasAdasAdhanatvAbhAve sAmAnyavyAptimAshritya bhagavad.hdveShatvaM heturuktaH, atra tu shubhamAtrasAdhanatvAbhAve visheShavyAptimevAshritya sad.hdveShatvamiti mahAnbhedaH | kramAdbhaktiriti | kramamanusR^itya ramAdiShu bhaktirdharmiNItyarthaH | tatpriyopagA bhaktiryata iti | haripriyaviShayabhaktitvAdityarthaH | tatpriyAnugachChati viShayIkarotIti tatpriyopagA | yA yatpriyaviShayA bhaktiH sA tatprItikAraNAt.h | yathA svasminbhaktiH | atra svashabdena devadatta uchyate | yathA rAjapriye devadatte bhaktI rAjaprItikAraNamityarthaH | iha kramAditi pratij~nAyAM visheShaNaprakShepeNa bhagavadbhaktabhakteH kartavyatvaM tattAratamyasya chAvashyakatvaM siddhayati | yadvA.anena prayogadvayaM sUchayati | bhAgavatabhaktirbhagavatprItikAraNaM bhagavatpriyabhaktitvAditi | bhagavAn.hrAmAdiShu tAratamyopetabhaktyaiva prasIdati | tAratamyenaiva tadviShayaprItimattvAditi cha | yuktishcheti sambandhaH | atra prAgukte.arthe | 
kiM sAmAnyavyAptyA, visheShavyAptirapyastItyAshayena prayogAntaramuchyate- prAdhAnyeti ||
uttamatvatAratamyAnusAriNI ramAdiShu bhaktirhareH prItidaiva | yasmAtsottamA bhaktiH | shAstravihitabhaktitvAdityarthaH | svopagA sA viShNuviShayA bhaktiryathetyarthaH | iti vA anumAtavyamiti sheShaH | atrApi pUrvavadvishiShyasAdhAtpR^ithak.hprayogadvayena vA sAdhyadvayasiddhiH | 
|| iti ubhayaliN^gAdhikArikAdhikaraNe ||
|| atha phalashrutyadhikaraNam.h ||
|| OM svAminaH phalashruterityAtreyaH OM || j~nAnaM mahAphalakAraNamiti puruShArthAdhikaraNe pratipAditam.h | j~nAnottaramanuShThitaM varNAshramakarma shamadamAdikaM chAnandAtishayakAraNamiti stutyadhikaraNe | tadetajj~nAnakarmAdiphalaM kiM prerakatvAddevAnAM bhavati uta kartR^itvAddevadattasyeti saMshaye prathamasUtreNa devAnAmeveti pUrvapakShayitvA | "ArtvijyamityauDulomistasmai hi parikriyate' ityekadeshimatena siddhAntamabhidhAya "sahakAryantaravidhiH pakSheNa tR^itIyaM tadvato vidhyAdivat.h' iti paramasiddhAnto.abhihitaH | tatra devAnAM j~nAnAdiphalamiti pUrvapakShAMsho grAhya eva | avadhAraNamAtrameva tyAjyam.h | ataH pUrvapakShasUtrArthaM vivR^iNoti- j~nAneti ||
phalaM cha devAnAM bhavatIti sheShaH | bhavachchaiShu deveShu kramopagaM krameNaivopagachChati | devadattenAnuShThitasya j~nAnAdeH phalaM devAnAM bhavatItyekA pratij~nA | bhavachcha tatkrameNaiva na tu sAmyena vaiparItyena veti dvitIyA | tatrAdyAyAM hetuM sUchayandvitIyamupapAdayati- svAtanteti ||
phalinAM phalabhAjAM, svAtantyatAratamyena svAmyatAratamyAnusAreNaiva hi phalena bhAvyam.h | natu sAmyena vaiparItyena vetyarthaH | brahmAdayastAratamyenaiva phalavantastatra tAratamyenaiva svAtantAdityuktaM bhavata | anena prathamapratij~nAyAM svAtantyahetuH sUchito bhavati yaH sUtre svAmipadenoktaH | yadyapi phalaprAptau tAratamyaM na sUtritam.h | tathA.api phalaprAptAvuktasya svAmitvahetoH sAmarthyena prAptamiti tadapyupapAditam.h |
yadi svAtantAddevadattAnuShThitaj~nAnAdiphalaM devAnAM syAttarhi tadanuShThitamithyAj~nAnAdiphalamapi prasajyetAvisheShAdityata Aha- ashubhaM tviti ||
anyagamashubhaM tveShAM devAnAM kvachidapi bhogAya na bhavati | kutaH | hareH prItito.ashubhe.apyeShAM svAtantAdbhagavatprasAdena 
maitadasmAnprApaditi nivAraNe teShAM sAmarthyasadbhAvAt.h | maitadetAnprApaditi harerevAj~nayA cha | anyagamiti vadatA svagataM tu bhavatIti sUchitam.h | anenAsati nivAraNakAraNa iti svAmitvaheturvisheShito bhavati |
yaduktamavisheShAditi tadasiddham.h | vyavasthApakashrutisadbhAvAdityAha- puNyameveti ||
anena "puNyamevAmuM gachChati na ha vai devAnpApaM gachChati' iti shrutimupAdatte | amuM saptAnnavidyopAsanena prerakatayA parapurapraveshinaM parakR^itaM puNyamevApnoti na pApam.h | kutaH | devo hyasau jAto | nahi devAnprApnotItyarthaH | ukte.arthe shubhameva bhavati nAshubhamityarthe | 
vyavasthApakAntaramAha- yuktaya iti ||
aparAH pUrvoktAbhyAm.h | ukte.arthe mAnamiti sambandhaH | 
kAstA yuktaya ityatastA darshayitumAgamavAkyaM paThati- upasaneti ||
yataH kAraNAddehAntare sthitiH, parapuraM pravishya tatra puNyapApapreraNaM, devAnAM bhagavadupAsanAjanitadharmaphalam.h | ataH kathaM pApAdikaM prerayanto.api doShAnavApnuyuH | nahi sAttviko dharmo duHkhaparyavasAyI | tattvavyAghAtAdityarthaH | parapure devAnAM pApAdipreraNaM na duHkhahetuH | sAttvikadharmaphalatvAttattvaj~nAnavadityuktaM bhavati | kiJNcha te devA vAsudevAj~nayaiva na tu svechChayA tattatkR^itapUrvakarmAnusArata eva | ata evArAgadveShato rAgadveShau vinaiva nityasho jIvAnpuNyapApeShu prerayanti hi yasmAttasmAtkathaM doShAnavApnuyuH | prabhorAj~nayA.aparAdhAnusAreNa chorashAsakarAjapuruShavaditi bhAvaH | pApAdipreraNena devAnAmashubhaM na bhavatItyeva kevalaM na, kintu haryAj~nA.anuShThAnAjjyotiShyomAdyanuShThAtR^ibhirivaibhirdevaiH puNyamevApyate | kiJNcha svavihitaparapreraNe haripUjeyamiti choddeshAtkathaM devA na shubhamApanuyuH | ata ityupasaMhAraH | 
dharmaj~nAnayoreveti yojyam.h | prApnuvanto.apyAviriJNchato yathAkramaM prApnuvantItyapUrvoktirnopasaMhAraH | anyagataM j~nAnAdiphalaM devAH prApnuvanti | devagataM tu kathamityapekShAyAmuktam.h- devA iti ||
devAnAmapakR^iShyAnAm.h | atastadIyaj~nAnAdiphalaM teShAM bhavatIti sheShaH | brahmA tviti AviriJNchata ityuktasya vivaraNam.h |
devAdigrahaNamupalakShaNam.h | adhikamiti kriyAvisheShaNam.h |
bhavatvanyagataj~nAnAdiphalaprAptirdevAnAm.h | tatrApi tAratamye ko heturityata uktam.h- dravyeti ||
dravyANIndriyAdIni teShu svAtantyaM dravyasvAtantyaM vij~nAnaprayatnau dharmAdyutpAnanimitte | adhikairiti sheShaH | chashabdo.anuktasamuchchayArthaH | madhyamairdravyasvAtantAdibhirmadhyamam.h | alpairalpamiti | teShvapi deveShu niravadhikadravyasvAtantyamattvAditi hishabdArthaH | phalanirNaya iti tatrApi prakaraNavisheShoktiH |
dravyasvAtantAdyatishayAtphalAtishaya ityuktasya vyAptiM darshayati- loke.apIti ||
etAdR^ishaguNairityadhikairdravyasvAtantAdibhiH samuditAyAM kR^iShau, yasyAdhikaM kShetrAdidravyasvAtantyaM, yasya chA.a.avApAdau j~nAnaprayatnAdhikyaM tasya phalAdhikyaM dR^ishyata ityarthaH | evaM madhyalpayorapyudAhatarvyam.h | anena svAtantyatAratamyenetyuktamupapAditaM bhavati |
prasaN^gAtpApAdiphalaM prerakANAmasurANAM tAratamyena bhavatItyAha- evaJNcheti ||
mahAprerakANAM mahadityAdItyarthaH | ashubheShvashubhanimittam.h | hishabdena svAtantyaM hetumAha | evamiti devadR^iShyAntam.h | asurANAM cheti sambandhaH |
prAgukte.athare.atra cha pramANAntaramAha- shubheti ||
yathAsaN^khayena shubhAshubhaphalam.h | yathAshaktIti krameNaivetyatra yuktiH | tasya vivaraNaM ye ye yathA prayojakAstathA tatheti | prerakA ityasya pUrvavachChaN^kAparihArashcha |
|| OM ArtvijyamityauDulomistasmai hi parikriyate OM || OM sahakAryantaravidhiH pakSheNa tR^itIyaM tadvato vidhyAdivat.h OM || evaM prapaJNchena pUrvapakShamuktvA siddhAntasUtratAtparyamAgamavAkyenAha- yadyapIti |
evamuktaprakAreNa yadyapi shubhAshubhebhyo j~nAnAdibhyo bhavatphalaM surANAM cha daityAnAM cha bhavatItyupapAditam.h | evaMcha tathA.api karturdevadattAderapi phalaM syAdeva | Agame.apyasyArthasya prakR^itatvAdyadyapItyAdi yujyate | etaduktaM bhavati | devAsurANAM shubhAshubhaphalamityetAvadabhyupagamyate pramitatvAt.h | teShAmeveti tu na kShamyate | kintu karturapi bhavatIti | kartuH phalAN^gIkAre yadu kiJNchemAH prajA iti sAvadhAraNashrutivirodha Atreyavachanavirodhashcha syAdityata uktam.h- mahaditi || devAdInAM mahatphalaM 
katarustvalpam.h | alpasya chasattvavivakShA bahulamupalabdheti bhAvaH |
kutaH kartuH phalAN^gIkAra ityata Aha- yathoditamita || shrutismR^itisadbhAvAdityarthaH | tAshcha bhAShyAdAvudAhR^itA draShyavyAH |
yuktamapyAha- tasmAditi ||

mano brahmetyupAsItetyevamAdiShu pratIkopAsaneShu saMshayaH kiM teShvapyAtmagrahaH kartavyo na veti | kiM tAvatprAptam.h | teShvapyAtmagraha eva yukttaH | kasmAt.h | brahmaNa AtmatvAt.h, pratIkAnAmapi brahmavikAratvAt.h brahmatve satyAtmatvopapatteriti | brUmaH | na pratIkeShvAtmamatiM badhnIyAt.h | nahi sa upAsakaH pratIkAni yattAnyAtmatvenAkalayet.h | yatpunarbrahmavikAratvAtpratIkAnAM brahmatvaM tatashchAtmatvamiti tadasat.h | pratIkAbhAvaprasaN^gAt.h | vikArasvarUpopamardena hi nAmAdijAtasya brahmatvamevAshritaM bhavati | svarUpopamarde cha nAmAdInAM kutaH pratIkasvarUpatvamAtmagraho vA | kiJNcha yathA ruchakasvastikayornetarAtmatvam.h | dvayorapi vikAratvAt.h | tathA pratIkAtmanorapi | suvarNAtmaneva brahmAtmanaikatve pratIkAbhAvaprasaN^gamavochAma | ato na pratIkeShvAtmadR^iShyiH kartavyeti dvitIyasUtrArthaH | 
tatra tAvatprathamasUtrasyApavyAkhyAnaM dUShayati- neti || 
atra pratipattirnAma pramitereva parasyAbhimatA | pratIkadasharnamityAshaN^kaya nirAkaraNAt.h | ato jIvatvena pratipattavyatvasya pratipAdakamiti, jIvatvasya pratipAdakamiti chaika evAtharH |
kuto netyataH padArthaj~nAnapUrvakatvAdvAkyArthaj~nAnasya prathamaM padArthaM nirAkaroti- Atmashabdamiti || 
svashabdAdeva prANabhR^ichcha noktta iti vedarADevAtmashabdaM hetuM kR^itvA jIvaM nyavArayadyatastasmAdAtmashabdodito viShNureva na chAparo jIva iti yojanA |
etadukttaM bhavati | bhavedayaM sUtrArtho yadyAtmashabdo jIvavAchI bhavet.h | na chaivam.h | sUtrakAravachanasAmarthyAdeva tasya tadvAchitvAbhAvAvagamAt.h | tathA hi | yasmindyauriti vAkyamudAhR^itya kimatra dyubhvAdyAyatanatvena pradhAnamuchyate uta jIvaH kiMvA paramAtmeti saMshaye pradhAnAdau prApte siddhAntitam.h | "dyubhvAdyAyatanaM svashabdAt.h' iti | svashabdAt.h "tamevaikaM jAnatha AtmAnam.h' iti dyubhvAdyAyatane AtmashabdashravaNAt.h dyubhvAdyAyatanaM paramAtmaiveti | tato "nAnumAnamatachChabdAt.h' iti pradhAnaM nirAkR^itya jIvanirAkaraNArthaM sUtritam.h | prANabhR^ichcheti | tatra chashabdo netyasya svashabdAditi hetoshchAnukarShaNArthaH | tatashchAtmashabdAjjIvo.api netyarthaH | yadevamAtmashabdaM hetuM kR^itvA jIvaM nivAritavAnsUtrakAraH, tadanyathA.anupapattyA jAnImaH sUtrakArasyAtmashabdo na jIvavAchItyabhipretamiti | tathAcha kathaM svAcharitaviruddhamidAnImAcharediti | 
etadeva vishadayati- yadIti ||
jIve.api vartata iti sUtrakR^ito.abhipretamiti sheShaH | tarhi kathaM sUtrakAro jIvamAtmashabdena vinivArayet.h | nahi gandhavattvena ghaTo nivArayituM shakyate | athavA yadyAtmashabdo jIve.api varteta tadA sa AtmashabdaH kathaM jIvaM nivArayet.h | pratyuta pratipAdayediti yojanA | 
AgamavAkyamapyatra paThati- Atmeti || 
anyAnna vadanti kuto yata AtmAdishabdAH pUrtivAchinastairanyairguNapUrNatA kvApyavasthAyAM na prAptA | yatkiJNchitpUrNatArthatve chAmukhyArthatApAta iti | Atmashabdo.apyAN^.hpUrvAttanotermanin.h pratyaye Tilope cha sati niShpannaH pUrNatAvachanaH | yadyasmAdevaM vacho.asti tasmAdapIti pUrveNaiva anvayaH | 
idAnIM vAkyArthaM dUShayati- yadIti || 
manyate(atra) tatra sUtre tadA tasmAt.h jIvAdAtmashabdaM kathaM nivArayati | kutra nivAritavAnityata ukttam.h- yukttita iti || 
jIvanirAkaraNayukttitvenokttatvAditi yAvat.h | 
idamukttaM bhavati | AtmashabdashravaNAt.h dyubhvAdyAyatanaM na jIva iti AtmashabdaM jIvanivAraNe hetuM vadatA sUtrakAreNAtmashabdo jIvAnnivArita iti gamyate | nAyaM puruSho viShANitvAditi yathA | nahi tatrasthena tannirAso yujyate | nAyaM 
gaurviShANitvAdityapi prasaN^gAt.h | prathamasUtre cha dyubhvAdyAyatanaM parameshvaro na jIva AtmashabdAdityAtmashabdasya parameshvare pravR^ittirabhyupagatA | anyathA tena tatsAdhanAnupapatteH | tatra yadi jIveshvarAvekameva tattvamiti sUtrakArasya mataM syAt.h | tadA tenAtmashabdastatraiva vartate, na vartate chetyukttaM bhavati | nacha vyAhataM sUtrakAro bhAShata iti yukttam.h | tasmAnna jIveshvaraikyaM tasya matamiti gamyata iti | 
upalakShaNaM chaitat.h | dyubhvAdyAyatanaM parameshvaro, na jIva iti, pratij~nAdvayaM cha vyAhatamityapi draShyavyam.h | 
sUtrAntaravirodhaM chAha- bhedasyeti || 
yadi jagatpatiH sUtrakAro jIveshvarayoraikyaM manyate tarhi kathaM sa eva "bhedavyapadeshAt.h' iti bhedasya vyapadeshaM cha "sthityadanAbhyAM cha' iti sthitiM chAdanaM cha satAtparyaM jIveshabhedaM dR^iDhayituM hetumAha | bhedasya prAgapi pratipAditatvAddarDhya ityukttam.h | atrApyanekapramANopanyAsAtsatAtparyamiti | 
na ko.apyayaM virodho.asti | paramArthato jIveshayorekatve.api hi vyAvahArikabhedo.asti tadapekShayA tAni sUtrANi | idaM tu paramArthApekShayeti vyavasthopapatterityAshayena shaN^kate- vyAvahAriketi || 
atra vyAvahArikashabdena bhrAntisiddho.abhipreyate | prAk.h prabodhAdityukttAnuvAdatvAt.h | jIveshvarabhedo bhrAntisiddha iti vadanpraShyavyaH | kimayameva bhedo bhrAntisiddhaH kiM vA bhedamAtramiti | nAdyaH | apasiddhAntAt.h | dvitIye doShamAha- kveti || 
bhrAnterabhrAntipUrvakatvAt.h | jIveshvarabhedasya bhrAntikalpitatve kvachitsatyo bhedo.aN^gIkartavyaH | kvAsau na kvApi | kutrApi bhedasya satyatvAN^gIkAre jIveshabhedAropo.api na sambhavatIti bhAvaH | 
syAdetat.h | nAstyeva ko.api bhedaH satyaH | tathA.api jIveshabhedabhrAntirupapadyate | bhrAntirhi saMskAramapekShyate | saMskArashcha j~nAnamAtram.h | ataH pUrvapUrvamasaMskArAduttarottarabhrAntyutpAdaH | anAdishchAyaM saMsAra iti | maivam.h | bhedamAtrasya mithyAtve pramite khalu tadbalAdeShA kalpanopapadyate | na chaivam.h | sarvo.api bhedo bhrAnta iti hi pratij~naiva tAvadvayahatA | dUre pramANopanyAsa ityAshayavAnsopapattikaM tAvatpR^ichChati- vyAvahArikamiti || 
bhedamAtramiti sheShaH | tiShThatu tAvadanyadityevArthaH | iti vikalpe tu pakShadvaite (dvaye)(dvaidhe) sambhavati kaM pakShamavalambya iti sheShaH | atra sarvatra vachanashabdena tadartho lakShyate | sarvo.api bhedo bhrAntikalpita iti vAkyArtho bhrAntikalpito.atha paramArtha iti prashnArthaH | 
AdyaM shaN^kate- yadIti ||

tasya vachanasyeti vartate | nirAkaroti- bheda iti ||

sarvo.api bhedo bhrAnta iti vAkyArthasya bhrAntatve bAdhyatve cha sarvasyApi bhedasya satyatA syAdityukttam.h | tatkuta ityatastadupapAdanAya vyAptiM tAvadAha- ekasyeti || yau dvAveva viruddhau tayormadhye ekasyAsatyatAyAM satyAmanyasya satyatA syAdeveti vyAptiH kena nivAryate | upAdhivyabhichArayorabhAvAnna kenApi | purovartinaH puruShatve.asati sthANutvameva bhavatIti niyamo nAsti | valmIkatvasyApi sambhavAt.h | ato dvayoreva viruddhayorityukttam.h | dvayoriti visheShaNasyAsamarthatAparihArAya viruddhagrahaNam.h | yaH padArtho dvayoreva viruddhayorekasya asatyatvavAn.h asAvanyasya satyatvavAnityukttaM bhavati | 
nidarshanamAha- anityamiti || 
AptenoktamasatyaM netyuktte satyukttaM satyamiti prajA jAnanti | tathA vipralambhakenokttaM satyaM no ityuktte tu tasyAsatyatAmapi jAnanti | satyatvAsatyatvayordvayoreva viruddhatA | tatra Aptoktte.arthe.asatyatAyAmasatyAM satyatAyAH satvamanAptoktte cha satyatAyAmasatyAmasatyatAyAH satvaM cha prasiddhamityarthaH | ityuktta iti pramitatvopalakShaNam.h | prajA jAnantItyanena 
A.avipAlAN^ganameShA vyAptiH siddhA na kevalaM parIkShakANAmiti sUchayati |

tatkiM dvayamapi satyamityata Aha- tatreti || 
tatra ghaTatadabhAvayormadhye | yadA.abhAvasyAsatyatA tadA ghaTaH satya eva | yadA cha ghaTasya asatyatA tadA.abhAvaH satya evetyatharH | tasmAnna vyAptibhaN^ga iti hishabdArthaH | kuto na dvayamapi mithyetyata Aha- bhAveti || 
yo yasyAbhAvo yashcha yasyAbhAvasya pratiyogI tAvubhAvapyekatraikadaiva na mithyeti vyApteH | svapne.api ghaTatadabhAvau kathaM tathA bhaviShyata iti bhAvaH | vyAhataM cha bhAvAbhAvayorubhayorasattvavarNanamityAshayenAha- bhAvasya hIti || 
hishabdo hetau | bhAvasya niShedhe kR^ite tu abhAvasyaiva vihitatvAt.h | punarnAbhAvasya niShedhanaM kartuM shakyate vyAghAtAt.h | evamabhAvasya niShedhe kR^ite.abhAvAbhAvo bhAva eva tadvayapto veti bhAvasya vihitatvAt.h punarna bhAvasya niShedhanaM yukttaM vyAhatatvAditi | astvevaM vyAptistataH kimityata Aha- svavacha iti ||
svashabdena prativAdyuchyate | tadvAgarthasya sakalabhedamithyAtvasya | tasmAt.h vyAptisadbhAvAt.h mithyAtvaM satyatvaM cha dvau viruddhadharmau | bhede tayoH, mithyAtve.asati satyatvaM satsyAdevokttavyAptibalAdityarthaH | 
prakR^itamupasaMharati- tasmAditi ||

evaM prathamasUtrasyApavyAkhyAM pratyAkhyAya dvitIyasyApi pratyAkhyAti- etasmAditi ||

tat.h tasmAtpUrvasUtragatasyAtmashabdasya paramAtmavAchitvAnna pratIka iti pratij~nAvAkyasya pratIkaviShayatvena viShNudR^iShTiH kartavyA na bhavedityevArthaH | idamukttaM bhavati | na pratIka ityatra tAvadAtmetItyanuvartanIyaM pUrvasUtrAt.h | anyathA pratij~nAvAkyasyAparipUrNatvAt.h | pUrvasUtre chAtmashabdo viShNuviShaya iti samarthitam.h | tathAcha pratIkaviShayAyA viShNudR^iShyerevAyaM pratiShedho vyAkhyeyaH | na pratIkeShu jIvamatiM badhnIyAditi tu pratij~nAvyAkhyAne prakR^itaparityAgo.aprakR^itasvIkArashcha prasajyeyAtAmiti | 
mano brahmetyAdishrutyarthatvena yatpratIkasaMsthitatvenetyukttam.h | tadapi notsUtra(trita)m.h | kintu pratIka iti saptamyantaM padamAvartate | tatrAdyaM viShayasaptamyantaM netyanena sambaddhayate | dvitIyamadhikaraNasaptamyantaM shrutivyAkhyAnam.h | ubhayatrAtmetIti padadvayaM pUvarsUtrAdanuvartata ityAshayavAnprasaN^gAd.h dvitIyaM vyAkhyAti- pratIka iti || 
yasmAtpratIkaviShayatvena viShNudR^iShyiH kartavyA na bhavettasmAditi shrutyartha iti sheShaH | hishabdena prathamAdivibhaktteH saptamyarthavAchitvaM shAbdikAnAM prasiddhamiti dyotayati |
itashcha nAyaM pratij~nArtha ityAha- nacheti ||
yasmAdviShNuH pratIkaM, chashabdAjjIvasya na bhavati, tasmAtpratIkeShvAtmeti jIva ityupAsanA na prasakteti sheShaH | ayamarthaH | prAptau satyAM hi pratiShedho vakttavyaH | nacha pratIkeShUpAsakasya AtmadR^iShyiH prasakttA prasaJNjakAbhAvAt.h | yattu prasaJNjakamukttaM brahmaNa AtmatvaM pratIkAnAM cha brahmavikAratvaM tadubhayamaprAmANikaM pramANaviruddhaM cha | na hyatyantAbhAsena prasakttirbhavati | atiprasaN^gAt.h | tataH prasaktayabhAvAtpratiShedho.anarthaka iti | 
nahi sa iti hetuvyAkhyAnaM dUShayati- nacha viShNuH pratIkaM yattasmAditi ||  tachChabdo hi prakR^itaparAmarshe vartate prakR^itashchAtmA | Atmashabdashcha viShNuvAchyeveti samarthitam.h | tathAcha hi yasmAtsa viShNuH pratIkaM naiva tasmAdityevArthaH sampadyate | nahi sa upAsakaH pratIkAnIti vyAkhyAne tu prakR^itaparityAgenAprakR^itaparAmarshaH prasajyata iti |

nAtmetyupAsanetyekadeshotkIrtanena "na pratIke na hi saH' iti samagrasUtrArthamanuvadati | pratIkeShvAtmeti jIva ityupAsanA na kAryA | nahi sa upAsakaH pratIkAni iti pakSho yadA ityevaM pUrvasUtravyAkhyAnaM yadA tadA.atra pratIkeShu brahmadR^iShyishcha viruddhayate | chashabdo.apavyAkhyAnanirAsasamuchchaye | 
etadvivR^iNoti- sa iti ||
pratIkAnAmAtmatvenopAsanasyAkartavyatve tvayA yA tAdAtmyAbhAvalakShaNA sa neti yukttirabhihitA sA tatrApi brahmapratIkayorapi sameti hetoH pratIkeShu brahmadR^iShyiH kartavyeti sUtre vyAkhyAyamAne sati ukttayukttiviruddhatA bhavatIti | etadukttaM bhavati | pratIkeShu brahmadR^iShyiH kartavyeti sUtravyAkhyAnamasat.h | pratIkaM brahmatayA nopAsyam.h | abrahmatvAt.h | yadyanna bhavati na tattatvenopAsyamiti yukttiviruddhatvAt.h | na cheyaM yukttirapramA | pratIkAnAmAtmatvenopAsanasya akartavyatAyAM pUrvasUtre pareNaivopanyastatvAt.h | anyathA.anaikAntyena sAdhikA na syAt.h | nacha brahmapratIkayorabhedaH brahmaNaH satyatvAt.h pratIkAnAM kalpitatvAt.h | pAramArthikabhedAbhAvaH tAvadastIti chet.h | tarhi jIvapratIkayorapi sa nAstItyasiddhiH syAditi | 
syAdetat.h | "nahi saH' iti na nirvisheShaNo hetuH sUtrakArasyAbhi(preto)mato yena brahmadR^iShyiH pratIkeShUkttayukttiviruddhA syAt.h  | kiM tUpAsyasyotkarShaprAptyabhAve satItyanena vishiShyaH | pratIkAnAM brahmatvenopAsane tUtkarShaprAptirasti | ato.atadbhAve.apyupAsanA (kAryA)yujyata ityata Aha- yadIti || 
Adye.apishabdo.atiprasaN^gasamuchchayArthaH | hishabdasyottarArdhenAnvayaH | yadi vishiShyahetuM vyAkhyAya pratIkAnAmatadbhAve.abrahmatve.apyutkarShaprAptimAtreNa brahmatvenopAsanA.aN^gIkriyate | tadA AtmatvenApi tadupAsanamaN^gIkAryaM natu nirAkAryam.h | kuta ityata Aha- utkarSha iti || 
yasmAdbrahmavadAtmano.api pratIkAdutkarSho.asti | katham.h | AtmanashchetanatvAt.h | achetanaM khalu pratIkam.h | tasyAtmatvenopAsanAyAmutkarShapraptiH syAditi | atiprasaN^gasya viparyayapayarvasAnamAha- tasmAditi || 
yasmAdvishiShyahetau vyAkhyAyamAne pUrvasUtre.asiddhiH syAt.h | tata eva pratIkeShu brahmopAsanavadAtmopAsanaM cha prasajyeta | tasmAt.h, atattvaM, yadyanna bhavati tattatvena nopAsyamiti sAmAnyameva sUtrakArasyAbhimatam.h | natu visheShaNaprakShepaH | tathAcha brahmadR^iShyiriti pratij~nA svokttayukttiviruddhaiveti | atra vyApternirvisheShaNatvAbhidhAnasya hetornirvisheShaNatva eva tAtparyam.h | spaShyatvArthaM tu vyAptyabhidhAnamiti vAchyam.h | 
pratij~nAvyAkhyAnamapAkR^itya utkarShAditi hetuvyAkhyAnamapAkaroti- utkarShAditi || 
brahmatAdhyAne pratIkAnAmutkarShAdutkarShasya dR^iShyatvAdaJNjasA phalaM puruShArtharUpaM phalaM yadi syAttadA, tadeva brahmaNo nIchatAdhyAnamiti, tasmAdanarthaH kiM na jAyate, jAyata eveti samavyayaphalatvAdakAryamevedamiti | 
्rabhyupagamyedaM samavyayaphalatvamukttam.h | vastutastu na puruShArthaH kiM tvanartha evetyAha- achetanasyeti || 
tuShyayabhAvAchcha na puuruShArthalAbhastataH | kvachidityanena yadachetanaM tadupachikIrShAlakShaNatuShyirahitamiti vyAptiM sUchayati | nIchasya pratIkasya svAtmatAdhyAnAdbrahma kupyati | tatashchAnatharM prayachChati | tatra dR^iShyAnto lokavaditi | yathA loke shilAdikaM rAjatvAdinA chintitaM na prasIdati nApi puruShArthaM prayachChati | yathA cha rAjA chaNDAlatvena dhyAtaH kupyati anarthaM cha dadAti tathetyarthaH | anena pratIkAnAmachetanatve.api brahmaiva savarAdhyakShatvAtphalaM dAsyatIti cha pratyukttam.h | tasyAnenopAsanena kupitatvAt.h | 
na vayaM brahmaNi pratIkatvopAsanaM brUmaH | yena brahma kupitamanarthaM prayachChet.h kintu pratIke brahmatvopAsanam.h | tataH puruShArthaprAptirityata Aha- chaNDAla iti || 
chaNDAlamuddishya chaNDAlo nR^ipa ityuktte tathA nR^ipamuddishya nR^ipashchaNDAla ityuktte nR^ipeNa parij~nAte satyanarthaprAptau kathaJNchana ko visheShaH syAnna kathaJNchitko.api | atrokttashabdena dhyAnamupalakShyate | aj~nAtopAsano rAjA nAnarthaM karotIti nR^ipeNa parij~nAta ityukttam.h | tathAcha pratIkaM brahmetyupAsane brahma pratIkamityupAsane cha sama evAnartha iti vAkyasheShaH |

etadukttaM bhavati | bhavedayaM parihAro yadi pratIka(sya) svarUpopamardena tasya brahmatvamupAsyamiti pakShaH syAt.h | na chaivam.h | pratIkAbhAvaprasaN^gasya pareNaivokttatvAt.h | bhedAbhedAbhiprAyeNAyaM parihAra ityapi nAsti | nahi ghaTo mR^idabhinno mR^idghaTAdbhinneti bhedAbhedau kinnAma parasparam.h | tasmAdanupamarditasvarUpasya pratIkasya brahmatve dhyAte brahmaNo.api pratIkatvaM dhyAtameveti yukttamukttamiti |

dvitIyapAdapratipAdyapradarshanaparaM bhAShyaM "devAnAM mokSha utkrAntishchAsminpAda uchyate' iti | tatra devAnAmityetadyadi mokShotkrAntibhyAM sambaddhayate tadA devebhyo.anyeShAM sasharIrANAmevAvasthAnamiti prApnoti | anyatra vA tachCharIraparityAgaprakArashchintanIyaH | achintane vA kAraNaM vAchyam.h | yadi cha mokSheNaiva sambaddhayate tadA devAnAM mokSha itareShAmutkrAntishchetyukttaM bhavati | mokShashcha prakaraNavashAddehAditi gamyate | tathAcha prathamapAde karmanAshAkhyaM phalamasminpAde uchyata iti yathA sAmAnyenokttaM tathA.atrApyutkrAntirasminpAda uchyata iti vakttavyam.h | kimanena vibhAge(netya)na kR^itaM syAdityata Aha- devAnAM cheti ||

nArAyaNamatishcha samyaktave.api parA guNebhya iti sheShaH | tatra pUrvavadeva hetuH | tataH shriyo.apyatishayena mahAshuddhachitiH | vishiShyanta iti visheShAH padArthAH | asheShANAmurUNAmanantAnAM visheShANAM dR^ishirviShayIkAriNI | atispaShyatayA.asheShapadArthaviShayetyetadapi bahulA chAtivishadetivadvayAkhyeyam.h | dR^ishiH sAkShAtkAra iti vA | nityamekaprakAretyutpattivinAsharahitetyayamapi guNAtItatve hetuH | kechidekameveshvaraj~nAnamityAsthitAH | apare tvanekAnIti | tadvivekArthamukttaM nirantarA nirbhedeti | tarhi kiM teShu teShu padArtheShu j~nAteShu vikriyate netyAha- nityamavikAriNyeveti | kathaM tarhi tattadviShayIkaraNamityata ukttam.h- sUryeti || yathA sUryaprabhA svayaM nirvikArA.api tAMstAnprAptAnviShayAnprakAshayati tatheyamapItyarthaH | atra cha visheSha eva nivarAhakaH | ata evaiketyanuktavA nirantaretyukttam.h | nirlepA vItadoShA cheti shuddhatvavyAkhyAnam.h | lepaH karmasambandhaH | mahachChabdavyAkhyAnaM pUrvavat.h | yadvA nityameveti tadarthamatrApi yojyam.h | parA svatantretyatishabdasya vyAkhyAtatvenApi vyAkhyeyam.h | ata eva tattantratvAchcheti vakShyati | 
etAni visheShaNAni lakShmImAne.apyatidishati- visheShAnIti || 
tadgatAnbhagavadgatAMstAni lakShaNAni yasyAH sA tathokttA | shriyo matiH pratipattavyeti sheShaH | bhagavadgatAsheShavisheShaviShayIkAritvaM vihAyAnyadharmavatI j~nAtavyetyarthaH | prAya ityukttasya tAtparyamAha- tathaiveti ||

lakShmImativisheShaNAni mukttabrahmamatAvatidishati- brahmaNastviti || 
brahmaNastu matiH shriyo yathaivaM prAyaH | tathA vaishadyAdyabhAvAtprAya ityukttam.h | kevalamityuktayabhAvAchcha | ata eva tatra tadukttam.h | brahmaNa iti vishiShyAbhidhAne ko heturityata Aha- mukttAnAM tviti || 
visheShabalena vR^iddhihrAsavatItyarthaH | yathokttaM avR^iddhihrAsarUpatvamityAdi | mukttagrahaNasya tAtparyamAha- agnIti ||
agnijvAlAyA agneriva saMsAriNAM dR^isho.antaHkaraNAdbhava utpattireva syAnna tu vyakttimAtram.h | 
bhavatvevaM j~nAnAnAM guNanimittaM nAnAvidhatvam.h | prakR^ite tu kimityata Aha- evaMvidheShviti || 
j~nAneShvevaMvidheShu satsu muShyadR^iShyayo.apahR^itasamyagj~nAnAH | samyagj~nAnAbhAve.anyathAdR^iktavamapi nopapadyate | adhiShThAnasAmAnyaj~nAnasya bhrAntyupayogitvAdityata ukttam.h- khadyoteti || 
yathA.andhatamase khadyotA api bhayahetavastathA viparyayabahulamalpaM samyagj~nAnamapi tAmasameva | yathokttam.h | atattvArthavadalpaM cheti | nAnAmatasamAshrayAnnAnA vadantIti yojanA | j~nAnAnAM guNavashAdanekavidhatvopapattestamasA.a.avR^ittA vAdinaH 
pramANAvadhIraNAtsamyagj~nAnavikalA AbhAsAdaraNAdadhiShThAnasAmAnyaj~nAnavattvAchcha viparItaj~nAnino mokShaM nAnAvidhamAchakShata ityarthaH | kAraNaikatvAnmithyAj~nAnenApyekavidhena bhAvyamiti chenna | sahakArivaichityAdvaichityopapatteH | tadidamukttam.h- nAnAmatamAshrayAditi || matAnAM cha pravAheNAnAditvamukttam.h | mUlakAraNe tamoguNe.api vaichityAchcha | ata evokttam.h- guNabhedata iti ||
samadhigatametat.h nAnAvidheShu mokShavAdeShvekaH pramANamUlo.anye mithyAj~nAnamUlA iti | natu visheSho.ataH punaH saMshaya evetyata paramatAnAM sarveShAM heyatvaM didarshayiShurAdau tAvajjinoditaM mokShasvarUpamanuvadati- Ashrityeti ||

chashabdo.anukttasamuchchayArthaH | tena vipratipanneti pratij~nAyAM siddhayati | hetau cha chetanAshriteti | tenAchetanagatau bAdho, devadattagatau siddhArthatvaM, achetanagatau vyabhichArashcha na sambhavati | duHkhenetA prAptA duHkhetA | prAptishcha na sAdhyasAdhanabhAvalakShaNA | tathA sati devadattasya sukhArthAyAM mandagatau vyabhichArApAtAt.h | dUratvasya chAniyatatvAt.h | tIvratvasyApyapariniShThitatvAt.h | kiM tarhi samAnakAlInena duHkhena sahaikAdhikaraNatvalakShaNA | kadAchiddevadattaH duHkhena vinApi gachChati tatra vyabhichAra iti chenna | devadattasya kadA.api nirduHkhatAyA anaN^gIkArAt.h | AdhyAtmikAdiShvanyatamena mahatA.alpena vA.ayaM khalu sadA saMvalitaH | chetanashabdena jAgrato.abhidhAnAnna suptagatau vyabhichAraH | sukhArthA.api gatiralpaM duHkhamutpAdayatItyabhyupagamya duHkhasAdhanatvaM vA sAdhyam.h | laukikI devadattAdigatiH | iti cha pratyanumAne kenachiduktte, ekaM cha tachCharaNaM chaikasharaNaM anumAnamekasharaNaM yasyAsau tathokttaH | anyathA pUrvakAlaiketyekashabdasya pUrvanipAtaH syAt.h | pratyanumAnasyottaraM shaN^kate- anUrdhveti ||
tatra devadattagaterduHkhatatve.anUrdhvatAvishiShyaM gatitvaM prayojakaM na gatitvamAtramiti yadi brUyAdityarthaH | pakShetaro.ayaM kasmAchChaN^kita iti che(t.h)nna | lakShaNasampattau tadupAdhitvasyoktatvAt.h | nirAkaroti- khagasyeti || 
tadA vadAma ityAdAvupaskartavyam.h | khagasya pArAvatAderdUrodhvargamane cha duHkhamastIti hetoH sa upAdhiH sAdhyAnugaH sAdhyavyApako na bhavatItyato.anupAdhiH | idamukttaM bhavati | kimayaM kevalasAdhyavyApako.abhimataH kiM vA sAdhanAvachChinnasAdhyavyApakaH | na prathamaH | adharme sAdhyasadbhAve.apyanUrdhvatAvishiShyagatitvasyAbhAvena sAdhyAvyApakatvAt.h | na dvitIyaH | khagasya dUrordhvagatau gatitvAvachChinne duHkhetatve satyapyanUdhvargatitvasyAbhAvAt.h | anenordhvagatitvAbhAvo.anUrdhvagatitvaM kevalasAdhye upAdhirityapi prayukttamiti | dUragrahaNaM khagasya duHkhaM vyaJNjayitum.h | tadA hi tasminduHkhakAryANi dR^ishyante | pratyAgamanasamayavartiduHkhakAryANi tAnIti chenna | UrdhvaM gachChatyeva taddarshanAt.h | 
mA bhUdayamupAdhiH sharIravR^ittitvaM tu bhaviShyati | devadattagatau yad.hduHkhetattvaM tatra na gatitvaM prayojakaM kiM nAma sharIravR^ittitvam.h | na chedaM sAdhyAvyApakam.h | yad.hduHkhetaM tachCharIrivR^ittItyasya vyabhichArAdarshanAdityataH sarvopAdhisAdhAraNaM dUShaNamAha- pratisAdhaneti ||

tatrAnekeShvAtmasu yasyAtmanastu shUnyaikarasatAj~nAnAchChUnyAdvitIyatAj~nAnAtsA saMvR^itirapagachChati mUlasaMvR^itirvyAvR^ittA bhavati | anyA nashyati | sa pudgalatvAtkartR^itvAdirUpAnnirmuktto mahAshUnyatvameShyatIva | yastu saMvR^ityA.avachChinna AtmA sa pudgalabhAvena duHkhAnyalaM paramArthabuddhayaivAnubhavati | iti prAhuriti sambandhaH |

ekajIvatvavAdino bahujIvamatAshcheti dvividhamAyinashchaivaM dvividhashUnyavAdivadeva mokShasvarUpamAhuH | eko jIvo yasmiMlloke sa tathokttastasya bhAvastattvaM tadvadantItyekajIvatvavAdinaH | bahavo jIvA yasmiMstattathokttaM bahujIvamataM yeShAM te bahujIvamatAH | 
nanu shUnyavAdinaH saMvR^itinibandhanaH saMsArastannivR^ittishcha mokSha ityAchakShate | mAyAvAdinastu mAyAhetuko.ayaM saMsArastannivR^ittishcha mokSha iti | ato vaiShamyamityata Aha- mAyeti || 
yA shUnyavAdyabhyupagatA saMvR^itiH saiva teShAM mAyinAM mAyA | anAdyanirvAchyatvalakShaNasya AvaraNavikShepAdeH kAryasya chaikatvAditi bhAvaH | shUnyavAdinaH shUnyaM tattvamAhurmAyAvAdinastu brahma | ato.asti vaiShamyamityata Aha- nirvisheShatveti || 
shUnyaM brahmeti chaitayorbhidA no vidyate | kutaH nirvisheShatvasya vAchaiva dvAbhyAM dvayornirvisheShatvenokttatvAt.h | vaidharmyaM khalu vastuno bhedakam.h | tachchAtra nAstIti dvayorapi sammatam.h | ataH shabdabhedamAtraM na vastubheda iti |
atha matam.h | satyaM j~nAnamanantaM brahma vij~nAnamAnandaM brahmaiveti shrutyaiva satyAdilakShaNaM brahma sarvato vyAvartitaM tatkathaM shUnyaM brahmeti no bhidetyuchyate iti | satyam.h | sadAdilakShaNairbrahma shrutyA sarvato vyAvartitamiti | tattu mAyAvAdimate nopapadyata ityAshayavAnAha- saditi || 
sadAdikaM cha kimeva na kimapItyarthaH | tathAhi | sadAdikaM kiM brahmasvarUpamutAnyat.h | Adye na lakShyalakShaNabhAvaH | anekapadavaiyarthyaM cha | na dvitIyaH | akhaNDavAditvAt.h | yathA bhavatAM satyatvAdikaM brahmasvarUpamapi tallakShaNaM tathA mamApi kiM na syAditi chenna | asmAbhiH visheShashaktayA tannirvAhAN^gIkArAt.h | pareNa tu kuto nirvAhyametat.h | mayApi visheSho.aN^gIkriyata iti chet.h | na | akhaNDavAditvAt.h | 
yadyapi satyAdipadapratipAdyavastuni na bhedaH | tathA.api vyAvartyAnAmasattvAdInAmastyeva atastadvayAvR^ittiprayojanAni tadvAchIni vA.anekAni padAni brahmaNi vartanta ityabhyupagamAtkathamasmanmate shrutyarthAnirvAha ityata Aha- vyAvartyeti || 
vyAvartyamAtrabhedastvityekadeshotkIrtanena sakalamapyukttamupalakShayati | eShA prakriyA samastA shUnyavAdino.api mate.astyevAto naitayA.api brahmashUnyayorbhedo vakttuM shakyate | shUnyavAdino.api vidyata iti kimApAdanenochyate | netyAha- anR^itAderiti ||

kiM chaivaMvidhaM vedaprAmANyaM shUnyavAdinA.apyaN^gIkR^itameveti kuto.ayaM visheShaH | na sarvasyApi vedasya mAyAvAdinA.atattvAvedakatvamuchyate | kiM nAma vidhipratiShedhaviShayasya | advitIyaM tattvaM pratipAdayatastattvamasItyAdermahAvAkyasya nirvisheShaM sachchidAnandAtmakaM tatpadArthaM pratipAdayato "yattadadreshyamagrAhyam.h' "satyaM j~nAnam.h' ityAderavAntaravAkyasya cha tattvAvedakatvamaN^gIkriyata eva, na chaivaM shUnyavAdinA, ityataH kathaM sAmyamityataH shUnyavAdinA.apyevamevAN^gIkriyate | tattvAvedakatvaM hi na viShayavisaMvAdAbhAvAtirikttaM kiJNchidasti | vAkyadvayArthasya chAvisaMvAdaH shUnyavAdinA.apyaN^gI(kR^ita)kriyata evetyAshayavAnmahAvAkyArthAN^gIkAraM tAvaddarshayati- nirbhedatvaM tviti ||

kiJNchokttarUpe shUnyavAdimayAvAdibhyAmutprekShite mokShe na kiJNchitpramANamasti | tathAhi | na tAvadatra pratyakShaM pramANam.h | pratyakShAviShayatvAdasyAtharsya | nApyAgamaH | vedAdyAgamasya shUnyavAdinA pramANatvenAnabhyupagamAt.h | tadIyAgamasyAsmAbhiranaN^gIkR^itatvAt.h | mAyAvAdinaM prati tu vakShyAmaH | tasmAdAtmashUnyatA puruShArtho duHkhanivR^ittyupayogitvAchCharIrAdishUnyatAvadityanumAnameva vakttavyam.h | yathoktam.h | "na tairvinA duHkhaheturAtmA chette.api tAdR^ishAH | nirdoShaM dvayamapyevaM vairAgyaM cha dvayostataH' iti | tadidaM satpratipakShatayA nAnumAnamityAha- na mokSha iti || 
vimataH shUnyabhAvo brahmabhAvo vA na mokSha iti pratij~nA | yasmAdadeha iti hetuH adehatvAditi | ghaTashUnyatA yatheti dR^iShyAntaH | yo.anumAmAtramAnakaH sa ityuktte kiM vadedityanenokttavidhayA pramANAntarAbhAvaM tata eva svAnumAnasyAbAdhitaviShayatvaM cha sUchayati | 
atrAnumAnaviShaye shrutimAlambya dUShaNaM na vadet.h | tathA.atra svAbhimate mokShe shrutiM pramANaM naiva vadedityarthaH | kuta ityata Aha- pUrveti ||
tasya mAyAvAdino mate shruteramAnatvAt.h | katham.h | "prAmANyAdi cha vedasya' ityAdinA pUrvokttenaiva vartmanA | nanu na sarvo vedo.atattvAvedakaH kintu vidhiniShedhAtmaka eva | atathAbhUtAstu vedAntAstattvAvedakA iti chenna | sarvadhamarojkhitasyAsya kiM  shAstreNAdhigamyata ityAdinA pUrvokttenaiva vartmanA.atra tattve shruteramAnatvAt.h | 
astu vA kathaJNchit.h shrutiH pramANam.h | tathA.api nAsmadanumAnasya tadbAdha ityAha- na cheti || 
mukttAviti sheShaH | tathA tadabhimatamokShavAdinItyapi grAhyam.h | "asharIraM vAva santaM na priyApriye spR^ishataH' ityAdishrutisadbhAvAtkathamadehatvavAdinI shrutirnAstItyuchyata ityata Aha- adehatvamiti || 
yadasyAM shrutAvadehatvamuchyate tatprAkR^itasharIrarAhityameva | natu sarvathA.apyadehatvam.h | prAkR^itashabdena jaDamupalakShyate | tadrAhityaM cha chaturthapAdoditaprakAreNa j~nAtavyam.h | evaM "brahma veda brahmaiva bhavati' ityAdishrutirAshaN^kaya vyAkhyAtavyA cha | 
asharIratvashruteH kuto.arthasaN^kochaH kriyata ityata Aha- mokSha iti ||
"sa tatra paryeti jakShankrIDanramamANaH strIbhirvA yAnairvA j~nAtibhirvA.aj~nAtibhirvA' iti shrutirmokShe stAdibhogaM brUte | na chAsharIrasyAsau sambhavatItyataH saN^kocha ityarthaH | 
tachChUnyatvaM brahmatvaM vA mokSho na bhavati nirduHkhatvAt.h pratipannaM ghaTashUnyatvaM yatheti chAnumAyAH kiM dUShaNaM syAnna kimapi | shUnyashabdena tadaN^gIkAravAn.h lakShyate | shU(nyaM cha mA)nyashcha mAyI cheti dvandvaH | yadvA shUnyaM cha mAyA cheti dvandvaH | te vidyete yayoriti vrIhyAdilakShaNa iniH | tatra cha tadantavidhiriShyate | 
pratipakShAntaramAha- duHkhamiti | 
mokSha iti shUnyaM brahma chochyate | prativAdibhyAM tathA.abhyupagatatvAt.h | sa mokSho duHkhAtmA syAt.h duHkhAdabhinnatvAt.h | duHkhapratiyogikabheda(rahitatvA)shUnyatvAtprasiddhaduHkhavat.h ityarthaH | shUnyabrahmaNorduHkhatve tadbhAvApattirna puruShArtha iti siddhayati | apishabdaH pratipakShAntarasamuchchayArthaH | asaMshayamiti vyApternishchitatvamAchaShye | 
duHkhapratiyogikabhedAbhAvaH kuta ityata Aha- bheda iti || 
duHkhAt.h shUnyabrahmaNoriti sheShaH | tathA chApasiddhAnta iti bhAvaH | 
kiJNcha duHkhApAyasyAtmanAshena vinA dehAdinAshenApi sambhavAdanyathAsiddhishcha anumAnasya | sharIrAdishUnyatA.api na duHkhadhvaMsopayogitvAtpuruShArthaH | kiM nAmAtmano nirduHkhatAM prati hetutvAt.h | nahi duHkhaM nashyatviti kashchidAshAste | api tarhi nirduHkhaH syAmiti | 
nanu shUnyabhAvo brahmabhAvo vA bhavatAM siddhashchedapasiddhAntaH, na chedAshrayAsiddhiriti chenna | parAnumAne.apyAtmashUnyatAyA asiddhatvenAshrayAsiddheH | iyAMstu visheShaH | yatparaprasiddhimAtreNa pratipakShaH sambhavatIti | 
nanu bhogashrutiH saguNamukttiviShayAstviti chenna | "paraM jyotirupasampadya svena rUpeNAbhiniShpadyate' ityukttavirodhAt.h | nirduHkhatvAnmokSho na bhavatIti viruddhamiti chet.h | parameShyasya Atmano nAshaH puruShArtha iti kathaM na viruddham.h |
्raiatha sato duHkhAdbhede sad.hdvaitatA syAt.h | duHkhaM tu mithyeti chenna | anubhavavirodhAderukttatvAt.h | 
bahujIvavAdinaM prati nAntimAnumAnamiti na kuchodyAvakAshaH | 
tadetatsarvamabhisaN^ghAyopasaMharati- ityAdIti ||
sahaiveti sambandhaH | 
vij~nAnavAdyabhimataM mokShasvarUpamapyukttadoSheNAtidishati- evamiti ||
shUnyavAdimAyAvAdyabhimatamokShavadvij~nAnavAdyabhipreto.api mokSho heya ityarthaH | nanu vij~nAnavAdino vij~nAnaM tattvamAhuH tasyApi kShaNikatvaM svakarmakaprakAshakatvalakShaNaM svaprakAshatvaM cha | nachaivaM pUrvakAvityato vaiShamyAtkathamatidesha ityata Aha- j~nAneti ||
j~nAnamAtraM chAsau visheShashcha j~nAnamAtravisheShaH | tamiti dvitIyArthe tasiH | yasmAtj~nAnamAtravisheShaM tasya j~nAnasya bhaN^guratvAdivisheShamapyapahAya vij~nAnavAdo.apyadvaitatAmataM j~nAtavyam.h | na vidyate dvaitaM yasya tattvasya tadadvaitaM tasya bhAvo.advaitatA | tasyA matamadvaitatAmatam.h | tataH kAraNAdukttadoSho.api samo bhavet.h | 
idamukttaM bhavati | astu vij~nAnavAdasya pUrvasmAtkashchidvisheShaH | tathA.api sa prakR^itAnupayogitvAnnAdaraNIyaH | mokShasvarUpaM tu prakR^itaM samAnam.h | pratipannaM jIvabhAvaM vihAyAdvitIyavij~nAnatvApattirmukttiriti vij~nAnavAdinA.apyaN^gIkR^itatvAt.h | ato yuktta evAtidesha iti | yadvA j~nAnamAtravisheShaM tasya bhaN^guratvAdivisheShaM chApahAya vij~nAnavAdo.api sAkShAdadvaitatAmataM j~nAtavya ityanenedamabhipraiti | na kashchidvij~nAnavAdasya pUvarAbhyAM visheShaH | j~nAnamiti visheShasya shabdamAtratvena heyatvAt.h | na hi j~nAnatvaM nAma dharmo.abhyupagamyate pareNa | bhaN^guratvAdikaM tu tenaiva kalpitamityukttatvAddheyameva | natu vastuto matabhedahetuH | yathokttaM "tatra santatibhedashcha' ityAdi | ato yuktto.atidesha iti | atideshaprakArastu spaShya eva | 
anumAnAntaramapi tannirAsArthamAha- kAla iti ||
mokShakAlo.advitIyaj~nAnavAnna bhavatItyarthaH | pratipannavadvartamAnakAlavat.h | rodhAdvirodhAt.h | tAdR^ik.h mokSharUpaM yasyAtmano.asau tAdR^iN^mokSharUpastasya bhAvastattA | j~nAnAtirikttasya kalpitatvAdvartamAnakAlo.api kevalaj~nAnIti chenna | mukttisaMsArayoravisheShApatteH | yastu visheSho.aN^gIkriyate tadabhAva evAnena sAdhyate | 
j~nAnavyatirikttaM kimapi nAstIti mate kAlo.api nAstyeva | ataH kimAshrayA.anumAnapravR^ittirityata Aha- yadIti || 
Aha vij~nAnavAdI | tadA kadA kAlo neti prashne pareNa kR^ite sati kimutaramasau vakShyati | niradhikaraNasyAbhAvasya nirUpayitumashakyatvAtkAlo netyetadapi durnirUpamApadyetetyarthaH | mokShAvasthAyAM kAlo netyuttaraM vakShyAmItyAshaN^kyAha- yadeti ||
vadetkAlAbhAvAdhikaraNatveneti sheShaH | tarhi sA mokShAvasthA pUrvAnumAne pakShatAM vrajet.h | pakShashabdena tadekadesho dharmI lakShyate | mokShAvasthA na kevalaj~nAnavatIti pratij~nAsyata ityarthaH | 
evaM tarhi kAlatvAditi hetuH svarUpAsiddhaH syAdityata Aha- avasthAtvAditi || 
yadA.avasthA pakShIkriyate tadA.avasthAtvAdityeva hi heturuchyate na kAlatvAdityato nokttadoShaH | 
evaM saMsArAvasthaiva dR^iShyAntIkriyata iti na dR^iShyAntadoSho.apIti vAchyam.h | prathamokttapakShahetudR^iShyAntAnAM tyAge pratij~nAhAniH syAditi chet.h | maivam.h | kAlAbhAvasyAvasthAmadhikaraNaM vadatA na kiJNchidAtmahitamAcharitam.h | anumAnAntaravirodhasyAparihAryatvAt.h | nahi prativAdinigrahamAtreNa viruddhaM tattvaM vyavatiShThate | mA hi bhUtkasmiMshchidanumAne sad.hdUShaNadvayena dUShite.adhikatvena cha prativAdini nigR^ihIte tasya sadanumAnatvamiti pradarshanArthamevAnumAnAntaramupanyastam.h | vastutastu kAlAbhAvameva nirAkurma ityAshayavAnAha- sA.apIti || 
mokShAvasthAM kAlAbhAvasyAdhikaraNatvena vadatA sA mokShAvasthA.atrapa kadeti kenachitpR^iShye bhAvanAparipAkottarakAla ityavasthAdhikaraNatvena kAla eva vakttavyaH | nahyevaM kadA.api na praShyavyamiti niyAmakamasti | tataH kAlasya sarvathA.aparihAryatvAdakAlatvaM kAlAbhAvo na bhavet.h | tathAcha tadAshrayeNa prathamAnumAnamapi pravartsyatIti | 
nanu kAlAbhAvAdAshrayAsiddhimAdyAnumAnam.h | yadatrokttaM kadeti tadasat.h | pratiyogyadhikaraNameva hyabhAvasyAdhikaraNam.h | nacha kAlasya kAlo.adhikaraNam.h | yena tadabhAvaH kAlAdhikaraNaH syAt.h | ataH kadeti prashna evAnupapannaH | kimuttareNeti chet.h | evaM tarhi kAlavisheShamadhikaraNatvenAnupAdAya kAlaM niShedhatA sAmAnyaniShedha eva kR^itaH syAt.h | tataH kimityata Aha- neti ||
kAlo neti sAmAnyato niShedhe kriyamANe hi kAlasya svarUpameva niShiddhaM syAt.h | tathA cha kAlaM gachChati viShayIkarotIti kAlagA pramA sAkShI (niru)viruNaddhi | sa hi pUrvottarakoTirahitatayA kAlasadbhAvaM gR^ihNAtIti | na kevalamayaM sAkShivirodho vij~nAnavAdinaH kiM nAma pUrvAbhyAM saha trayANAM chetyAha- samashcheti ||
uukttAH pratyukttAH | 
nanu kathaM shUnyavAdimAyAvAdinorayaM sAkShivirodhaH | tAbhyAM kAlAbhAvasyAnabhyupagatatvAt.h | yathA hi loke.anekeShu mAyAmayAn.h gajaturagAdInpashyatsu yasya kAraNavisheSheNa mAyA.apagachChati sa eva tAnna pashyati anye tu pashyantyeva | tathA dvaitadarshanakAraNamaj~nAnaM yasyApagataM sa eva tanna pashyati | anyeShAM tu kAlAdiprapaJNchadarshanamanuvatarta eveti khalu tAbhyAmabhyupetamityata Aha- eketi ||
satyamevaM bahujIvavAdinaH shUnyavAdino mAyAvAdinashcha matam.h | nacha tayorasmAbhiH sAkShivirodho.abhihitaH | kiM tarhyekamukttireva sarvamukttiH ekasminmuktte na kiJNchidavashiShyata ityekajIvavAdapakShe tu mukttau kAlAbhAvAbhyupagamAdiyaM pramA sAkShirUpA kupitA virodhinI bhavatyeva | 
shUnyavAdimAyAvAdinau prati sAkShivirodhAbhidhAnamasaN^gatam.h | kAlAbhAvAbhyupagame.apIdAnIM tasyAprastutatvAdityata Aha- kAlamiti ||
vAditrayasAdhAraNamanumAnAntaramAha- vimata iti ||

pUrvamadvaitaniShedhamukhena pravR^ittam.h | idaM tu prapaJNchavidhimukheneti bhedaH | jIvasya mukttasya | 
ukttAtideshenAdvaitamatAntarANi dUShayati- kAleti || 
yadyadanuviddhaM pratIyate tattatrAropitam.h | yathedamAkAre rajatam.h | kAlAnuviddhaM cha samastaM pratibhAti | tasmAttatraivAropitam.h | sa eva tu paramArthaH | atastanmAtrAvasthAnaM mukttiriti kAlaikatvavAdinaH | evameva shabdaikatvavAdino vaiyAkaraNAH prAhuH | yathA "na so.asti pratyayo loke yaH shabdAnugamAdR^ite | anuviddhamiva j~nAnaM sarvaM shabdena gamyate' iti | shaivaikadeshinaH svAgamamAshrityeshvaraikatvamAhuH | 
kathaM nirAkR^itAnItyata Aha- teShAM cheti || 
teShAM shUnyavAdiprabhR^itInAM eteShAM cha pakShastAvatsamAna eva | shUnyAdishabdabhedasyAprayojakatvAt.h | pratipannasvarUpajIvavinAshAdeH sarvairabhyupagatatvAt.h | ataH parameShyanAshenApuruShArthatvamityAdidoSho.api samAna eveti | anumAnaM tu pratyakShavirodhAdinA duShyameva | tathA.a.agamo.apIti sphuTatvAnnokttam.h | 
vaibhAShikasautrAntikAbhimataM mokShaM nirUpayati- j~nAnamiti ||
evashabdena viShayasambandhaM vyAvartayati | iShyate mukttau | ayamarthaH | j~nAnamevAtmA | tachcha j~nAnaM svabhAvenaiva bhaN^guram.h | ata eva kShaNikam.h | tatsantAnastu nityaH | tasyAnAdivAsanAvashAdyo viShayoparakttasyotpAdaH sa saMsAraH bhAvanAprakarShavashena vasAnAyAmutsannAyAM yo viShayopaplavaM vinA shuddhasyaivAdayaH sa mokShaH ityubhayasamAnam.h | sautrAntikAstu saMsAre sAkAratvaM mukttau nirAkAratvaM cha visheShamAhuriti | 
nirAkaroti- tatrApIti || 
vimataH kAlo na nirviShayaitajj~nAnasantatimAn.h kAlatvAdidAnIntakAlavadityAdirukttA ukttasarUpA anumA ripurvirodhinItyatharH | 
anumAnAntaramAha- mokSha iti || 
shuddhavij~nAnasantAnI(ti) nirviShayachitsantAnasambandhI | kAlagatvataH kAlasambandhitvAt.h | pratipannaH saMsAraH | taduttaraM tatpakShasya dUShaNam.h | aprAmANikashchAyaM mokShaH | pUrvavatpratyakShAgamayorabhAvAtkevalAnumAnAni vAchyAni | tatrAha- anumAnAnIti ||
ukttabhaN^gayaiva pratisAdhanasambandhena | shrutiviruddhatvena kAlAtyayApadiShyAni cheti bhAvenAha- shrutayashcheti ||
