sAN^khayAdyabhimataM mokShamanuvadati- sAN^khayeti || 
AdyagrahaNena vaisheShikA uchyante | yathA pUrve.anupapannabhAShiNastathaite.apIti j~nApanArthashchashabdaH | kuta evaM prAhurityata Aha- ichCheti ||
tatra mukttAvichChAdveShaprayatnAderapi layamAhuH | suptipralayavailakShaNyaM darshayituM sarvAtmanetyukttam.h | nivR^ittajAtIyasya tasminnevAtmani punaranutpAdaH sarvAtmanA layaH | Adipadena buddhiduHkhadharmAdharmANAM sharIrendriyANAM cha grahaNam.h | 
tatashchAyamAshayaH | na tAvanmukttasya sukhamanAdItyupapadyate | saMsAre.api tatpratibhAsaprasaN^gAt.h pratibhAsata eveti chenna | pratibhAsamAnasyAnAditAyAM sAdhanopAdAnavaiyathyarApatteH | 
avyakttatvAtsaMsAre na pratibhAsate vyakttatvAttu mukttau pratibhAsata iti chenna | avyakttirhi pratibhAsAbhAvo vyakttishcha pratibhAsaH | tatashchApratibhAsAnna pratibhAsate pratibhAsanAchcha pratibhAsata ityukttaM syAt.h | kiJNcha pratItikAraNAntaHkaraNasadbhAve saMsAre na pratIyate | mukttau tu tadapagame pratIyata iti subhAShitam.h | AvR^itatvAnna pratIyata iti chenna | mUrtatvAbhAvenAvaraNAnupapatteH | tadanirUpaNAchcha | sukhamiva tatpratItirapyanAdishchetkimAvaraNakR^ityam.h | viShayaviShayibhAvaH pratibadhyata iti chenna | nirviShayAyAH pratIteranupapatteH | sukhatatpratItyoranAditAyAM pramitAyAmeva chaiShA kalpanA yukttA | nacha tatra pramANaM pashyAmaH | tataH sukhasya tatpratIteshcha mukttAvutpattireva vakttavyA | sA.api na sambhavati | kAraNAbhAvAt.h | sharIre sati tadAshrayendriyasadbhAvaH, tairarthAlochanaM, tataH pUrvAnubhUtasArUpyeNeShyAniShyasAdhanatvAnumAnaM, tasmAdichChAdveShau, tAbhyAM prayatnaH, tatashcheShyasAdhanopAdAnaM, aniShyasAdhanahAnaM cha, tataH sukhotpAdaH, tadanantaraM tatpratItirityeva dR^iShyakAraNakramaH | 
adR^iShyaM cha sarvatra vijayate | na chaiSha kAraNapravAho mukttAvasti | tatsadbhAve duHkhasyApi prasaN^gena mukttatvavyAghAtAt.h | 
tasmAtsukharahita eva mokShaH | 
kathamayaM puruShArtha iti chet.h sharIraM ShaDindriyANi ShaD.hivaShayAH ShaD.hbuddhayaH sukhaM duHkhaM chetyekaviMshatibhedaduHkhAtyantanivR^ittitvAditi brUmaH | duHkhanivR^ittiH puruShArtha eva na bhavati | tadIyapuruShArthatvasya sopAdhikatvAt.h | sukhaM duHkhAbhAve satyeva bhavatIti sukhArthaM duHkhAbhAvo mR^igyate na tu sa eva puruShasya samIhita iti chet.h (na) | viparyayasyApi sadbhAvAt.h | bhojanAdisukhe satyeva bubhukShAdiduHkhaM nivartata iti duHkhanivR^ittyarthameva bhojanAdisukhaM mR^igyate na punastadeva puruShasya samIhitamiti kalpyate | kvachidduHkhanivR^ittyabhAve.api sukhasyeShyamANatvAditi chenna | duHkhanivR^ittirapi kvachitsukhAbhAve.apIShyamANatvAt.h | duHkhanivR^ittau satyAM sukhameva bhaviShyatItyabhisandhistAvadastIti chet.h | sukhAvasthAyAM niyato duHkhaviraho bhavatItyabhisandhestatrApi sadbhAvAt.h | tasmAdyadyapi duHkhAbhAve sukhaM sukhe cha duHkhAbhAvo niyataH | tathA.api parasparaM nirapekShameva puruShArthatvamanayoH | ichChAyA asaN^kINarviShayatvAditi | 
bhavati duHkhahAniH puruShArthaH kiM tvanubhUyamAnatayA | nahi viShAdijanyamohAvasthAyAM duHkhanivR^ittiriti tatra prekShAvantaH pravartante | tasmAnmokShe duHkhahAnerananubhUyamAnatvAnna puruShArthatvamiti chenna | putrAdiviyogajanyaduHkhahAnimichChatAM keShAJNchidviShashastrodbandhanAdAvapi pravR^ittidarshanAt.h | prekShAvanto naivaM kurvantIti chenna | puruShAthartvAvirodhAt.h | 
nahi paradAreShu shAstraniShedhAN^kushavAritaH prekShAvanto nAbhivartanta iti na tatra kAmaH puruShArthaH | api tvalpIyaH sukhaM mahIyAnanartha


atrAha mAyAvAdI | nedaM pratyanumAnaM mAnam.h | videhAvasthaiva mokSha iti shrutisadbhAvena kAlAtItatvAt.h | kiJNcha shrutyaiva brahmabhAvAvirbhAvo mokSha ityuktatvAtkimanumAneneti | tatrAha- nacheti ||
anumAnaviShaye shrutimAlambya dUShaNaM na vadet.h | tathA.atra svAbhimate mokShe shrutiM pramANaM naiva vadedityarthaH | kuta ityata Aha- pUrveti || 
tasya mAyAvAdino mate shruteramAnatvam.h | katham.h | "prAmANyAdi cha vedasya' ityAdinA pUrvoktenaiva vartmanA | nanu na sarvo vedo.atattvAvedakaH kintu vidhiniShedhAtmaka eva | atathAbhUtAstu vedAntAstattvAvedakA iti chenna | sarvadharmojkhitasyAsya kiM shAstreNAdhigamyata ityAdinA pUrvoktenaiva vartmanA.atra tattve shruteramAnatvAt.h | 
astu vA kathaJNchit.h shrutiH pramANam.h | tathA.api nAsmadanumAnasya tadbAdha ityAha- nacheti ||
muktAviti sheShaH | tathA tadabhimatamokShavAdinItyapi grAhyam.h | "asharIraM vAva santaM na priyApriye spR^ishata' ityAdishrutisadbhAvAtkathamadehatvavAdinI shrutirnAstItyuchyata ityata Aha- adehatvamiti ||
yadasyAM shrutAvadehatvamuchyate tatprAkR^itasharIrarAhityameva | natu sarvathA.apyadehatvam.h | prAkR^itashabdena jaDamupalakShyate | tadrAhityaM cha chaturthapAdoditaprakAreNa j~nAtavyam.h | evaM "brahma veda brahmaiva bhavati' ityAdishrautirAshaN^kaya vyAkhyAtavyA cha | 
asharIratvashruteH kuto.arthasaN^kochaH kriyata ityata Aha- mokSha iti ||
"sa tatra paryeti jakShankrIDan.hramamANaH strIbhirvA yAnairvA j~nAtibhirvA.aj~nAtibhirvA' iti shrutirmokShestAdibhogaM brUte | nachAsharIrasyAsau sambhavatItyataH saN^kocha ityarthaH | 
parakIyAnumAnasya pratipakShAntaramAha- nirduHkhatvAditi ||
tachChUnyatvaM brahmatvaM vA mokSho na bhavati nirduHkhatvAt.h pratipannaM ghaTashUnyatvaM yatheti chAnumAyAH kiM dUShaNaM syAnna kimapi | shUnyashabdena tadaN^gIkAravAn.h lakShyate | shU(nyaM cha mA)nyashcha mAyI cheti dvandvaH | yadvA shUnyaM cha mAyA cheti dvandvaH | te vidyete yayoriti vrIhyAdilakShaNa iniH | tatra cha tadantavidhiriShyate | 
pratipakShAntaramAha- duHkhamiti ||
mokSha iti shUnyaM brahma chochyate | prativAdibhyAM tathA.abhyupagatatvAt.h | sa mokSho duHkhAtmA syAt.h duHkhAdabhinnatvAt.h | duHkhapratiyogikabheda(rahitatvA)shUnyatvAtprasiddhaduHkhavat.h ityarthaH | shUnyabrahmaNorduHkhatve tadbhAvApattirna puruShArtha iti siddhayati | apishabdaH pratipakShAntarasamuchchayArthaH | asaMshayamiti vyApternishchitatvamAchaShye | 
duHkhapratiyogikabhedAbhAvaH kuta ityata Aha- bheda iti ||
duHkhAt.h shUnyabrahmaNoriti sheShaH | tathA chApasiddhAnta iti bhAvaH | 
kiJNcha duHkhApAyasyAtmanAshena vinA dehAdinAshenApi sambhavAdanyathAsiddhishcha anumAnasya | sharIrAdishUnyatA.api na duHkhadhvaMsopayogitvAtpuruShArthaH | kiM nAmAtmano nirduHkhatAM prati hetutvAt.h | nahi duHkhaM nashyatviti kashchidAshAste | api tarhi nirduHkhaH syAmiti | 
nanu shUnyabhAvo brahmabhAvo vA bhavatAM siddhashchedapasiddhAntaH, na chedAshrayAsiddhiriti chenna | parAnumAne.apyAtmashUnyatAyA asiddhatvenAshrayAsiddheH | iyAMstu visheShaH | yatparaprasiddhimAtreNa pratipakShaH sambhavatIti |
nanu bhogashrutiH saguNamuktiviShayAstviti chenna | "paraM jyotirupasampadya svena rUpeNAbhiniShpadyate' ityuktivirodhAt.h | nirduHkhatvAnmokSho na bhavatIti viruddhamiti chet.h | parameShyasya Atmano nAshaH puruShArtha iti kathaM na viruddham.h | 
atha sato duHkhAdbhede sad.hdvaitatA syAt.h | duHkhaM tu mithyeti chenna | anubhavavirodhAderuktatvAt.h |
bahujIvavAdinaM prati nAntimAnumAnamiti na kuchodyAvakAshaH | 
tadetatsavarmabhisaN^ghAyopasaMharati- ityAdIti ||
sahaiveti sambandhaH | 
vij~nAnavAdyabhimataM mokShasvarUpamapyuktadoSheNAtidishati- evamiti ||
shUnyAvAdimAyAvAdyabhimatamokShavadvij~nAnavAdyabhipreto.api mokSho heya  ityarthaH | nanu vij~nAnavAdino vij~nAnaM tattvamAhuH tasyApi kShaNikatvaM svakarmakaprakAkatvalakShaNaM svaprakAshatvaM cha | nachaivaM pUrvakAvityato vaiShamyAtkatamatidesha ityata Aha- j~nAneti ||
j~nAnamAtraM chAsau visheShashcha j~nAnamAtravisheShaH | tamiti dvitIyArthe tasiH | yasmAtj~nAnamAtravisheShaM tasya j~nAnasya bhaN^guratvAdivisheShamapyapahAya vij~nAnavAdo.apyadvaitatAmataM j~nAtavyam.h | na vidyate dvaitaM yasya tattvasya tadadvaitaM tasya bhAvo.advaitatA | tasyA matamadvaitatAmatam.h | tataH kAraNAduktadoSho.api samo bhavet.h | 
idamuktaM bhavati | astu vij~nAnavAdasya pUrvasmAtkashchidvisheShaH | tathA.api sa prakR^itAnupayogitvAnnAdaraNIyaH | mokShasvarUpaM tu prakR^itaM samAnam.h | pratipannaM jIvabhAvaM vihAyAdvitIyavij~nAnatvApattirmuktiriti vij~nAnavAdinA.apyaN^gIkR^itatvAt.h | ato yukta evAtidesha iti | yadvA j~nAnamAtravisheShaM tasya bhaN^guratvAdivisheShaM chApahAya vij~nAnavAdo.api sAkShAdadvaitatAmataM j~nAtavya ityanenedamabhipraiti | na kashchidvij~nAnavAdasya pUrvAbhyAM visheShaH | j~nAnamiti visheShasya shabdamAtratvena heyatvAt.h | nahi j~nAtavyaM nAma dharmo.abhyupagamyate pareNa | bhaN^guratvAdikaM tu tenaiva kalpitamityuktatvAddheyameva | natu vastuto matabhedahetuH | yathoktaM "tatra santatibhedashcha' ityAdi | ato yukto.atidesha iti | atideshaprakArastu spaShya eva | 
anumAnAntaramapi tannirAsArthamAha- kAla iti ||
mokShakAlo.advitIyaj~nAnavAnna bhavatItyarthaH | pratipannavadvartamAnakAlavat.h | rodhAdvirodhAt.h | tAdR^ik.h mokSharUpaM yasyAtmano.asau tAdR^iN^mokSharUpastasya bhAvastattA | j~nAnAtiriktasya kalpitatvAdvartamAnakAlo.api kevalaj~nAnIti chenna | muktisaMsArayoravisheShApatteH | yastu visheSho.aN^gIkriyate tadabhAva evAnena sAdhyate | 
j~nAnavyatiriktaM kimapi nAstIti mate kAlo.api nAstyeva | ataH kimAshrayA.anumAnapravR^ittirityata Aha- yadIti ||
Aha vij~nAnavAdI | tadA kadA kAlo neti prashne pareNa kR^ite sati kimuttaramasau vakShyati | niradhikaraNasyAbhAvasya nirUpayitumashakyatvAtkAlo netyetadapi durnirUpamApadyetetyarthaH | mokShAvasthAyAM kAlo netyuttaraM vakShyAmItyAshaN^kayAha- yadeti ||
vadetkAlAbhAvAdhikaraNatveneti sheShaH | tarhi sA mokShAvasthA pUrvAnumAne pakShatAM vrajet.h | pakShashabdena tadekadesho dharmI lakShyate | mokShAvasthA na kevalaj~nAnavatIti pratij~nAsyata ityarthaH | 
evaM tarhi kAlatvAditi hetuH svarUpAsiddhaH syAdityata Aha- avasthAtvAditi ||
yadA.avasthA pakShIkriyate tadA.avasthAtvAdityeva hi heturuchyate na kAlatvAdityato noktadoShaH | 
evaM saMsArAvasthaiva dR^iShyAntIkriyata iti na dR^iShyAntadoSho.apIti vAchyam.h | prathamoktapakShahetudR^iShyAntAnAM tyAge pratij~nAhAniH syAditi chet.h | maivam.h | kAlAbhAvasyAvasthAmadhikaraNaM vadatA na kiJNchidAtmahitAmAcharitam.h | anumAnAntaravirodhasyAparihAryatvAt.h | nahi prativAdinigrahamAtreNa viruddhaM tattvaM vyavatiShThate | mA hi bhUtkasmiMshchidanumAne 
sad.hdUShaNadvayena dUShite.adhikatvena cha prativAdini nigR^ihIte tasya sadanumAnatvamiti pradarshanArthamevAnumAnAntaramupanyastam.h |
vastutastu kAlAbhAvameva nirAkurma ityAshayavAnAha- sA.apIti ||
mokShAvasthAM kAlAbhAvasyAdhikaraNatvena vadatA sA mekShAvasthA.api kadeti kenachitpR^iShye bhAvanAparipAkottarakAla ityavasthAdhikaraNatvena kAla eva vaktavyaH | nahyevaM kadA.api na praShyavyamiti niyAmakamasti | tataH kAlasya sarvathA.aparihAryatvAdakAlatvaM kAlAbhAvo na bhavet.h | tathAcha tadAshrayeNa prathamAnumAnamapi pravartsyatIti |
nanu kAlAbhAvAdAshrayAsiddhamAdyAnumAnam.h | yadatroktaM kadeti tadasat.h | pratiyogyadhikaraNameva hyabhAvasyAdhikaraNam.h | nacha kAlasya kAlo.adhikaraNam.h | yena tadabhAvaH kAlAdhikaraNaH syAt.h | ataH kadeti prashna evAnupapannaH | kimuttareNeti chet.h | evaM tarhi kAlavisheShamadhikaraNatvenAnupAdAya kAlaM niShedhatA sAmAnyaniShedha eva kR^itaH syAt.h | tataH kimityata Aha- neti ||
kAlo neti sAmAnyato niShedhe kriyamANe hi kAlasya svarUpameva niShiddhaM syAt.h | tathA cha kAlaM gachChati viShayIkarotIti kAlagA pramA sAkShI (niru)viruNaddhi | sa hi pUrvottarakoTirahitatayA kAlasadbhAvaM gR^ihNAtIti | na kevalamayaM sAkShivirodho vij~nAnavAdinaH kiM nAma pUrvAbhyAM saha trayANAM chetyAha- samashcheti ||
uktAH pratyuktAH | 
nanu kathaM shUnyavAdimAyAvAdinorayaM sAkShivirodhaH | tAbhyAM kAlAbhAvasyAnabhyupagatatvAt.h | yathA hi loke.anekeShu mAyAmayAn.h gajaturagAdInpashyatsu yasya kAraNavisheSheNa mayA.apagachChati sa eva tAnna pashyati anye tu pashyantyeva | tathA dvaitadarshanakAraNamaj~nAnaM yasyApagataM sa eva tanna pashyati | anyeShAM tu kAlAdiprapaJNchadarshanamanuvartata eveti khalu tAbhyAmabhyupetamityata Aha- eketi || 
satyamevaM bahujIvavAdinaH shUnyavAdino mAyAvAdinashcha matam.h | nacha tayorasmAbhiH sAkShivirodho.abhihitaH | kiM tarhyekamuktireva sarvamuktiH ekasminmukte na kiJNchidavashiShyata ityekajIvavAdapakShe tu muktau kAlAbhAvAbhyupagamAdiyaM pramA sAkShirUpA kupitA virodhinI bhavatyeva | shUnyAvAdimAyAvAdinau prati sAkShivirodhAbhidhAnamasaN^gatam.h | kAlAbhAvAbhyupagame.apIdAnIM tasyAprastutatvAdityata Aha- kAlamiti ||
iyaM prameti vartate | AdhAya upapAdya | ayamabhisandhiH | advitIyasya shUnyasya brahmaNo vA.avasthAnaM muktiriti tAvadekajIvavAdibhyAM tAbhyAmabhidhIyate | tatra vayaM brUmaH | kAlasadbhAvAnnAdvaitatvamupapadyata iti | tatra paraH kAlo.api nAstIti vadati tadA sAkShivirodho.abhidhIyata ityetAM saN^gatimAshrityAtideshaH kR^ito, na tvAshrayAsiddhiprasaN^geneti |
vAditrayasAdhAraNamanumAnAntaramAha- vimata iti ||
kAlaH prapaJNchavAnityukte siddhasAdhanatA syAt.h | ato vimata ityuktam.h | mokShakAla ityarthaH | tasya spaShyIkaraNAya kAla ityuktam.h | kAlAbhAvasyAnupadameva nirastatvAnnAshrayAsiddhiH | prapaJNcho viyadAdiH pratipanno vatarmAnakAlaH | pUrvoktamevedaM kutaH punaruchyata ityAshaN^kAnirAsAyoktamanyA.anumA cheti | yadyapi dvayordharmyAdikaM prayojanaM cha samAnam.h | tathA.api pUrvamadvaitaniShedhamukhena pravR^ittam.h | idaM tu prapaJNchavidhimukheneti bhedaH | jIvasya muktasya | 
uktAtideshenAdvaitamatAntarANi dUShayati- kAleti ||
yadyadanuviddhaM pratIyate tattatrAropitam.h | yathedamAkAre rajatam.h | kAlAnuviddhaM cha samastaM pratibhAti | tasmAttatraivAropitam.h | sa eva tu paramArthaH | atastantrAvasthAnaM muktiriti kAlaikatvavAdinaH | evameva shabdaikatvavAdino vaiyAkaraNAH prAhuH | yathA "na so.asti pratyayo loke yaH shabdAnugamAdR^ite | anuviddhamiva j~nAnaM sarvaM shabdena gamyate' iti | shaivaikadeshinaH svAgamAshrityeshvaraikatvamAhuH | 
kathaM nirAkR^itAnItyata Aha- teShAM cheti ||
teShAM shUnyavAdiprabhR^itInAM eteShAM cha pakShastAvatsamAna eva | shUnyAdishabdabhedasyAprayojakatvAt.h | pratipannasvarUpajIvavinAshAdeH sarvairabhyupagatatvAt.h | ataH parameShyanAshenApuruShArthatvamityAdidoSho.api samAna eveti | anumAnaM tu pratyakShavirodhAdinA duShyameva | tathA.a.agamo.apIti sphuTatvAnnoktam.h | 
vaibhAShikasautrAntikAbhimataM mokShaM nirUpayati- j~nAnamiti ||
evashabdena viShayasambandhaM vyAvartayati | iShyate muktau | ayamarthaH | j~nAnamevAtmA | tachcha j~nAnaM svabhAvenaiva bhaN^guram.h | ata eva kShaNikam.h | tatsantAnastu nityaH | tasyAnAdivAsanAvashAdyo viShayoparaktasyotpAdaH sa saMsAraH bhavanAprakarShavashena 
vAsanAyAmutsannAyAM yo viShayopaplavaM vinA shuddhasyaivodayaH sa mokShaH ityubhayasamAnam.h | sautrAntikAstu saMsAre sAkAratvaM muktau nirAkAratvaM cha visheShamAhuriti | 
nirAkaroti- tatrApIti ||
vimataH kAlo na nirviShayaitajj~nAnasantatimAn.h kAlatvAdidAnIntanakAlavadityAdiruktA uktasarUpA anumA ripurvirodhinItyarthaH | 
anumAnAntaramAha- mokSha iti ||
shuddhavij~nAnasantAnI(ti) nirviShayachitsantAnasambandhI | kAlagatvataH kAlasambandhitvAt.h | pratipannaH saMsAraH | taduttaraM tatpakShasya dUShaNam.h | aprAmANikashchAyaM mokShaH | pUrvavatpratyakShAgamayorabhAvAtkevalAnumAnAni vAchyAni | tatrAha- anumAnAnIti ||
uktabhaN^gayaiva pratisAdhanasambandhena | shrutiviruddhatvena kAlAtyayApadiShyAni cheti bhAvenAha- shrutayashcheti ||
uchyata ityuktiH asmaduktiM gachChanti pratipAdayantItyasmaduktigAH | asmadabhimatameva mokShasvarUpaM pratipAdayantItyarthaH | shrutiprAmANyaM tu prAgeva samarthitamiti |
saN^khayAdyabhimataM mokShamanuvadati- sAN^khayeti ||
AdyagrahaNena vaisheShikA uchyante | yathA pUrve.anupapannabhAShiNastathaite.apIti j~nApanArthashchashabdaH | kuta evaM prAhurityata Aha- ichCheti ||
tatra muktAvichChAdveShaprayatnAderapi layamAhuH | suptipralayavailakShaNyaM darshayituM sarvAtmanetyuktam.h | nivR^ittajAtIyasya tasminnevAtmani punaranutpAdaH sarvAtmanA layaH | Adipadena buddhiduHkhadharmAdharmANAM sharIrendriyANAM cha grahaNam.h | 
tatashchAyamAshayaH | na tAvanmuktasya sukhamanAdItyupapadyate | saMsAre.api tatpratibhAsaprasaN^gAt.h pratibhAsata eveti chenna | pratibhAsamAnasyAnAditAyAM sAdhanopAdAnavaiyarthyApatteH| 
avyaktatvAtsaMsAre na pratibhAsate vyaktatvAttu muktau pratibhAsata iti chenna | avyaktirhi pratibhAsAbhAvo vyaktishcha pratibhAsaH | tatashchApratibhAsAnna pratibhAsate pratibhAsanAchcha pratibhAsata ityuktaM syAt.h | kiJNcha pratItikAraNAntaHkaraNasadbhAve saMsAre na pratIyate | muktau tu tadapagame pratIyata iti subhAShitam.h | AvR^itatvAnna pratIyata iti chenna | mUrtatvAbhAvenAvaNAnupapatteH | tadanirUpaNAchcha | sukhamiva tatpratItirapyanAdishchetkimAravaNakR^ityam.h | viShayaviShayibhAvaH pratibadhyata iti chenna | nirviShayAyAH pratIteranupapatteH | sukhatatprItyoranAditAyAM pramitAyAmeva chaiShA kalpanA yuktA | nacha tatra pramANaM pashyAmaH | tataH sukhasya tatpratIteshcha muktAvutpattireva vaktavyA | sA.api na sambhavati | kAraNAbhAvAt.h | sharIre sati tadAshrayendriyasadbhAvaH, tairarthAlochanaM, tataH pUrvAnubhUtasArUpyeNeShyasAdhanatvAnumAnaM, tasmAdichChAdveShau, tAbhyAM prayatnaH, tatashcheShyasAdhanopAdAnaM, aniShyasAdhanahAnaM cha, tataH sukhotpAdaH, tadanantaraM tatpratItirityeSha dR^iShyakAraNakramaH | adR^iShyaM cha sarvatra vijayate | na chaiSha kAraNapravAho muktAvasti | tatsadbhAve duHkhasyApi prasaN^gena muktatvavyAghAtAt.h | 
tasmAtsukharahita eva mokShaH | 
kathamayaM puruShArtha iti chet.h sharIraM ShaDindriyANi ShaD.hivaShayAH ShaD.hbuddhayaH sukhaM duHkhaM chetyekaviMshatibhedaduHkhAtyantanivR^ittitvAditi brUmaH | duHkhanivR^ittiH puruShArtha eva na bhavati | tadIyapuruShArthatvasya sopAdhikatvAt.h | sukhaM duHkhAbhAve satyeva bhavatIti sukhArthaM duHkhAbhAvo mR^igyate natu sa eva puruShasya samIhita iti chet.h(na) | viparyayasyApi sadbhAvAt.h | bhojanAdisukhe satyeva bubhukShAdiduHkhaM nivartata iti duHkhanivR^ittyarthameva bhojanAdisukhaM mR^igyate na punastadeva puruShasya samIhitamiti kalpyate | kvachid.hduHkhanivR^ittyabhAve.api sukhasyeShyamANatvAditi chenna | duHkhanivR^itterapi kvachitsukhAbhAve.apIShyamANatvAt.h | duHkhanivR^ittau satyAM sukhameva bhaviShyatItyabhisandhistAvadastIti chet.h | sukhAvasthAyAM niyato duHkhaviraho bhavatItyabhisandhestatrApi sadbhAvAt.h | tasmAdyadyApi duHkhAbhAve sukhaM sukhe cha duHkhAbhAvo niyataH | tathA.api parasparaM nirapekShameva puruShArthatvamanayoH | ichChAyA asaN^kIrNaviShayatvAditi | 
bhavati duHkhahAniH puruShArthaH kiM tvanubhUyamAnatayA | nahi viShAdijanyamohAvasthAyAM duHkhanivR^ittiriti tatra prekShAvantaH pravartante | tasmAnmokShe duHkhahAnerananubhUyamAnatvAnna puruShArthatvamiti chenna | putrAdiviyogajanyaduHkhahAnimichChatAM keShAJNchidviShashastrodbandhanAdAvapi pravR^ittidarshanAt.h | prekShAvanto naivaM kurvantIti chenna | puruShArthatvAvirodhAt.h | nahi paradAreShu shAstraniShedhAN^kushavAritAH prekShAvanto nAbhivatarnta iti na tatra kAmaH puruShArthaH | api tvalpIyaH sukhaM mahIyAnanartha iti 
nivR^ittiH | tathA viShAdAvapi pravR^ittasya shAstre garhitatvAdalpIyAnanartho nivartate mahIyAnpravartata iti na te pravartante | iyameva hi prekShA yatpuruShArthe.api shAstralokavirodhaparAmarshaH | svarUpeNeShyamANatAmAtranibandhanatvAtpuruShArthatAyAH | ata eva yatra lokashAstrAvirodhastatra vyAdhyAdiparipIDitAH prayagavAripAtAnashanAdinA.api dehaM tyajantaH prekShAvanto.api dR^ishyante | 
na kvachid.hduHkhanivR^ittimanubhaviShyAmIti tatsAdhane pravartante | api tu duHkhaM hAsyAmIti | api cha duHkhanivR^itteranubhUyamAnatAmAtraM vivakShitaM, duHkhanivR^ittisattA.api vA | AdyeshchettuShyatu durjanaH charame janmanyanubhUyata eva | samAdhibhAvA(vadhiva)dAtyantikI duHkhanivR^ittirapyanAgatA.avartamAnA.apyachiramanubhUyata eva | dvitIye tu prasaktakaNTakAdihetukaduHkhanivR^itterapuruShArthatvaprasaN^gaH | sarvadA.ananubhUyamAnatvAt.h | tathAtve vA viShayAntarasaJNchArAbhAvaprasaN^gaH | nivR^itteH sarvadA tAdavasthyAt.h |
tasmAtsukharahito mokShaH puruShArtha iti |
nirAkaroti- naitaditi ||
atra muktau | etat.h sukharAhityamatamapi na shobhanam.h | kuta ityata Aha- shrUyata iti ||
atreti vartate | bhogam.h tadanubhavam.h | niyamena avigAnena | iti shrutInAM prasiddhatAmAchaShye | tAshchodAhariShyante | 
nanu "asharIraM vAva santaM na priyApriye spR^ishate' iti muktasya duHkhavatsukhasyApi hAniH shrUyate | tathA "na pretya saMj~nA.asti' iti j~nAnAbhAvAchcha | tatkathametadityataH sukhAspR^iShyishrutiM tAvadvayAchaShye- prAkR^iteti ||
asyAM shrutau prAkR^itaM yadantaHkaraNapariNatirUpaM priyaM taddhAnireva priyAspR^iShyiritishabdena pratipAdyate | natu sarvathA sukhAbhAvaH | 
evaM tarhyapi्rayAspR^iShyirapyevaM vibhAgena vyAkhyAtavyA | visheShAbhAvAt.h | tathAcha mokShe duHkhasadbhAva(prAptiri)prasaktirityata Aha- api्rayamiti ||
yasmAtsakalamapyapriyaM (duHkhaM) pratikUlaM mumukShoranapekShitam.h | tattasmAdapriyamatrAvisheSheNa shabditam.h | 
etaduktaM bhavati | sarvAtmanA.aniShyanivR^ittirmokSha iti tAvadavivAdaM sarvavAdinAm.h | duHkhaM tu yAdR^ishatAdR^ishamapyaniShyameva | ato na tadvibhAgena vyAkhyAtuM yuktamiti | 
yadvA | yena nyAyena priye vibhAgaH kriyate tadavisheShashchedapriye syAttadA tadapi vibhAgena vyAkhyAtavyaM bhavet.h | nachaivam.h | sAmastyena priyahAniraniShyA | aniShyaprAptau cha mokShasyApuruShAthartvaM syAdityato hi priye vibhAgaH kalpyate | tathAcha vakShyAmaH | nacha sAmastyena duHkhahAniraniShyA | sarvasyApi duHkhasyAniShyatvena taddhAneriShyatvAt.h | tarhi sarvasyApi sukhasyeShyatvAt.h prAkR^itasukhahAnirapi nAN^gIkaraNIyeti chenna | tasya duHkhAnuShaktatvena viShasampR^iktamadhuvadaniShyapakShanikShepAditi bhAvaH | 
itashcha nApriyaM prAkR^itatvena visheShaNIyamityAha- nAstIti |
aprAkR^ite duHkhe sati tadvayAvR^ittaye prAkR^itamiti visheShaNIyaM syAt.h | sato muktiyogyasya | jIvasyAprAkR^itaM duHkhaM nAsti pramANAbhAvAt.h | ato vyarthaM visheShaNamiti | kutrachit.h shrutau smR^itau choktamiti sheShaH | 
evaM tarhyaprAkR^itasya sukhasyApyapramitatvAttatrApi visheShaNaprakShepeNa vyAkhyAnamayuktamityata Aha- priyamiti ||
"balamAnanda ojashcha saho j~nAnamanAkulam.h | svarUpANyeva jIvasya vyajyante paramAdvibhoH' iti shrutivAkyAdasya sato jIvasya priyaM svarUpamevetyavagamyate | svarUpaM chAprakR^itam.h | atastadvayavachChedAya visheShaprakShepeNa vyAkhyAnaM yujyate | (etena) anena sukhasyotpattimattve yo doSho.abhihitaH so.anaN^gIkAraparAsto veditavyaH | svarUpatvenAnAditvasyoktatvAt.h | yadatroktaM tadapyasat.h | AvR^itAH santo vyajyanta iti shrutatvAt.h | AvaraNaM cha mAyA.avidyAdisamAkhyAtA prakR^itireva | nacha vishadashrutisiddhe.arthe kAchidanupapattiH | j~nAnasya svarUpatvenAnAditve.apyavidyayA viShayaviShayibhAvaH pratibadhyate | nachoktadoShaH | AtmasvarUpAdau tasyApratibaddhatvAt.h | 
uktamarthaM saMkShipyAha- heyatvAditi ||
apriyasya duHkhasya heyatvAdevetyevashabdena sarvatheti sUchayati | "asharIraM vAva santam.h' ityasyAM shrutau prokte mokShe samastapriyAbhAvo na vyAkhyAtuM yujyate | kutaH priyahAneraniShyatvataH | kintu prAkR^itatvavisheShaNaprakShepeNeti tushabdaH | apriyahAnaM tvavisheSheNa vyAkhyeyamityupaskartavyam.h | tatra heturapriyasya sarvathA heyatvAditi | upalakShaNaM chaitat.h | sato jIvasyAprAkR^itaduHkhAbhAvAchchetyapi draShyavyam.h | 
nanu sajjIvasyApyapriyaM svarUpabhUtamaprAkR^itamasti | tatkathametadityata Aha- apriyasyeti ||
asurAshcha na mokShayogyA iti bhAvaH | tAM shrutimarthataH paThati- asurA iti ||
anena "nityAnando nityaj~nAno nityabalaH paramAtmA | naivamasurA evamanevaM cha manuShyA iti shrutimupAdatte | nityatvoktyA svarUpatvaM siddham.h | vR^ittInAmanityatvAt.h | paramAtmA parameshvaraH | sajjIva iti vA | naivamiti | etadviruddhasvabhAvA ityarthaH | evamanevaM cheti | ubhayasvabhAvaH' ityarthaH | asurA naivaM, akhilamAnuShA evaM cha naivaM cheti yojanA | iti shrutamiti sambandhaH | 
apriyahAnAvapi saN^kochaH kriyatAmityatiprasaN^gaM nivArayataiva sAmAnyataH shrutA priyAspR^iShyiH kuto visheShe.avasthApyata ityAshaN^kA.api parihR^itA | niyAmakasya sUchitatvAt.h | tadeva niyAmakaM vispaShyamAchaShye- Atmeti ||
AtmA cha tatpriyaM cheti Atmapriyam.h | AtmanaH priyamiti vA | tadichChati cheti chashabdaH | 
yadi priyAspR^iShyiravishiShyA syAttadA na kashchitprekShAvAnmokShamichChet.h | nApi tadarthaM prayateta | yadyapi dveShavashAtparakIyasukhahAnAdAvichChAdikaM sambhavati | tathA.api na kashchid.h buddhimAnAtmanaH sukhahAnamichChati | tadatharM prayatate vA | vR^ittirUpasukhasyAniShyabhUyiShThatvAttattyA(gechChA)gAyechChAdikaM yujyate | svarUpasukhaM tu niShkaNTakaM kasmAttyAjyam.h | nacha tannAsti, shrutisiddhatvAt.h | kAraNaikyanimitto hi sukhasya duHkhAnuShaN^gaH | nachAtmasukhasya kAraNamasti | ashakyaM chAtmasukhahAnam.h | nachAshakyaviShayechChAprayatnau buddhimataH sambhavataH | AtmahAnaM khalu vinAshalakShaNamanutpAdalakShaNaM cha na sambhavati, nityatvAt.h | nApi viyogalakShaNaM, pareShAM mate vibhutvAt.h | asmAkaM svAtmani kriyAvirodhAt.h | nApyaj~nAnalakShaNaM svaprakAshatvAt.h | 
tadevaM bAdhakasadbhAvAtpriyAspR^iShyirvisheShaniShThaiva vyAkhyeyA | tathAcha "asharIraM vAva santam.h' iti shrutyuktopapattiH shliShyata iti |
evaM sukhAspR^iShyishrutiM vyAkhyAya j~nAnAbhAvashrutiM cha vyAkhyAti- saMj~neti ||
shrutirvaktIti vakShyamANamatrApi sambaddhayate | "na pretya saMj~nA.asti' ityapi shrutirasya muktasyAmuktaj~neyatA nAstItyeva vakti | natu mukto na jAnAtIti | eko hishabda evArthaH | dvitIyastu svoktArthasya shabdashaktyanatikramaM sUchayati |
tathAhi | pretya maraNAnantaraM saMj~nAM j~nAnaM nAstIti tAvachChrauto.atharH | tatra prakaraNavashAtpretyetyetanmaraNavisheShamokShAnantaramiti vyAkhyeyam.h | j~nAnaM tu muktasambandhi pratiShidhyamAnaM tatkartR^ikameveti kalpane na niyAmakaM pashyAmaH | atastatkamarkasyaiva j~nAnasyAyaM pratiShedho vij~nAyate | sarvathA.aj~ne(yatAyAM vA) yAnAM chAsattvaM prasajyata ityamuktaj~neyatAniShedha iti kalpyate | amuktAnAmapyasmadAdInAmaparokShaj~nAnasyAyaM pratiShedhaH | nAradAdibhirAparokShyeNAsmadAdibhishcha shAstreNa tajj~nAnAt.h | ata eva saMshabdaprayoga iti |
nanu sAdhAraNe vAkye muktaviShayasya j~nAnasyAyaM pratiShedho natu tatkartR^ikasyeti kutaH kalpyata ityata Aha- dharmeti || 
yataH kAraNAt.h "ayamAtmAnuchChittidharmaH' ityuttarashrutirasya muktAtmano dharmAnuchChittimeva vakti | na vidyate uchChittiryeShAM te tathoktAH | anuchChittayo dharmA yasyAsAvanuchChittidharmeti | tasmAdevaM vyAkhyAta iti |
syAdetat.h | anuchChittidharmetyetatsaN^khayAdidharmANAmanuchChittiM vaktItyapi shakyate vaktum.h | yadvA uchChitterabhAvo.anuchChittiH sA dharmo yasyAsAvanuchChittidharmeti | tatkathametanniyAmakamityAshaN^kAnirAsAyAdita eva vAkyaM vyAchaShye- AshaN^kayeti ||
"vij~nAnaghana evaitebhyo bhUtebhyaH samutthAya tAnyevAnuvinashyati na pretya saMj~nA.asti' vij~nAnamUtirrayamAtmA.anAdirapi charame janmanyetebhyo bhUtebhyaH samutthAya bhUtAtmakasharIrotpattinimittamevotpannavyavahAraviShaye bhUtvA punastAni bhUtAnyanveva tannAshanimittameva nityo.api vinashyati | vinaShyavyavahAra(gocharo bha)viShayo bhavati | apavrajyata iti yAvat.h | tataH pretya mokShAnantaramasya muktasya saMj~nA j~nAnaM nAstItyavishadaM yAj~navalkyavAkyaM shrutvA asya muktasya j~nAnahAnimAshaN^kayAnena vAkyena mukto na jAnAtItyuchyata iti matvA maitreyyA "atraiva mA bhavAnmohAntamApipat.h' iti vAkye bhavAnmAM prati yadAha mukto na jAnAtIti tanmohakamevetyarthamuktavatyA chodita iti sheShaH | 
yAj~navalkyo na vA are.ahaM mohaM bravImItyanena j~nAnopadeshAya pravR^itto.ahaM paramapriyAyai te mohaM na vadAmIti pratij~nAmuktvA kathamityAshaN^kAyAmavinAshI vA are.ayamAtmetyAtmasvarUpasyAnAshamUchivAn.h | 
yadvA AshaN^kayeti NijantAllayap.h | yAj~navalkyaH saMmugdhena vachasA.asyAmaitreyyA j~nAnahAnimAshaN^kayochivAniti yojanA | 
tasyAstathA shaN^kA jAtetyatra kiM mAnamityatroktaM mohamAha mAM bhavAnityuktavatyA hIti vachanaliN^genAshaN^kA(va)gamyata ityarthaH | ayamarthaH spaShya eva shrutAviti dvitIyo hishabdaH | 
j~nAnavinAshavachanaM mohakamityAkShepe svarUpAnAsho.asaN^gataH kathamukta ityata Aha- j~nAnasvarUpasyeti ||
yat.h yasmAjj~nAnarUpastAvadAtmA tasya cha vij~nAnanAsho nAma tannAsha eva | nachAtmanAsho.asti | tathA sati mukterapuruShArthatvaprasaN^gAt.h | ato na j~nAnanAsho.asti | ata eva na madvachanaM tadartham.h, kiM tvamuktAnAM muktaviShaye saMj~nA nAsti, muktAnAmeva vA vR^ittirUpA saMj~nA nAstItyAdireva madvachanArtha ityabhiprAyavAnsvarUpAnAshamUchivAniti sambandhaH | 
astvevaM saN^gatistathA.api j~nAnaM na nashyatIti sAkShAdanuktvaivaM vachanaM kimarthamityata Aha- shUnyeti ||
na kevalamatra prameyanirUpaNamAtrArthaM pravR^itto yAj~navalkyaH kintu parI(kShAyAM)kShayA | ata eva na pretya j~nAyata iti vishadamanuktvA shaN^kotpAdanAya na pretya saMj~nA.astIti sAdhAraNaM vAkyamAha | parIkShA cha svAnabhimatanirAsarUpA | ata evamuttare datte shUnyamatasyAtmanAshalakShaNasya niraso.api kR^ito bhavatIti tadarthaM svarUpAnAshamUchivAn.h |
yadarthamAdito vAkyaM vyAkhyAtaM tadidAnImanuchChittidharmetyetadvayAchaShye- punariti ||
svarUpAnAshamuktvA punarapi muktasyAnandapUvarkAndharmAnanuchChinnAnAha yAj~navalkyaH | svarUpAnAshoktyaiva dharmAnuchChittisiddhau punaruktiriyamityata uktamAnandapUrvakAniti | vAkyopakrame vij~nAnaghana eveti vij~nAnasyAtmasvarUpatvamuktaM na punarAnandapUrvakAniti | vAkyopakrame vij~nAnaghana eveti vij~nAnasyAtmasvarUpatvamuktaM na punarAnandapUrvakANAm.h | ataH svarUpAnAshoktyA vij~nAnAvinAsha eva suj~nAno nAnandAdyavinAshaH | ataste.api vij~nAnavat.h AtmasvarUpabhUtA eva nochChidyante ityarthapratipattyarthamidaM vAkyamiti | 
tAtparyAntaraM sUchayati- tArkikairiti |
uktametatparIkShAyAM pravR^itto yAj~navalkya iti | ataH svarUpAvinAshamaN^gIkR^itya ye tArkikA buddhisukhAdIndharmAnmuktasya vinivArayanti te.apyasamIchInavAdina iti j~nApanAyedaM vAkyamiti na paunaruktyadoShaH |
nanu svarUpAvinAshoktyA dharmAvinAsho.api siddha eva | satyam.h | svamatarItyA tat.h | tArkikAstu na j~nAnasukhAdInAmAtmasvarUpatvaM manyante | ataH kimidAnIM mokShaprasaN^ge teShAmAtmasvarUpatvopapAdanena | AtmasvarUpaprakriyAyAM tadapi vaktavyamityAshayenAnuchChittirevokteti |
idamatrAkUtam.h | anuchChittidharmeti yadi saN^khayAdidharmANAmanuchChittiruktA syAt.h tadA asaN^gatamidaM vAkyamApadyeta | j~nAnavinAshavachanaM moha ityAkShepe saN^khayAdyavinAshakathanasya saN^gatyadarshanAt.h | yadi cha svarUpAvinAsho.anenokta iti syAttadA tasya pUrvavAkyenaivoktatvAt.h punaruktidoShaH syAt.h | asmatpakShe tvasti sarveShAM vAkyAnAmuktarItyA sAphalyam.h | tasmAjj~nAnAnandAdiguNAnAmevAnuchChittimAhedaM vAkyamiti gamyate | tadbalAchcha na pretya saMj~nA.astItyetadapi uktArthameveti | 
itashchaitaduktAtharmevetyAha- mAtreti || 
yathA dharmAnuchChittimAha tathA mIyanta iti mAtrA rUpAdayo viShayAsteShAM saMsargamupabhogalakShaNamapyasyAha "mAtrAsaMsargastvasya bhavati' iti vAkyena | tato na j~nAnavilopo vyAkhyAtuM shakyate | nedaM vAkyaM shrutAvupalabhyata ityata uktam.h- mAdhyandinashrutiriti || 
maitreyIyAj~navalkyasaMvAdarUpamidaM prakaraNaM kANvamAdhyandinashrutyoH samAnam.h | idaM tu vAkyaM yadyapi kANvashrutau nAsti tathA.api mAdhyandinashrutAvastyeveti |
ito.api saMj~nA nAstIti vAkyamuktArthamevetyAha- AchikShepeti ||
shrutiriti vakShyati | yatra hi "dvaitamiva bhavati' ityAdiruttarA shrutiryasminmate muktasya na viShayAdanaM rUpAdiviShayabhogo nAstItyabhyupagamastanmatamAchikShepa ninditavatIti | tatashcha na tadvAkyaM muktasya j~nAnAbhAvaM pratipAdayati | nahi j~nAnarahitasya ghaTakalpasya viShayasaMsargo vA tadabhAvanindA vopapadyate | kathamAchikShepeti chet.h | uchyate | yatra yadi, dvaitaM bhavati tat.h tarhyeva, itara itaraM pashyatItyAdinA vyAptimabhidhAya hishabdena tasyAH pramitatvaM choktvA yatra yadi, tu , asyAtmano.apekShitaM sarvamAtmaivAbhUt.h svavyatiriktaM na syAt.h | tat.h tarhi kena sAdhanena kam.h arthaM pashyeta | na kenApi kiJNchidityaniShyaprasaN^go.abhidhIyate |
evaM tarhi yadi muktau dvaitaM na syAttadA rUpadarshanAdikaM na bhavediti tarkitaM bhavati | tathAcha dvaitAbhAvamatamanayAkShiptaM, na viShayabhogAbhAvamatamityata Aha- ghrANAdIti ||
ghrANAdinA gandhAderbhogo ghrANAdibhogaH | kena kamiti karaNasya karmaNashchoktatvAt.h | tushabdo visheShArthaH | hR^idA.abhiprAyeNa | 
pUrveNaiva sambandhaH | 
satyametat.h shUnyamataM tArkikamataM cha nirAkR^ityAdvaitamanayA shrutyA nirAkriyata iti | tachcha viShayabhogAbhAvaprasaJNjanena | prasaJNjanIyaM cha tadbhavati yadaniShyam.h | ato.advaitamate ghrANAdibhogAbhAvaM prasaJNjayantI shrutistasyAniShyatvamabhipraitIti gamyate | aniShyaM cha taduchyate yadaprAmANikaM pramANaviruddhaM cha | ato viShayabhogAbhAvanindA shrutyabhiprAyavyAptA bhavatyeveti |
bhavedevamarthApattyA viShayabhogAbhAvanindAvagamo yadyatrAdvaitamate viShayabhogAbhAvaH prasaJNjanIyaH syAt.h | na chaivam.h | api tarhi vastusthitikathanametat.h | tathAhi | ayamAtmA avinAshI ata evAnuchChittistasya dharmaH | muktau mAtrAbhirasaMsargastasya bhavati | kutaH | yatra hi saMsAre dvaitamiva bhavati tattatretara itaraM pashyatItyAdi | yatra tu muktAvasya sarvamAtmaivAbhUtsvavyatiriktaM kimapi nAsti tatra kena kaM pashyenna kenApi na kimapItyadvaitinaH | tatrAha- yeneti || 
yenedamakhilaM veda taM cha kena vijAnIyAt.h vij~nAtAraM cha kena vijAnIyAdityanena yenedaM sarvaM vijAnAti taM cha kena vijAnIyAt.h vij~nAtAramare kena vijAnIyAditi vAkyadvayamupAdatte | vij~nAtAramityetatsvameveti vyAchaShye | prathamavAkyaviShayaM sUtrasya vakShyati | iti vAkyadvayoktaM viShNuj~nAnarAhityaM svaj~nAnarAhityaM cha | 
etaduktaM bhavati | atrAnte yenedamiti vAkyadvayaM shrUyate | tadarthaH parameshvaraj~nAnAbhAvaH svaj~nAnAbhAvashcha tAvadaniShyo na vAstavaH | tatastatprasaN^gakathanameveti j~nAyate | tatsAhacharyAtkena kaM pashyedityAdikamapi prasaJNjanameva na vastusthitikathanamiti j~nAtavyamiti |
nanvIshvarastAvatsarvathA.apyavisheSha eva | yato vAcha ityAdishruteH | jIvAtmA cha na svavij~nAnI | ekasyAM kriyAyAmekasyaiva kartR^ikarmabhAvasya viruddhatvAt.h | ataH parameshvaraj~nAnAbhAvaH svaj~nAnAbhAvashcha kathamaniShya ityataH parameshvarasya savarthA.apyavij~neyatvaM tAvannirAkaroti- neti ||
atrAkhilaj~nApaka ityanena yenedamiti vAkyArthamanUdya viShNuriti tasya viShayo darshitaH | prAgavyAkhyAtatvAt.h | viShNuM vinaitadvAkyAtharsyAsambhavAt.h | hishabdastAvadarthe | viShNurniyamena sarvathA.apyaj~neya iti tAvanna bhavati | kuta ityata Aha- taditi ||
sarve vedA ityAderiti sheShaH | viShNoH sarvathA.apyaj~neyatve.akhilavedavaiyarthyaprasaN^gAdyato vAcha ityAdikamanyathA vyAkhyeyamiti bhAvaH | 
evaM paramAtmano j~neyatvamupapAdya jIvAtmanaH svaj~nAnamupapAdayati- pratyakShamiti || 
kriyAvisheShaNametat.h | Atmavij~nAnaM chAvirodhashcheti dvandvaH | avirodhashcha prasaN^gAdAtmA vij~nAna eva | tayoranubhavaH | sa cha pratyakSharUpaH tasmAt.h | apipadena shrutyAdigrahaNam.h | svavij~nAnitAyAM jIvasya kashchana virodho neyate | na kA.apyanupapattiH pratIyate | Atmavij~nAnAnubhavastAvat.h mAmahaM jAnAmIti sAkShirUpaH prasiddha eva | yathA ghaTamahaM jAnAmItyatra na kAchidanupapattiH pratIyate | kiM tvanupalambhasanAthena sAkShiNA.anupapattyabhAva eva sAkShAtkriyate | tathA tadavishiShye mAmahaM jAnAmIti j~nAne.api | shrutayo.api "ahamityeva yo vedyaH' ityAdyAH | yadi chAtmA na svAtmAnaM jAnIyAttadA mamedamiShyasAdhanamityAdij~nAnAbhAvAttathAvidhechChAprayatnayorapyabhAvAtsarvapravR^ittinivR^ittivilopaprasaN^gaH | svaprakAshatvaM j~nAnAshrayatayA prakAshamAnatvaM cha na svaj~nAnAtirekeNopapadyata iti |
ChidAdiShu kartR^ikarmaNorbhedadasharnAttadekatvAbhyupagamo viruddha iti yaduktaM tannirAkaroti- katarR^ikarmeti ||
ekasyAM kriyAyAM kartR^ikarmatvayorvirodhaH kartR^ikarmavirodhaH | nityAnubhavaH uktasAkShyanubhavaH | padam.h Aspadam.h prakR^ita iti sheShaH | 
ayamAshayaH | uktametalliN^gapAde | yatkartR^ikarmaNorbheda ityautsargiko.ayaM nyAyaH | apavAde satyabhedo.api bhavatIti | atra cha mAmahaM jAnAmIti sAkShyanubhavavirodhAnnAyamasya nyAyasya viShayaH | kintu yatrAdR^iShyabAdhanaM pramANavirodhAbhAvastatraivAyaM virodhaH pravartate | yathAN^gulyagreNAN^gulyagrasparshane | yathA vA.asidhArayA.asidhArAChedana iti |
astvevamIshvarasya j~neyatvaM, jIvasya cha svaj~nAnitvam.h | tathA.api muktau tajj~nAnAbhAvaH kathamaniShya iti chet.h | uchyate | "nAtmAnaM na parAMshchaiva na satyaM nApi chAnR^itam.h | prAj~naH kiJNchana saMvetti turyaM tatsarvadR^ik.h sadA' iti shrutau svaj~nAnamIshvaraj~nAnaM cha nAstItyabhidhAya muktasya tu tadastItyuchyate | atastadabhAvaH pramANaviruddha iti kathaM nAniShyaH | na kevalamevamaniShyaprakaraNAdviShayabhogAbhAvasyAniShyatvaM gamyate kintu viShayabhogasyApi shrutisiddhatvAchchetyAha- sa iti || 
atha mukteranantaramiti shrutidvayasyopakrame sambaddhayate | uktamevArthaM muktasya viShayabhogasadbhAvam.h | ata eva mAtrAbhirasaMsarga iti vyAkhyAnamasadeveti |
syAdetat.h | yatra hi dvaitamiva bhavatIti ivashabdena dvaitAbhAvaH pratipAdyate tatkathaM dvaitAbhAve.aniShyaprasaN^gAbhidhAnametadityata Aha- asvAtantAditi ||
dvaitasyAsvAtantyamabhipretya dvaitamivetyuktam.h | natu dvaitAbhAvamabhipretya | kutaH | kvachidabhidhAnAdAvivashabdasyAbhAvavAchitA.anukterityarthaH | asvAtantyaM chAtra svarUpamAtramuktam.h | 
ivashabdasyAbhAvArthatve bAdhakaM chAha- Atmaiveti |
ivashabdasyAbhAvArthatve dvaitamiva bhavatItyasya dvaitaM nAstItyarthaH syAt.h | yatra tvasya sarvamAtmaivAbhUdityasya tAvad.h dvaitAbhAvo.arthaH sphuTa eva | tatastasmAdasya visheSho na bhavet.h | tathA cha dvaitAbhAve itara itaraM pashyet.h | dvaitAbhAve kena kaM pashyediti vAkyadvayArthaH prasajyeta | tatashcha unmattavAkyatA shruterApadyata iti |
nanvivashabdasyAsvAtantyavAchitvaM kuta ityata Aha- asvAtanteti ||
abhedabhedeti pratIyogidvayopalakShaNam.h | ivAnta ekasminnukte tatpratiyogI dvitIyo.api labhyata ityarthaH | 
nanvasmAkamupamAyAmevevashabdaH | dvaitAbhAvastvarthasiddhaH | yathA gauriva gavaya ityukte gavayasya gotvAbhAvo.avagamyata iti chet.h | tarhi dvaitasadR^ishaM kiM taditi vAchyam.h | kalpitaM dvaitamiti chenna | tasya sattAbhAvena bhavatItyanupapatteH | bhavanamapi tasya kAlpanikamiti chet.h | evaM tarhi yadi dvaitadarshanaM syAditi syAt.h | tathA chetara itaraM pashyatItyetadapi tadeveti na hetuhetumadbhAvo.avakalpyata iti |
na pretya saMj~nA.astIti vAkyasya mukto na jAnAtItyevArthamaN^gIkR^ityAvinAshItyAdivAkyAnya(pya)nyathA vyAkurvato bAdhakamAha- maitreyIti ||
na pretya saMj~nA.astIti vAkyaM shrutvA maitreyyoktamatraiva mA bhavAnityAdi | tattAvannAhR^idayaM nirdalAkShepakaraNe.asuj~natvaprasaN^gAt.h | tataH praj~nAnaghana ityAtmano j~nAnasvarUpatvamabhidhAyedAnIM j~nAnAbhAvaM vadatastava vAkyaM mohakamityabhiprAyaH kalpyaH | apuruShArthatvaprasaN^go vA | yathoktaM "saMj~nAnAsho yadi bhavetkiM muktyA naH prayojanam.h | mohaM mAM prANayAmAsa bhavAnatreti choditaH' iti | anyathAvyAkhyAne maitreyyuktaM niruttaraM prasajyeta | na hyetairvAkyaiH svavachanavyAghAtaH parihR^ito nApi puruShArthatA samarthiteti |
evaM sAN^khayanaiyAyikAdyabhimatasya mokShasyAprAmANikatvamabhidhAya, yaduktaM mokShasyApuruShArthatvaprasaN^ga iti tatprapaJNchayati- sukhAdIti ||
sukhAdidharmahAnau muktitvenAN^gIkR^itAyAmiti sheShaH | tushabdaH svapakShAdvishinaShyi | parasyApAdyamAno doShaH svamate nAstItyAshayaH | mukteriti sambandhamAtre ShaShThI | kimAkShepe | chashabdo.aprAmANikatvena samuchchayArthaH | prayujyate pravartyate puruSho.aneneti prayojanam.h | mukteH prayojanaM kimiti | muktyarthe puruShaM pravartayatkimapi nAstItyarthaH | 
dvividhaM prayojanam.h | iShyAvAptiraniShyanivR^ittishcha | tatra yadyapi muktiriShyaprAptirUpA na bhavati tathA.apyaniShyanivR^ittirUpA bhavatyeva | ataH puruSheNArthyata ityAshaN^kate- yadIti ||
duHkhahAnirUpA muktiH puruShasyArtho.arthanIyaH syAditi yadi brUShe | atrochyate | bhavatyaniShyanivR^ittiH puruShArthaH | muktishcha samastaduHkhahAnistathA.api na puruShArthaH kathamityata Aha- anartha iti || 
sukhanAsharUpo.anartho.apyasti yataH | 
idamuktaM bhavati | kevalasya duHkhasyAtyantikI nivR^ittirbhavati puruShArthaH, iyaM tu duHkhavat.h sukhasyApyAtyantikI nivR^ittiriti kathaM puruShAtharH | aniShyanivR^ittyAshayA pravR^ittau iShyanivR^ittibhiyA nivR^ittyApatteH | duHkhashabalasukhahAnau sukhashabaladuHkhopAdAnaprApteshcha | 
yadatroktaM "yasya duHkhamupAdeyaM tasya heyaM kimuchyatAm.h | heyahInasya kA muktiH kena chApyupadishyate' iti, tadidamasaN^gatam.h | nahi vayaM duHkhasyopAdeyatvamupapAdayAmaH | kintu samavyayaphalatvena vinigamane kAraNAbhAvAnna pravR^ittyupapattiriti brUmaH | yathoktam.h "asatyAni durantAni samavyavaphalAni cha | ashakyAni cha vastUni nArabheta vichakShaNaH' iti | aN^gIkR^ityaiva samavyayaphalatvamuktam.h | vastutastu AyAdapi vyayo garIyAnityAha- tayoshcheti || 
sukhaduHkhahAnayormadhye | nahi rAjAdayo rAjyAdyapagame duHkhahAnena sukhahAnavyathAM samAdadhati | tato nivR^ittireva mukteriti bhAvaH | 
yatra nivartamAnaM duHkhamalpIyaH | sukhaM tu mahattatraivametat.h | iha tu mahad.hduHkhaM nivartate sukhaM tvalpIyastatkathaM na puruShArthatvam.h | "yastu ghanataraduHkha(timira)nirantarAtsaMsArakAntArAtsukhakhadyotikAsu dyotamAnAsvapi bibheti, taM pratyayaM nirastataskaratayA sugamo mArga upa(dishyata)darshitaH' iti | tatrAha- prApyApIti || 
yato jAndhikAdirjanaH sumahadduHkhaM prApyApi sukhaleshAptaye yatate | tasmAdalpasyApi sukhasya hAnau mahato.api duHkhasya mokShAya kaH pumAnyateta na ko.api | abhyupagamavAdashchAyam.h | nahi sAMsArikasukhasya duHkhApekShayA.alpatvaM pramitam.h | kasmiMshchana janmanyayaM (daridro)(durbhago) duHkhito bhavati kasmiMshchitsArvabhaumaH kadAchinnarakamanubhavati kadAchitsvargam.h | yA cha mokShashAstreShu sAMsArikasukhanindA sA nirastasamastaduHkhaM mokShagataM paramAnandamapekShyAlpatvAbhiprAyeNeti |
mahAduHkhahAnAdalpaM sukhaM garIya ityetatprakArAntareNopapAdayati- alpAchcheti || 
(hAnasyA)nAshasyAlpatvaM pratiyogyalpatvanimittam.h | alpasyApi sukhasya (hAnAdi)nAshAditi yAvat.h | sukhanAshanivR^ittaya iti | prasaktasya sukhanAshahetornivR^ittaya ityarthaH | udAharaNAni tu loke spaShyAnyeva kathaM tarhi madhuviShasampR^iktAnna(bhojana)parityAga iti chet.h | bahutarasukhahAniprApteriti brUmaH | anyathA pareNApi vyavasthAyAH katarvyatvAt.h | 
syAdetat.h | dvividhAH puruShAH rAgiNo vItarAgAshcha | tatra rAgiNaH sukhArthaM duHkhamapyanubhavanti | te hi madhuviShasampR^iktamapyannaM madhutayA.a.apAtaramaNIyaM viSha(viShaMgA)saMyogAttu mArayatu mA vA mImaradupa(bhuMjmahe)yuMkShmahe tAvadApAtasukhaM ko hi hastagataM pAdagataM karotIti vichintyopabhuJNjate | vItarAgAstvA(yati)pattimAlochayantaH svagarmapi kupitabhogiphaNamaNDalachChAyApratimamityapajahatItyata Aha- nacheti ||
yadetaduktaM, prApyApItyAdi tadrAganimittam.h | mumukShavastu vItarAgAH tasmAtsukhamanAdR^itya duHkhadhvaMsAyaiva yatanta iti, tachcha netyarthaH | kuta ityata Aha- vIteti ||
sphuTamiti nAradAdInAM vItarAgatvaM shrutyAdiprasiddhamityarthaH | aJNjaseti shravaNAdalpAya sukharUpArthAyeti yojyam.h | yasmAditi vakShyamANamihApi sambaddhayate | etatkuta ityata Aha- yuddhAdIti ||
sukhAtharAyeti vartate | nAradAdyA iti cha | Adipadena dUragamanAdisAdhyaM svayaMvaradarshanaM cha gR^ihyate | etadapi kuta ityata Aha- yadeti ||
naivAjarhuryuddhadarshanaM yuddharasAdyuddhadarshananimittAtsukhAtkAraNAt.h | yadAshabdasya pUrvatrottaratra vA sambandhaH | yasmAditi atrApi sambaddhayate | 
idamatrAkUtam.h | atra rAgashabdena kiM sukhechChA.abhipretA | uta lakShaNayA avivekaH | Adye satyametat.h | kintu mumukShavo.api rAgiNa eva | rAgiNAM kathaM muktiriti chet.h dveShiNAmapi katham.h | duHkhadveShAddhi te duHkhaM jahati | asthAne dveSho bandhaka itrata chet.h | rAgo.api tatheti samAnam.h | kiJNcha duHkhochChede rAgaH pareNApi svIkAryaH | na duHkhadveSho.asau kintu nirveda eveti chet.h | tarhi na sukharAgo.asau api tu shraddhaiveti vadAmaH | dvitIye tu nAradAdayo nidarshanam.h | te.api tadA.avivekina iti chet.h | kathametadvij~nAtaM laukikavaidi(kalo)kottarapraj~neneti |
nacha rAgetyAdinoktamupasaMharati- tasmAditi ||
vItarAgo.apIti sheShaH |
evaM paranirUpite mokShe duHkhAbhAvamabhyupetya tatra pravR^ittyabhAvaprasaN^go.abhihitaH | idAnIM tu duHkhAbhAvo.api nopapadyata ityAha- vimata iti ||
muktatvena parAbhyupagato.atra pakShaH | duHkhayugityApAdyam.h | yasmAchchetanaH santsukhojkhita ityApAdakam.h | ghaTAdau vyabhichAranirAsAya chetanaH sannityuktam.h | atra chetana ityAtmatvopalakShaNamiti nApAdakasiddhiH | svargavAsiShvanaikAntyaparihArAya sukhojkhita iti | IshvarasyApi sukhasAdhanAnna tatra vyabhichAraH | pratipanno nArakI yathA | evashabdaH pratij~nayA sambaddhayate | na cheyaM sAdhanAnumA yena bAdhAdikasyAvasaraH kintu prasaN^gAnumaiva | tadidamAha ityanumA kena vAryata iti | yadi muktaH sukhI na syAttadA.anAtmA vA duHkhI vA syAt.h sammatavadityAdayo.api atiprasaN^gA draShyavyAH |

tathAshabdaH samuchchaye | tAni shrutyAdInyudAharati- sa iti ||
anena "so.anAnandAdvimuktaH AnandIbhavati' iti shrutimupAdatte | Anandasya svabhAvasiddhatvAdbhavatIti kathamityataH sphuTamityuktam.h | anAnandAt.h duHkhAt.h | nirguNa iti bhAgavate bhagavadvAkyam.h | yatra paramAnande prApte kA(mastR^iShNA.ava)maH spR^ihA.avasIyate | avasAnaM gachChati |
na viShNusadR^ishamityetadapi purANavAkyam.h | yatra loke | AnandAdishabdAH sukhavisheShANAM vAchakAH | kAmasya kAmAH ichChAyA viShayAH | AptAH paryAptAH | kR^idhi kurviti vAyuM prati prArthanam.h | shruR^iNupR^ikR^ivR^ibhyaH Chandasi | shrutyormadhye purANapaThanaM tasya shrutikalpatvapradarshanArtham.h |

na kevalaM sukhAdyabhAva iti chashabdaH | jIvanmuktau shiraHkarAdibhAvo na paramamuktAvityataH kvachidityuktam.h | kuta ityata Aha- shrutayashcheti |

kathaJNchitpramayeti kenApi pramANenetyarthaH | shrutInAM prAganyathA vyAkhyAtatvAt.h | yadvA kathaJNchit.h kenApi sAdhanena na syAt.h kutaH | pramayA muktAvapi bhede pramANasadbhAvAdityarthaH | tatpramANaM paThati- sa iti ||

atrAnumAnamapyAha- kAlo.apIti ||
asau mokShasambandhyapi, jIvasya pareNa yadaikyaM tadyuto na bhavatItyarthaH | kAlo yataH kAlatvAt.h | eSha yadvatsaMsArakAlavat.h | anumA api | muktAvapi jIvasya parabrahmatvanivAraNe pramANamasti, kiM tat.h anumA iti yojanA | ye prAgatyantabhinnasya muktAvaikyaM vadanti | teShAmaikyamiti paratvamiti cha yathAshrutaM vyAkhyeyam.h | ye tu prAgbhedAbhedAvupetya muktAvatyantAbhedamAhustAnpratyaikyAdishabdo.atyantAbhedaparo vyAkhyeyaH | tathAcha na dR^iShyAntadoShaH | jIvashabdashcha niShkR^iShyavyaktiviShayo varNanIyaH | anyathA punardR^iShyAntadoShApatteriti | 
svakIyamAdipadaM vyAkurvannanumAnAntaramAha- kathaM cheti ||
yo jIvaH pUrvaM saMsAre.asau paramAtmA na bhavati, asau pashchAnmuktau sa paramAtmaiva bhavedityetatkathaM yuktimeti | anupapannamityarthaH | atrApi pUrvavanmatabhedena vyAkhyAnaM kartavyam.h | ata eva sa evetyavadhAraNam.h | prayogastu prAgeva darshitaH | apishabdo.anumAnasamuchchaye | asya vyaptimupapAdayati- yata iti ||
yataH kAraNAt.h yatkiJNchidghaTAdikaM vastu pUrvaM yadghaTAdikaM nAbhUt.h | yena satA vastvantareNaikIbhUtaM na bhavatIti yAvat.h | tat.h pashchAtkutashchitkAraNAttadAsa tenaikyamApannamityetanna dR^iShyam.h | nacha dR^ishyate nApi drakShyate | tasmAditi pUrveNa sambandhaH | etenAdadhibhUtasya kShIrasya pashchAddadhibhAvadarshanAdvayabhichAra ityasaN^gatam.h |

mokShavAdArthamupasaMharati- itthamiti ||
itthamuktaprakAreNa jainAdimatAni bhramajAni | upalakShaNametat.h | kAnichidvipralambhajAni ityapi j~neyam.h | tasmAddheyAnIti sheShaH | nanu vaktR^INAM kvachidbhramaH sambhavatyeva | ko doSha ityata Aha- yasmAditi ||

siddhAntanirNItervishiShyahetavaH | 
|| OM naikasmindarshayato hi OM || atrAgnau sarve devA vilIyante | bhUteShu devA vilIyante iti shrutidvayavipratipattyA kimagnAvekasminsarve devA vilIyante, uta paJNchasvapi bhUteShviti saMshaye.agnAvekasminneva sarveShAM devAnAM layaH | agnishruterniravakAshatvAt.h | bhUtashrutestu sAvakAshatvAt.h | ekasminnagnau sarveShAM cha laye.agneshcha vAyau vAyorAkAshe sati bhUteShviti bahuvachanopapatteriti prApte siddhAntitam.h | naikasminnagnau sarveShAM devAnAM layaH | kintu paJNchasvapi bhUteShu | kutaH | "pR^ithivyAmR^ibhavo vilIyante, varuNe.ashvinau, agnAvagnayo, vAyAvindraH, soma Adityo bR^ihaspatirityAkAsha eva sAdhyA vilIyante' (mR^ityavaH) "R^ibhavaH pR^ithivyAM, varuNa ApaH, agnayastejasi, maruto mArute, AkAshe vinAyakA vilIyante' iti shrutI yathAyogaM paJNchasvapi bhUteShu devAnAM layaM darshayato hIti |
atra vAyAvindra iti vAyushabdo bhUtavAyorapradhAnasya vAchako vivakShita iti pratIyate | pR^ithivyAdisaN^kIrtanena bhUta(prakara)kAraNAt.h | sUtrakR^itA cha sarveShu bhUteShu devAnAM laya ityatrArthe gR^ihIte.ayaM shrutiH | bhUteShu tachChaterityupakramAt.h | tato.apyapradhAno vAyuriti pratItinivAraNAya Aha- pradhAneti ||
tushabdo.avadhAraNe | iha shrutau bhUteShviti proktagato.apIti shaN^kAbIjAnuvAdaH | bhUteShu layaM vakShyAmItyAshayena shrutyA proktaM yatpR^ithivyAdikaM tadgato.apIti | yadvA bhUteShu devAnAM laya ityatrArthe proktaM sUtrakR^itA gR^ihItaM shrutivAkyaM tadgato.apIti | kutaH | yuktyA uttamAnAmindrAdInAmadhame bhUtavAyau layAnupapatterityarthaH | pradhAnavAyAvapi kathamindrAdInAM layopapattirityata Aha- yasmAditi ||
yasmAtkAraNAt.h "sA vA eShA devatA.anAdiryo.ayaM pavate' iti shrutau chashabdAdanyAsvapi shrutiShu pradhAnavAyuH bhUritvena sakalajIvottamatvena proktaH, tasmAt.h tasminnindrAdInAM pralayopapatteH, pradhAnavAyustviha vAyunAmeti sambandhaH | yadvA "eSha vai brahma yo.ayaM pavate tametAH paJNcha devatAH parimriyante vidyud.hvR^iShyishchandramA Adityo.agniH' iti shrutiratra vivakShitA | tatra bhUrispaShyaM sUryAdInAM saMhartA prokta iti | evaM tarhi bhUtaprakaraNabAdhaH syAdityata Aha- yata iti || 
na kevalamapradhAnavAyuH kintu sa pradhAnavAyurapi bhUtamAnitvAdbhUtanAmA cheti chArthaH | ataH prakaraNavirodhAbhAvAtpradhAnavAyureveha vAyunAmeti |
uktameva prapaJNchayati- mahAmAnIti ||
mahAMshchAsau mAnI cheti mahAmAnI sarvAbhimAnIti yAvat.h | yathA samastarAShyrAdhipatI rAjA tadantargatasya grAma(ka)syAdhipatirbhavatyevaM sarvAbhimAnI pradhAnavAyuralpasya vAyobharUtasyAbhimAnI bhavedeva | tachChabdena bhUtashabdena | na kevalaM vAyushabdenetyaperarthaH | 
|| iti shrImannyAyasudhAyAM anekalayAdhikaraNam.h ||
|| atha shrImannyAsudhAyAM paralayAdhikaraNam.h ||
|| OM tAni pare tathA hyAha OM || itisUtram.h | asyArthaH | tAni bhUtAbhimAnipR^ibhR^itIni daivAni pare paramAtmani lIyante tathA hyAha shrutiriti | atra sarveShAM devAnAM paramAtmani sAkShAllayaH pratIyate | tatparihArAya bhAShyaM "prANadvAreNa' iti | tatrApi prANe sarveShAM sAkShAllayaH pratIyate | ato vispaShyaM vyAchaShye- tasminniti ||
asheShakramavirodhena shrutyAdyuktaM sarvaM kramamanusR^itya | bhUtAni bhUtAdIni daivAni tasmiMnpradhAnavAyau layaM yAnti | sa eva viShNau layaM yAti | yashcha yAvadindra iti shrutAvindrAdInAM pradhAnavAyau layo.abhihitaH so.api na sAkShAdityAha- indrAdInAmiti ||
tatra pradhAnavAyau | visheShAditi tR^itIyArthe paJNchamI | visheShavAkyena proktamanusR^itya vyAkhyAtavyaH | na tvanyadvayAkhyAnaM sAkShAttatra laya iti | visheShavAkyavirodhAditi bhAvaH | 
tameva kramaM saN^kShepeNa tAvadAha- tasmAditi ||
visheShapramANasya sarvathA.anusartavyatvAditi bhAvaH | atra girijAshabdo vAruNIsauparNIparo vyAkhyeyaH | tathA rudrashabdaH sheShagaruDaparaH | tathAcha vakShyati | tayA girijayA sahaiva rudraM prApya, patiM vANyAH | samastajIvA ityasyaiva vivaraNamasheShA iti | yadvA rudraM pravishantItyadhyAhAreNa vyAkhyeyam.h | asyaiva vivaraNamuttaravAkyajAtam.h | 
tatra vAyAvindra iti shrutAvuktAnAmindrAdInAM chaturNAM pR^ithivyAdInAM bhUtAnAM cha krameNaiva vAyau pravesha iti yaduktaM tattAvatprapaJNchyate | 
iha dvau mArgau sheShamArgo garuDamArgashcha | tatra sheShamArgamAdAvAha- somastviti || 
vArIshayuta ityanenAbdevatAyA varuNasya some laya ityuchyate | ihendrAdichatuShyaye somasya bhUteShvapAM cha vAyupraveshe nirNayaH | prAggirijAM rudramityuktam.h | idAnIM cha giraM vAyumiti | ete chatvAraH shabdAH prasiddhapadArthakA iti pratItiM vArayitumAha- umeti ||
umAgirIshAviti bhAratIrAvityapi | IraH samIraH | vAgityetatparyAyasamudAyo gR^ihyate | pratItArthatve kiM bAdhakamityata uktam.h- vimuktikAla iti | vimuktipratipAdanAvasare | etenomAdInAM chaturNAmiha janmani muktyabhAvAditi bAdhakaM sUchitaM bhavati | vedavAkyAnusAriNo vayamapi tathaiva prayuktavantaH sma iti bhAvaH | umAdishabdAnAM vAruNyAdivR^ittau kiM nimittamityata Aha- ta eveti ||
yadyasmAtta umAdyA eva tatpadaM vAruNyAdipadamuttarakalpe prApnuvanti tasmAditi pUrveNa sambandhaH | anenomAtvAdInAM vAruNItvAdInAM chaikadravyasambandho lakShaNAbIjamityuktaM bhavati | prasiddhapadatyAgenAprasiddhapadaprayoge kiM prayojanamityata Aha- tatkAla iti ||
tatkAle umAtvAdikAle | etAnumAdIndevAn.h | brahmatvakAle teShAmeva vAyvAdInAM brahmatvAdeH kAle | etAn.h vAruNyAdIn.h | cho yasmAdityarthe | iti tasmAt.h | vAk.h vedavANI | tAdR^ishatAm.h umAdishabdavattAm.h | 
etaduktaM bhavati | yo yasminnatiparichayavAMstasyAshramAntaraprAptyAdinA nAmAntare prApte.api prayoga iti kiM prayojanAnveShaNeneti |
idAnIM garuDamArgamAha- sUyar iti || 
agniyukta ityanenAgneH sUrye laya ityuchyate | anenAgnirindra iti shrutiH paramparApekShetyuktaM bhavati | etadgato vANIgata eva | etenendrAdiShvindrAdityabR^ihaspatInAM, bhUteShu tejaso, vAyau layo vivR^ito bhavati | 
nanvetat.h "indra umAyAmumA rudre vilIyate' iti shrutiviruddham.h | umArudrashabdayoH svArthaparityAge.api vAruNIsheShaparatayA vyAkhyAtatvAdityata Aha- indreti || 
yadAtadAshabdAvadhikaraNamAtrasyApalakShakau yatra shrutau atra umAyAmindrapravesha uchyate | tasyAshchomAyA rudre | suparNapatnnayeva | girIshanAmnA girIshaparyAyeNa | sauparNyAmindralayasya balavachChatisiddhatvAditi hishabdaH | atra padasAdR^ishyaM pravR^ittinimittamiti bhAvaH | 
adhunA "tAni pare' ityuktAnAM hiraNyagarbhe layaprakAramAha- bhR^igvAdaya iti ||
suparNapatnnayAH suparNe layaH siddha eva | indraparyantameva vaktavye.adhikavachanamuktadArDhyArtham.h | evamuttaratrApi | ye manavo vaivasvatAdyAH ye cha rAjamukhyAH priyavratAdyAste svAyambhuvamanuM pravishya atra svAyambhuve manau gatA vartamAnA mahendram.h | vishantItyubhayatra sambadhyate | 
vAyubhUtasya mukhyAbhimAnI pradhAnavAyurityuktam.h | amukhyAbhimAninastu "shakraM marudgaNAH' iti layo vakShyate | sanAdaya iti | sanatkumAravyatiriktAH | tasya kAmAvatAratvAt.h | kAmasya tu vAruNyAmukta eva layaH | shiShyA uktebhyaH | etena "agnau sarve devA vilIyante' ityasya viShayo darshitaH | 
asyApavAdamAha- varNAshrameti ||
etatprasaN^gAnmuktau praveshamAtramuktaM na tu dehalayaH | teShAmutkramaNasya vidyamAnatvAt.h | varNAshramAchAraratA ityanena manuShyANAM muktau varNAshramavattvamastIti sUchayati | dharmasya tu svAyambhuve manau laya eva | kAle mokShakAle | sarve pitaraH taM dharmameva saMyAnti | sarve surAnugA gandharvAdyA kuberam.h | upasaMharati- vimuktIti ||
evaM sarve yathoktaprakAreNa vimuktikAle pravishantyuttamAniti sheShaH | na kevalaM pravishanti kiM tarhItyata Aha- abhIkShNamiti || AviShyagrahavadityarthaH | kimanena praveshenetyata Aha- Anandeti || 
amutra uttameShu praveshena |
praviShyAnAM punarnirgamo.asti na veti shaN^kAyAmAha- atashcheti ||
ata ebhya uttamebhyo nirgatAshcheti sambandhaH | iShyam.h ichChA | napuMsake bhAve ktaH | nirgatAnAM punaH pravesho.asti na vetyata Aha- bhUyashcheti ||
tAn.h pUrvapraviShyAneva |
nanvevaMvidhA muktiH kvApi nopalabdhetyata Aha- sAyujyamiti ||
vadanti purANAdIni | sayujAM bhAvo hi sAyujyam.h | kimidaM sAyujyaM sarveShAmasti | neti brUmaH | tarhi sAyujyahInAnAM kIdR^ishI vR^ittirityata Aha- sAyujyeti || 
laye tu laya eva | vishantyuttamAn.h | bahistebhyaH | etatsAyujyabhAjAmapi samAnamiti netyAha- tata iti ||
tataH layakAlAt.h | 
nanvetatsarvaM kutaH pramANAtpratipattavyamityata Aha- uktamiti ||
asyAsmiMllaya ityuktaM samastam.h | paramashrutishcha vistarabhayAnna paThitA | chashabda uttaravAkyena sambaddhayate | pramANAntaramAha- sargeti ||
muktau sargakramato viparyaya iti | yo yasmAjjAtastasya tasminmuktiriti tAvadaN^gIkaraNIyamityarthaH | etachchApavAdAbhAve satIti j~neyam.h | tathAcha nyAyavivaraNe | kuta etadityata Aha- laya iti ||
sAdhAraNapralaye sargakramAdviparyayasya sattvAditi bhAvaH | etadapi kuta ityata Aha- atho iti ||
athoshabdo.arthAntare | viparyayeNa sargakramamapekShya | avadat.h upapAditavAn.h | girAM vedavAchAM prabhuH sUtrakAraH | yathA "viparyayeNa tu kramo.atra upapadyate cha' iti | laye sR^iShyikramato viparyayashchenmuktau tathA bhAvyamityatra kiM niyamAkamityata Aha- laya iti || 
yataH kAraNAtsurANAM laya eveyaM muktirna tu manuShyANAmiva prAgeva dehAdutkrAntiH | tasmAduktaM yuktam.h | sAmAnyavisheShabhAvAnna sAdhyavishiShyatAdoShaH | sargashchoktAnuguNa eva shrutyAdisiddha iti bhAvaH | nanu prAN^.h muktAnAM bhogAdikaM samarthitam.h | idAnIM tUchyate laya eva muktiriti | tatkathaM pUrvAparavirodho na bhavatItyata Aha- bhoga iti ||
visheSheNa devapadAdapyatishayena | dehahAnilakShaNA muktirlayAnna vishiShyata ityuktaM na tu sarvA.apIti bhAvaH | ata eva prAgiyamityuktam.h | 
bhogashcha muktiriti sUtrakArAnuktaM kasmAdupasaN^khayeyamityata Aha- yamiti ||
yaM bhogaM chaturthapAde sUtrakAro vakShyati muktitvena saH | pramANAntaraM chAha- uktashcheti || 
bimbapratibimbabhAvo devAnAmuktalayAnusArata iti | yasminyasyAsmAbhirlaya uktaH sa bimbaH aparaH pratibimba ityuktamastItyarthaH | tataH kimityata Aha- bimba iti ||
mokShAnantaramapi sarvadA | etaduttaratropayogi | prasaN^gAdihoktam.h | yadyasmAnmuktau pratibimbasya bimbe layo niyataH pramANaprasiddhaH, tAni chAnyatra tasmAduktaM yuktamiti |
yaduktaM sarveShAM bhUtAnAM prANe layastasya viShNAviti tadasat.h | "prANastejasi tejanaH parasyAM devatAyAm.h' iti shrutivirodhAt.h | bimbe pratibimbasya laya iti chAsat.h | nahi prANastejAbhUtasya pratibimba ityata Aha- tejo.abhidhAmiti || 
vAyuH pralaye tejo.abhidhAM shriyamApya tatra lIno bhUtvA viShNumAptaH | sR^iShyikAle jAte.agre sarvebhyaH pUrvaM, tato viShNoH, putratayA hiraNyagarbhatvena prasUtaH | punareva pralaye muktau viShNuM pravishya atra viShNau tiShThati |
idamuktaM bhavati | tejaHshabdasya lakShmIvAchitvAnnoktavirodhaH | evaM tarhi "vilIno hi prakR^itau saMsArameti' iti shrutervAyoH saMsAraprasaN^ga iti chenna | iShyatvAt.h | hiraNyagarbhatvena punajarnanAN^gIkArAt.h | evamapi brahmavido muktyabhAvaprasaN^ga iti chenna | hiraNyagarbhatvAnantaraM muktisvIkArAditi | idaM cha prANashabdasya vAyuvAchitvapakShamAdAyoktam.h | hiraNyagarbhavAchitvapakShe tu bhAShyoktaM draShyavyam.h | 
muktAnAM svastottamadevatAH pravishyAvasthAnamityuktam.h | naitAvadeva | kintu bhagavatpravesho.apyasti | uktashcha bhogo nAnandasya janakaH kintu vyaJNjaka eva | Anandastu svarUpabhUta ityAha- sarve.apIti ||
sarve.apItyukte devAnAM prakR^itatvAtta eveti pratItiM vArayitumasheShato.apItyuktam.h | bhuJNjantaH anubhavantaH | 
shiShyA havyavAhamityasyApavAdAntaramAha- prayAtIti ||
nirR^itistu dhamarM prayAti | marudgaNAH shakraM prayAnti | tathAshabdaH samuchchaye | pR^itanAdhipAdyA viShvaksenAdyAH sarve bhagavataH pArShadA aniruddhaM prayAnti | dehalayArthamiti sheShaH | aniruddhasya tu kAme laya ukta evetyevArthaH | atra pramANamAha- tureti || 
ata evaitattatraiva noktaM paramashrutAvanuktatvAt.h | 
pAdArthamupasaMharati- iyamiti ||
devAdInAM dehalayarUpA vimuktirukteti | 
|| iti shrImatpUrNapramatibhagavatpAdasukR^iteranuvyAkhyAnasya praguNajayatIrthAkhyayatinA kR^itAyAM TIkAyAM viShamapadavAkyArthavivR^itau chaturthe.adhyAye.atrotkramaNacharaNaH paryavasitaH ||
mAgaro gamyaM chAsminpAda uchyata iti bhAShyam.h | tatprAk.h prasaN^gAdvivR^itamapIhAvaraprAptau visheShato vivR^iNoti- utkrAnteti ||
ye sharIrAdutkrAntA mAnuShAsteShAM mArgo bhagavallokagamanArthaH | gamyamapi teShAmeveti pratItinirAsAyoktam.h- vimukteti || ye karmaNo dehAchcha vimuktAsteShAM sarveShAmapi gamyam.h | idamubhayametatpAdoditam.h | 
atrAdhikaraNeShu pUrvapakShayuktiH siddhAntayuktIshchAha- sukrameti ||
anyamatasyeti jAtAvekavachanam.h | siddhAntanirNItikarAstarkA iti sheShaH | || OM apratIkAlambanAnnayatIti bAdarAyaNa ubhayathA cha doShAttatkratushcha OM || vimuktagamyaM pratipAdayitumidaM sUtram.h | tadbhAShye na vispaShyamityataH spaShyIkariShyanpratIkashabdArthaM tAvadAha- pratIkamiti ||
Adipadena manaHprabhR^itInAM bhagavatpratimAnAM grahaNam.h | yadyapi sUtre.apratIkAlambanAnAM gamyamuktaM pratIkAlambanAnAM tu parisheShasiddham.h | tathApyaspaShyaspaShyIkaraNArthaM pravR^ittatvAdabhAvasya bhAvapUrvakatvAchcha parisheShasiddhamevArthamAdAvAha- tadgatamiti ||
pratIkagatameva viShNum.h | te pratIkAlambanAH | purataH prAk.h pralayakAlAt.h | asmAt.h brahmaNaH | matiM bhagavajj~nAnavisheSham.h | prApsyanti pralaye | idAnIM sUtritAmapratIkAlambanAnAM gatiM prapaJNchayati- ata iti || 
pratIkAlambanebhyo.anye vyoptopAsakA apratIkAlambanAH | prathamatastaM viShNumApyApi parAntakAle | tasmAdviShNostaM brahmANamApya hariM gatA bhavantIti | 
|| iti shrImatpUNarpramatibhagavatpAdasukR^iteranuvyAkhyAnasya praguNajayatIrthAkhyayatinA kR^itAyAM TIkAyAM viShamapAdavAkyArthavivR^itau chaturthAdhyAye.a(rchiHprabhR^iti)smingamanacharaNaH paryavasitaH ||
|| iti shrImannyAyasudhAyAM chaturthAdhyAyasya tR^itIyaH pAdaH ||
|| atha shrImannyAyasudhAyAM chaturthAdhyAyasya chaturthaH pAdaH ||
pAdapratipAdyaM tatsaN^gatishcha prasiddhaivetyataH pUrvottarapakShayuktirevAha- atikrameti ||
anyapakShe pUrvapakSheShu | sunirNayaH siddhAntanirNayaH arthaH prayojanaM yAsAM tAH sunirNayArthA yuktayaH | 
|| OM ata eva chAnanyAdhipatiH OM || idaM (etat.h) sUtraM kashchidvayAkhyAti | ata eva chAvandhyasaN^kalpatvA(devAna)danyAnadhipatirvidvAnbhavati | nAsyAnyo.adhipatirbhavatItyartha iti | tadidamasaditi bhAvenAha- ananyeti ||
iha sUtre muktasyAnanyAdhipatiriti yadananyabhR^ityatvamuktaM tattUditebhyA ye yasya muktasyAdhipatitvenoditAH shAstre tebhyaH anyasya bhR^ityo na bhavati mukta iti pratipAdanAya | natu sarvathA adhipatinivAraNAya | kutaH | ananyapadaprayogAt.h | anyathA.apatirityakShyat.h | 
itashchaivamevetyAha- patimiti ||
yat.h yasmAddhareramR^itatvasyota yatpatitvaM tasya vAk.h "utAmR^itatvasyeshAnaH' iti shrutiriti yAvat.h | viShNumeShAM muktAnAM patimAha | tato.apyukta eva sUtrArtho nApara iti |
anumAnenApyetamarthaM samarthayate- ete.apIti ||
api cheti pramANasamuchchaye | ete muktAH | anyo.adhipatiryeShAM te.anyAdhipatayaH | teShAM bhAvo.anyAdhipatitvaM tena yuktAH | viShNvanyatvena chittvena jIvatvena cha | tushabdo visheShArthaH | parakIyavyAkhyAnAnusAreNAnyAdhipatitvayuktA iti pratij~nAtam.h | svamate tvadhipatiyuktA ityeva pratij~neti | yadi kashchidudAhR^itashrutyarthe vipratipadyeta tasyAnumAnenaivAla(mityukta)mityanumaiva cheha mukteShvabhIShyasyAdhipatisAhityasya siddhayai bhavatIti | katham.h | vyAptipakShadharma(tva)tayoH pramitatvAditi hishabdaH | muktA adhipatirahitA muktatvAdavandhyasaN^kalpatvAdIshvaravadityanumAnapratirodha iti chenna | mUlaprakR^itAvanaikAntyAt.h | vipakShe bAdhakAbhAvAchcha | tadidamuktaM nishchayAditi | 
na kevalaM muktAnAM bhagavAnadhipatiH kiM tvanye.api yathAsambhavaM bhavantItyAshayavAnAha- mukteti ||
brahmapuraHsarANAmapi muktau muktAshcha te svakIyAH svaiH saha muktiM gatAshcha cha te.avarAshcha muktasvakIyAvarAstAnniyantR^itA.asti | amuktAnprati yantR^itA sarvathA nAsti | yathA.a.aha sUtrakAraH "vikAravatir cha' iti | mukteShvapi kalpAntare muktAnsvakalpe mukteShvapyuttamAnsamAMshcha prati nAstItyato muktetyAdyuktam.h | anena parodAhR^itashrutInAM gatishchoktA bhavati |
kuta etadityata Aha- aneneti ||
anena chakShurantasthena devena prasannena tathA.amunA.a.adityAntargatena cha parArvAktanalokavartinAM muktAnAmIShye IshitA bhavatIti shrutirj~nAnato muktaniyantR^itvaM phalamAha- hIti || atrAmunA paralokinAM, anena arvAktanalokinAmiti j~neyam.h | anena "atha ya evaM vidvAn.h' ityAdyAM "so.amunaiva ye chAmuShmAtparAJNcho lokAstAMshchApnoti devakAmAMshcha, athAnenaiva ye chaitasmAdarvAJNcho lokAstAMshchApnoti manuShyakAmAMshcha' iti shrutimupAdatte |
nanvasyAM shrutAvuktamidaM j~nAnaphalaM muktigatamityetatkuta ityata Aha- muktAviti || 
etachcha sarvalokAptilakShaNaM phalaM muktAveva | "udeti ha vai sarvebhyaH pApmabhyo ya evaM veda' iti sarvapApakShayaliN^gAt.h | nahi mukteritatraitatsambhavati | prArabdhapApasya AmokShaM vidyamAnatvAt.h | 
yadidaM sarvalokAdhipatyaM muktau phalamuktaM tatsarveShAmapi muktAnAmiti pratItinirAsAyAha- loketi || 
sarvAtmanA lokAdhipatyaM cha muktasya vidhAtureva | anyeShAM yathAyogyamiti bhAvaH | svakIyetyuktamanusandheyam.h | atra pramANamAha- ityAheti ||
sA chAnyatra draShyavyA | chashabdo vakShyamANayuktisamuchchayArthaH | shrutyantaramapyevameva vyAkhyeyamityAha- sarva iti ||
"sa veda brahma, sarve.asmai devA balimAvahanti' iti shrutyuktaM muktasya sarvadevapUjyatvaM chAnavadhikaM vidhAtureva na sarveShAmuktashruterevetyarthaH | ito.apyevamityAha- neti || pUjakA api hi devA muktA eva | amuktAnAM muktasambandhasya nivAritatvAt.h | tathAcha sarve devA muktAH sarvairmuktairdevaiH pUjyanta ityuktaM syAt.h | etachcha vyAhatam.h | tata eva na (syaivotta)syottamatvasyAdhamatvasya kvApyadarshanAt.h | ata ukta eva shrutyarthaH | 
syAdetat.h | tAMshchApnotItyukta AptA sarvAshubhanAshaliN^gAdbhavatu muktaH | tasya chAtra lokAptirevochyate | natu (mukta)svakIyAvarayantR^itetyata Aha- loka iti ||
iha shrutau lokA iti padaM tAvallokinAM vachaHpratipAdakam.h | na kevalamAptA muktaH | lokapadamapi lokiviShayamityapishabdaH | tushabdo vR^ittivisheShadyotakaH | yathA maJNchashabdo maJNchastheShu puruSheShu vidyate tathA lokashabdo.api lokastheShu puruSheShviti | atra lakShaNAbIjasambandhastu sphuTa eva | lAkShiNikaprayogaprayojanaM vAchyamityata Aha- loka iti ||
hishabdaH prasiddhau | prayojanAnusandhAnena vinetyevashabdaH | ravaH shabdaH | prajAsu prajAviShaye | rUDhalakShaNaiShA tatra kiM prayojanAnveShaNeneti bhAvaH | 
athavA kiM lakShaNayA | yato vAchaka eva lokashabdo janAnAmiti bhAvenAha- lokA iti sarvajanairiti shabdashaktij~naiH | 
prakArAntareNa lokashabdasya puruShavAchitvamAha- taditi ||
lokAbhimAninaH | abhimAnyadhikaraNanyAyeneti bhAvaH | 
astu lokashabdasya janeShu vR^ittistathA.apyasyAM shrutau tadvivakShA kuto j~nAyate | na tAvatA.apIShyasiddhiH | muktaviShayatAyAM pramANAbhAvAt.h | Aptireva chehochyate natu tanniyamanamityata Aha- tadgA iti ||
tushabdo.avadhAraNe | iha ye chAmuShmAdityasyAM shrautau tadgAH parAvaralokagatAH muktA eva loka iti shabdo eShAM te lokashabdAH | 
te chAnyonyanAthAH uttamA adhamAnAM svIyAnAM niyAmakA ityevametachChativyAkhyAnarUpA paiN^gishrutirasti | yadyapi muktasya vikArAvartivyApAraniShedhAdevaitatsiddham.h | tathA.api dArDhyAya shrutyudAharaNam.h | etena lakShaNApakShe mukhye bAdhakaM choktaM bhavati | abhimAnipakShe tu bhUtapUrvagatyA mukteShu lokashabdo vyAkhyeyaH | 
prakArAntareNAsyAM shrutau muktasya muktaniyAmakatvaM pratipAdayannAha- aloketi ||
lokadoShAtItatvAdvidehatvAdveti bhAvaH | tataH kiM prakR^ita ityata Aha- padamiti ||
iha parAJNcho lokA arvAJNcho lokA ityatra tAdR^igaloka ityapi padaM ChettuM yuktam.h | lokAlokashabdayoH saMhitAyA(yAM)H samAnarUpatvAditi bhAvaH | 
yogavR^ittyA.api lokashabdasya mukteShu vR^ittiH sambhavatItyAha- loketi ||
yataH sarve.api muktAH satatamapi prakAsharUpAH prasiddhAstato.api lokAbhidhAH | lokateH pachAdyachi kR^ite rUpametat.h | darshanaM prakAsha iti cha nArthAntaram.h | 
yaduktaM prAglokAbhimAnino ye muktAsta iha lokashabdArthA iti tadasat.h | te hi uttamAH | nacha tanniyamanaM muktAnAM sambhavatItyato moktaM vismArShIrityAha- brahmaiveti ||
tathAcha nAnupapattiriti ||
evaM svamatena shrutiM vyAkhyAya yatpareShAM vyAkhyAnamAdityamaNDale parameshvaramupAsInasya viduShaH paralAkAdhipatyaM bhavati chakShuShyupAsInasyArvAktanalokAdhipatyaM bhavatIti tannirAkaroti- nacheti ||
iha shrutau | lokAdhipatyaM vij~nAnaphalaM samuktamiti vyAkhyAnaM na yuktam.h | kuta ityata Aha- ravIti ||
chashabdena chakShurgate cheti samuchchinoti | yasmAt.h kAraNAt.h tat.h lokAdhipatyaM puraiva pUrvavAkya eva ravibimbage harau chakShurantargate cha pR^ithak.h vibhAgenoktam.h | AdityagataM prakR^itya "sa eSha ye chAmuShmAtparAJNcho lokAsteShAM cheShye manuShyakAmAnAM cha' iti | tasmAnneti |
etaduktaM bhavati | na samastalokAdhipatyaM viduSho yujyate | tasya bhagavaddharmatvenAtraivoktatvAditi |
bhagavaddharmo.api viduSho bhavatItyaN^gIkAre ko doSha iti chet.h | tatkiM bhagavAn.h svIyasarvalokAdhipatyaM parityajya viduShe dadAtIti | uta vidvAMsamavAntareshvaraM karotIti | atha vidvAMstAdAtmyaM prApnotIti |
nAdyaH | bhagavadaishvaryasya samastashrutyAdau nityatvAvagamAt.h | kiM chaikasmai viduShe dattasvAdhipatyo magavAnanyasmai (viduShe) kiM dadyAt.h | sarvapApakShayaliN^gavirodhAchcha | ata eva na dvitIyaH | hiraNyagarbhe tadyujyata iti chenna | pApma(pa)shabdena prakR^itderbandhasya vivakShitatvAt.h | ata evoktaM sarvAshubheti | "tasyoditi nAma' iti hi parameshvarasyochChabdaM nAmatvenoktvA tasya nirvachanaM kriyate "sa eSha sarvebhyaH pApmabhya udite' iti | tatroditatvamevochChabdAtharH | kasmAdityapekShAyAM yogyaM kimapi grAhyam.h | nacha tatpApameveti niyAmakamasti | ataH sarvamapyashubhaM tatra vivakShitam.h | tadeva cha viduShaH phalamuchyate | tR^itIyaM nirAkaroti- bheda iti || 
viduShaH | parameshvarAditi sheShaH | AdipadenAnenetyasya grahaNam.h | kriyAvisheShaNaM chaitat.h | bhedashcheti sambandhaH | samyagiti | spaShyam.h | nahi tadAtmA tatprasAdAttaddharmA bhavati | 
bhavedetadyadyamunA.anenetyetadamunA devena prasannena nimitteneti vyAkhyAyeva | nachaivam.h | kiM nAma | amunA rUpeNAmuShya tAdAtmyaM prApyeti | nachaivaM sati bhedoktirastItyata Aha- tvapratyayamiti ||
chashabdastatsamAnArthapratyayAntarasamuchchayArthaH | apishabdo rUpeNeti padasya | tena ityamunA anenetyubhayorgrahaNam.h | atihAya pravR^ittAyAmiha shrutau | bhave(devaM pa)dayaM parasyasyAbhilAShaH shrutistu na tathA vakti | yadi khalvadastvenAdastayedaMtvenedaMtayeti bhAvavAchI pratyayaH syAt.h | yadi vA(chA)munA rUpeNAtmanA, anena rUpeNAtmaneti padaM syAt.h | tadA pratImo.ayamarthaH shrutyabhipreta iti | nachaitadastIti |
nanu bhAvapradhAnA nirdeshA bahulamupalabhyate | tato vinA.api pratyayena so.artho bhaviShyati | sopaskarANi cha vAkyAni bhavanti | tato rUpeNetyAdipadAdhyAhAro vA kariShyate | ko doSha iti chenna | nishchite hi vAkyArthe tadupapadyate | nacha tannishchAyakamatrAstItyAshayavAndoShAntaramAha- bhavatIti ||
yadyasyAM shrutau tAdAtmyaprAptyA(ptau) tadIyaM sarvalokAdhipatyamasya bhavatItyartho vivakShitaH syAt.h | tarhyatraitadarthapratipAdane.ayaM 
vidvAnasau paramAtmA bhavatItyetAvadeva vaktavyam.h | natu so.amunaivetyAdikam.h | tAdAtmyaprAptau taddharma(rmya)sya svataH siddhatvAt.h | ayamasau bhavatItyalpaM shabdaM vihAya bahUni vAkyAni prayuJNjAnAyAH shruterakushalatvadoShaH syAt.h | nahi kashchidalpIyasA prayatnena siddhatyarthe mahAntaM prayatnamAtiShThamA(naH sadbhi)no mahadbhirAdriyate | kiM chAtra parameshvaraH saguNo vA vivakShito nirguNo vA | Adye na viduShastattAdAtmyamasti | pareNA(pya)nabhyupagatatvAt.h(mAt.h) | na dvitIyaH | nirguNasyA.a.adityAdiparichChedAnupapatteH | aishvaryAsambhavAchcha |
nacha tad.hbhUyaMgatasya sarvalokAdhipatyaM bhavatIti |
apavyAkh.hyAnanirAkaraNamupasaMharanpAdArthaM saN^kShepeNAha- ata iti || 
jagachChabdena svI(syakI)yAvaramuktA gR^ihyante | jagadvayApAravarjamityetanmuktetarajagadviShayam.h | ato na tadvirodha ityetadapyanena sUchayati | anyathA svAvaramuktanimakA evetyavakShyat.h | tathAchAnanyAdhipatipadamuktArthameveti bhAvaH | AtmIyaM natu parameshvaram.h | ajAt.h parameshvarAttamavihAyetyarthaH | tatprasAdAditi vA |
|| iti shrImannyAyasudhAyAM ananyAdhipatitvAdhikaraNam.h ||
evaMparisamApitagrantho bhagavAnAchAryaH svapratipAditaprakAraM svasyAtivishadAnAdisAvarj~napradaM nirupAdhikaparamapremAspadaguNagaNaM puruShottamaM paunaHpunyena praNamati- nama iti ||
asheShavisheShaiH pUrNA ye guNAsteShAM pradhAnAshrayAya, bhakte mayyanukampAdanukroshAt.h | ata eva tAchChIlikasya tR^inaH prayogaH | sadguNAnuvAdenAnupAdhipriyatvaM tAdAtmyaM cha vidhIyata iti na punaruktiH |
yathA bhagavatsvarUpavij~nAnaM samastapuruShArthasAdhanaM tathA svasvarUpavij~nAnamapItyataH tadAviShkurvannAha- yasyeti ||
yasya vAyordevasya vedavachane baLitthetyAdAvalaM divyAnyadbhutAni trINi rUpANyuditAni | amunA vAyunA.ayaM keshave viShaye granthaH kR^ita ityanvayaH |
kIdR^ishaM tasya mUlarUpaM kathaMbhUtAni cha tAni trINi rUpANItyata uktam.h- baDityAdi ||
yasya tanmUlarUpaM baT.h balAtmakaM darshataM j~nAnarUpaM cha | dR^isherauNashadiko.atachpratyayaH | 
anena vAyushabdo niruktaH | vashabdo balavAchI | ayatiH gatyarthaH | gatyarthAshchAvagatyarthAH | tata uN.h | vashchAsau Ayushcheti vAyuriti |
kiJNcha bhargo bharaNagamanayoH kartR^i | hubhR^iJN.h bharaNe, gamlR^i gatau, AbhyAmasun.hpratyayo Dichcha | idamapi vAyushabdavyAkhyAnam.h | vA gatigandhanayorityataH kR^ivApAjimisvadisAdhyashUbhya uNityuN.h | anekArthatvAddhAtUnAM vAtirbharaNe.api vartate | api cha mahat.h shreShTham.h | vayaH shreShThatva ityasmAduN.h | 
na kevalaM mUlarUpamevaM kintu yasyAvatAreShu nihitaM rUpamitthameva | 
yasya prathamakaM prathamaM rUpaM rAmaviShayANi vachAMsi mUlarAmAyaNAdIni rAmavachAMsi teShAM nayaM nIyante shiShyeShu pravartyante.aneneti | erajityach.h |
yasya dvitIyaM vapuH pR^ikShaH | pR^ichChabdaH pR^itanAvAchI prasiddhaH | tasminkarmaNyupapade kShai kShaya ityetasmAt.h Ato.anupasagare ka iti kaH | upapadatakAralopashChAndasaH | puMliN^gaM(N^gaH) cha shrutyanusAreNa | asunvA pratyayaH | kidita napuMsakamevedam.h | ripupR^itanAkShayakArItyarthaH |
yasya tR^itIyaM vapuH etanmadhvaH | madhushabdaH sukhavAchI | "madhuta dyaurastu naH pitA' iti prayogAt.h | vashabdaH shAstrAparaparyAyatIrthavAchI | vAteravagatyatharAtkaraNe ghaJNarthe kavidhAnamiti kaH | sukhasAdhanaM tIrthamasyeti | svarityatrevokAralopaH | 
bhagavatsvarUpapratipAdanenaiva granthopasaMhAraH samuchita ityAshayavAnnityAparokShaM bhagavantaM sambodhya stauti- niHsheShamiti ||
bhUtiH mahAlakShmIH |
vachanaprasUnamAlA jayatIrthAkhyena bhikShuNA rachitA |
dhriyatAM hR^idaye sadaye kamalAmahilena pUruSheNa || 1 || 
na vaiduShyabhrAntyA nacha vachanachAturyakudhiyA na mAtsaryAveshAnnacha chapalatAdoShavashataH |
paraM shraddhAjADyAdakR^iShi kR^itimAchAryavachasi skhalannapyetasmAjjagati nahi nindyo.asmi viduShAm.h || 2 ||
anuvyAkhyA.amR^itAmbhodheH samutpannA.atinirmalA |
iyaM nyAyasudhA bhaumairvibudhaiH sevyatAM sadA || 3 ||
iti shrImatpUrNapramatibhagavatpAdasukR^iteranuvyAkhyAnasya praguNajayatIrthAkhyayatinA | 
kR^itAyAM TIkAyAM viShamapadavAkyArthavivR^itau chaturthe.adhyAye.asmiMshcharamacharaNaH paryavasitaH || 4 || 
|| iti shrImannyAyasudhAyAM chaturtho.adhyAyaH sampUrNaH ||
